【第一題 / NO. 1】


Universal Containers utilizes opportunities and a custom object called Detailed_Sales__c. The company would like to roll sales metrics up to an opportunity for only Detailed_Sales__c records that have their picklist status set to Active. What is the recommended method for the app builder to achieve this request?


Universal Containers 公司使用「機會 (Opportunity)」和一個名為 Detailed_Sales__c 的自訂物件。公司希望將銷售指標匯總到「機會」上，但僅限於 Detailed_Sales__c 記錄中選項清單 (picklist) 狀態設定為「啟用 (Active)」的記錄。對於應用程式建構者 (App Builder) 來說，建議用哪種方法來實現這個需求？


A. Utilize the AppExchange to download a third-party application that can roll up the sales dollars with the appropriate filter.
     

利用 AppExchange 下載一個可以使用適當篩選條件來匯總銷售金額的第三方應用程式。

B. Create a master-detail relationship between the parent and child object with a roll-up summary field that filters on the status field.
     

在父物件和子物件之間建立一個主從式關係 (master-detail relationship)，並使用一個可以根據狀態欄位進行篩選的總計欄位 (roll-up summary field)。

C. Create a lookup relationship between the parent and child object with a roll-up summary held that filters on the status field.
     

在父物件和子物件之間建立一個查詢關係 (lookup relationship)，並使用一個可以根據狀態欄位進行篩選的總計欄位。

D. Utilize Apex code to roll up the desired amounts.
     

使用 Apex 程式碼來匯總所需的金額。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
Create a master-detail relationship between the parent and child object with a roll-up summary field that filters on the status field is the recommended method for the app builder to achieve the request. According to the Salesforce documentation, "Roll-up summary fields calculate values from related records, such as those in a master-detail relationship." A roll-up summary field can filter on a field value of the child records and sum up only those records that match the criteria.
建議的方法是在父物件和子物件之間建立一個主從式關係，並使用一個可以根據狀態欄位進行篩選的總計欄位。根據 Salesforce 的文件，「總計欄位」是從相關記錄（例如主從式關係中的記錄）計算值的。總計欄位可以根據子記錄的欄位值進行篩選，並且只加總符合條件的記錄。

【第二題 / NO. 2】


Which two solutions prevent a formula field from being referenced by a Roll-Up Summary Field? (Choose 2 answers)


哪兩個解決方案會阻止公式欄位被「總計欄位 (Roll-Up Summary Field)」引用？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. A cross-object workflow updating a field referenced by the formula field
     

跨物件工作流程更新了公式欄位所引用的欄位。

B. A cross-object field reference in the formula field
     

公式欄位中有跨物件的欄位引用。

C. The CASE() function in the formula field
     

公式欄位中有 CASE() 函數。

D. The NOW() function in the formula field
     

公式欄位中有 NOW() 函數。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, D

詳解 (Explanation):
A formula field cannot be referenced by a roll-up summary field if it contains a cross-object field reference or a time-based function. A cross-object field reference is a reference to a field from a different object, such as Account.Name on a Contact object. A time-based function is a function that returns the current date or time, such as NOW() or TODAY().
如果公式欄位包含「跨物件欄位引用」或「時間相關函數」，則該公式欄位不能被總計欄位所引用。跨物件欄位引用是指引用來自不同物件的欄位，例如在「連絡人」物件上引用 Account.Name。時間相關函數是指會返回當前日期或時間的函數，例如 NOW() 或 TODAY()。

【第三題 / NO. 3】


The Service Manager provided the app builder with color code requirements for case age on open cases. * New cases populate a green circle * Day-old cases populate a yellow circle * Three-day-old cases populate a red circle How should an app builder implement this requirement?


服務經理向應用程式建構者提供了關於未結案個案 (open cases) 存在天數的顏色代碼要求：
新個案顯示一個綠色圓圈
存在一天的個案顯示一個黃色圓圈
存在三天的個案顯示一個紅色圓圈 應用程式建構者應如何實現此要求？


A. Formula Field
     

公式欄位

B. Quick Action
     

快速動作

C. Custom Button
     

自訂按鈕

D. Lightning Web Component
     

Lightning Web 元件
點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
A formula field is a read-only field that derives its value from a formula expression you define. You can use formula fields to display images based on certain conditions. In this case, a formula field can be used to display a green, yellow, or red circle image based on the case age.
公式欄位是一個唯讀欄位，其值由您定義的公式表達式衍生而來。您可以使用公式欄位根據特定條件顯示圖片。在這個情境中，可以使用公式欄位根據個案的存在天數來顯示綠色、黃色或紅色的圓圈圖片。

【第四題 / NO. 4】


After universal containers converted qualified leads. Sales reps need to be able to report on converted leads. How should an app builder support for this requirement?


在 Universal Containers 公司轉換了合格的潛在客戶 (leads) 之後，銷售代表需要能夠對已轉換的潛在客戶進行報告。應用程式建構者應如何支援此要求？


A. Enable preserve lead status in the lead conversion settings
     

在潛在客戶轉換設定中啟用「保留潛在客戶狀態」。

B. Assign the representative view and edit converted leads permission
     

指派給代表「檢視和編輯已轉換的潛在客戶」權限。

C. Ensure the representative has read access to the original lead records
     

確保代表對原始潛在客戶記錄具有讀取權限。

D. Create a custom report type with converted leads as the primary object
     

建立一個自訂報告類型，並將「已轉換的潛在客戶」作為主要物件。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
The solution that an app builder should use to meet this requirement is creating a custom report type with converted leads as the primary object. A custom report type is a template that defines the objects and fields that are available for a report. This way, sales reps can create reports on converted leads and see their related information.
應用程式建構者應使用的解決方案是建立一個自訂報告類型，並將「已轉換的潛在客戶」作為主要物件。自訂報告類型是一個範本，它定義了報告中可用的物件和欄位。這樣一來，銷售代表就可以建立關於已轉換潛在客戶的報告，並查看其相關資訊。

【第五題 / NO. 5】


To increase adoption, Universal Containers is proposing changes to its Salesforce data model to allow easier visibility for sales reps into key metrics. The proposal has three custom objectsrelated to the Account object, one with a master-detail, and two that are not. Each of these objects has 15 fields they would like to summarize on the Account object. What are two considerations for this proposal? (Choose 2 answers)


為了提高採用率，Universal Containers 公司提議對其 Salesforce 資料模型進行變更，以便銷售代表更容易查看關鍵指標。該提案有三個與「帳戶 (Account)」物件相關的自訂物件，其中一個是主從式關係，另外兩個不是。他們希望在「帳戶」物件上匯總這三個物件中各 15 個欄位的資料。 對於此提案，有哪兩項考量因素？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Roll-up summaries allow MAX, MIN, SUM, COUNT, and AVG.
     

總計欄位允許 MAX、MIN、SUM、COUNT 和 AVG 函數。

B. An object can have 20 object references.
     

一個物件可以有 20 個物件引用。

C. An object can have 25 roll-up summaries.
     

一個物件可以有 25 個總計欄位。

D. Roll-up summaries are limited to master-detail relationships.
     

總計欄位僅限於主從式關係。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, D

詳解 (Explanation):
Roll-up summaries allow MAX, MIN, SUM, COUNT, and AVG functions on numeric fields from child records related by a master-detail relationship. Roll-up summaries are limited to master-detail relationships and cannot be used with lookup relationships. An object can have up to 40 roll-up summary fields, not 25.
總計欄位允許對透過主從式關係關聯的子記錄中的數字欄位使用 MAX、MIN、SUM、COUNT 和 AVG 函數。總計欄位僅限於主從式關係，不能與查詢關係一起使用。一個物件最多可以有 40 個總計欄位，而不是 25 個。

【第六題 / NO. 6】


DreamMouse Realty has a mentorship program that pairs experienced Realtors with new Realtors. Each experienced Realtor can mentor one or several new Realtors, and each new Realtor is required to work with a single experienced Realtor they report to for a probationary period. What type of relationship would an app builder set up to meet this specification?


DreamMouse Realty 有一個導師計畫，將有經驗的房地產經紀人與新進經紀人配對。每位有經驗的經紀人可以指導一位或多位新進經紀人，而每位新進經紀人都必須在試用期內與一位他們所屬的有經驗的經紀人合作。 應用程式建構者應設定哪種類型的關係來滿足此規範？


A. Indirect lookup

     

間接查詢

B. Many-to-many
     

多對多

C. Master-detail
     

主從式

D. Lookup
     

查詢

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
Lookup is the type of relationship that would be set up to meet the specification. According to the Salesforce documentation, "A lookup relationship creates a loose association between objects. The lookup field allows users to select a record from another object." Master-detail is used for creating parent-child relationships.
查詢 (Lookup) 關係是滿足此規範的關係類型。根據 Salesforce 的文件，「查詢關係在物件之間建立一個鬆散的關聯。查詢欄位允許使用者從另一個物件中選擇一筆記錄」。這種關係是一對多的，正好符合一位有經驗的經紀人對應多位新進經紀人，而每位新進經紀人只對應一位導師。主從式關係 (Master-detail) 用於建立更緊密的父子關係。

【第七題 / NO. 7】


Manage at Universal Containers want a quick to create additional accounts to form a hierarchy from a parent account record. They want to auto-populate five fields based on the parent to make it easier for users to create the child accounts quickly.


Universal Containers 的經理希望有一種快速的方法，可以從一個父帳戶記錄中建立額外的帳戶來形成一個層級結構。他們希望根據父帳戶自動填入五個欄位，以便使用者能更輕鬆地快速建立子帳戶。


A. Custom Global Quick Action
     

自訂全域快速動作

B. Custom Global Quick Account.
     

自訂全域快速帳戶 (此選項原文可能有誤)

C. Custom action on Account
     

在「帳戶」上的自訂動作

D. Custom link on Account
     

在「帳戶」上的自訂連結

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
A custom action on Account can be used to create additional accounts from a parent account record. A custom action can have predefined values for certain fields based on the parent record. A custom global action can be used to create records that do not have any relationship with other objects.
在「帳戶」上的自訂動作 (Custom action on Account) 可用於從父帳戶記錄建立額外的帳戶。自訂動作可以根據父記錄為某些欄位預先定義值。而全域快速動作 (Global Quick Action) 則是用於建立與其他物件沒有任何關係的記錄。

【第八題 / NO. 8】


Universal Containers wants to match Opportunity data from Salesforce to the records in a financial database. What is required to configure an indirect lookup relationship in Salesforce between the Salesforce Opportunity records and those in a financial database?


Universal Containers 公司希望將 Salesforce 中的「機會 (Opportunity)」資料與財務資料庫中的記錄進行匹配。若要在 Salesforce 的「機會」記錄與財務資料庫的記錄之間設定一個間接查詢關係 (indirect lookup relationship)，需要什麼？


A. Salesforce Record ID
     

Salesforce 記錄 ID

B. TEXT(Id)

C. External ID
     

外部 ID

D. CASESAFE(Id)


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
An indirect lookup relationship is a custom relationship between two objects that are linked by an external ID field. The external ID field must be a custom field on the parent object that has the "External ID" attribute enabled.
間接查詢關係 (Indirect lookup relationship) 是兩個物件之間的一種自訂關係，它們透過一個「外部 ID (External ID)」欄位進行連結。外部 ID 欄位必須是父物件上的一個自訂欄位，並且已啟用「外部 ID」屬性。 這種關係通常用於連結 Salesforce 物件與儲存在外部系統中的資料。

【第九題 / NO. 9】


Universal Containers manages leads in a Lead qualification queue where sales reps can accept ownership of the Lead. Campaign members are required to have a sales owner. What validation rule should an app builder configure?


Universal Containers 公司在一個「潛在客戶資格佇列」中管理潛在客戶，銷售代表可以在此接受潛在客戶的所有權。系統要求「行銷活動成員 (Campaign members)」必須有一個銷售負責人。應用程式建構者應該設定什麼樣的驗證規則？


A. AND(ISBLANK(Lead.Owner.Id))

B. NOT(ISNEW() && ISBLANK(Lead.Owner:Queue.Id))

C. AND(ISNEW(), ISBLANK(Lead.Owner:User.Id))

D. NOT(ISBLANK(Lead.Owner:Queue.Id))


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
The validation rule should be AND(ISNEW(), ISBLANK(Lead.Owner:User.Id)). This rule will prevent saving a new lead record if the owner is not a user. This will ensure that campaign members have a sales owner.
驗證規則應為 AND(ISNEW(), ISBLANK(Lead.Owner:User.Id))。這個規則的邏輯是：當 (AND) 這是一筆 新建立的 (ISNEW()) 記錄，而且 (&&) 這筆記錄的 負責人不是一位使用者 (ISBLANK(Lead.Owner:User.Id)) 時，驗證失敗，從而阻止記錄被儲存。這確保了新的潛在客戶在成為行銷活動成員時，其負責人必須是一位具體的使用者 (銷售人員)，而不是一個佇列。

【第十題 / NO. 10】


Cloud Kicks (CK) wants to set up a custom child object to track gift cards issued to a customer. A key requirement is to track the total number of gift cards opened and gift cards issued on an Account. CK wants to permanently ensure the gift cards are unable to be moved across any other Account once it is created. On the gift card object, what type of field should be created to support this requirement?


Cloud Kicks (CK) 想要設定一個自訂的子物件來追蹤發給客戶的禮品卡。一個關鍵需求是，在「帳戶 (Account)」上記錄已開卡和已發行禮品卡的總數。CK 希望永久確保禮品卡一旦建立，就不能被移到任何其他帳戶下。在禮品卡物件上，應該建立哪種類型的欄位來支援此需求？


A. Master-detail relationship
     

主從式關係

B. Roll-up summary
     

總計

C. Formula
     

公式

D. Lookup relationship
    

查詢關係

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should create a master-detail relationship field on the gift card object. A master-detail relationship creates a parent-child relationship where the master record controls certain behaviors of the detail record. This meets the requirements: * Track the total number: This can be done by creating roll-up summary fields on the Account object. * Permanently ensure... unable to be moved: In a master-detail relationship, the child record (gift card) cannot be "re-parented" to another master record (Account) once it is created.
應用程式建構者應在禮品卡物件上建立一個主從式關係欄位。主從式關係會建立一種父子關係，其中主記錄 (Master) 控制著明細記錄 (Detail) 的某些行為。 這滿足了所有需求： * 追蹤總數： 可以在「帳戶」物件上建立總計欄位來計算相關禮品卡的數量。* 永久確保無法移動： 在主從式關係中，子記錄（禮品卡）一旦建立，其父記錄（帳戶）就不能再被更改，也就是無法「更換父親」。

【第十一題 / NO. 11】


Universal Containers has deployed custom tabs to Production via changes sets, without including the profile settings or permission sets. What is the settings for the visibility of custom tabs?


Universal Containers 公司已透過變更集 (Change Sets) 將自訂索引標籤部署到生產環境中，但沒有包含設定檔 (Profile) 或權限集 (Permission Set) 的設定。 在這種情況下，自訂索引標籤的可見度設定是什麼？


A. Custom tabs are default off for all users.
     

對於所有使用者，自訂索引標籤預設為關閉。

B. Custom tabs are default on for all uses.
     

對於所有使用者，自訂索引標籤預設為開啟。

C. Custom tabs are hidden for all users.
     

對於所有使用者，自訂索引標籤是隱藏的。

D. Custom tabs are NOT deployed.
     

自訂索引標籤未被部署。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The setting for the visibility of custom tabs is default off for all users when they are deployed via change sets without including the profile settings or permission sets. This means that the custom tabs are not visible in any apps or navigation menus for any users unless they are manually added by each user or by an administrator.
當自訂索引標籤是透過變更集部署，且沒有包含設定檔或權限集設定時，其可見度對所有使用者來說都是「預設關閉 (Default Off)」。 這意味著這些自訂索引標籤不會出現在任何應用程式或導覽功能表中，除非由管理員或使用者手動將它們加入。

【第十二題 / NO. 12】


When a sales rep submits an account for approval, Universal Containers wants the user to answer additional questions via a popup window to populate additional record fields. What should an app builder use to achieve the desired result?


當銷售代表提交一個帳戶以供審核時，Universal Containers 公司希望使用者能透過一個彈出視窗回答額外的問題，以填入該記錄的其他欄位。 應用程式建構者應該使用什麼來達到預期的結果？


A. Process Builder and Flow
     

Process Builder 和 Flow

B. Lightning component and Process Builder
     

Lightning 元件和 Process Builder

C. Custom picklist field and Process Builder
     

自訂選項清單欄位和 Process Builder

D. Custom button and Flow
     

自訂按鈕和 Flow

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should use a custom button and Flow to achieve the desired result. A custom button is a button that can invoke custom logic or actions when clicked by a user. A Flow is a type of automation tool that can guide users through a series of screens and perform actions based on user input. In this case, the app builder can create a custom button on the Account object that launches a Flow when clicked. The Flow can display a popup window with questions for the user to answer and populate additional fields on the Account record based on the user input.
應用程式建構者應使用「自訂按鈕」和「Flow」來實現此需求。使用者點擊「自訂按鈕」後可以觸發自訂的邏輯或動作。而「Flow」是一種自動化工具，可以引導使用者完成一系列畫面 (screens) 並根據使用者的輸入執行操作。在此情境下，建構者可以建立一個自訂按鈕來啟動一個 Flow，這個 Flow 會顯示一個包含問題的彈出視窗，並根據使用者的回答來填入帳戶記錄上的額外欄位。

【第十三題 / NO. 13】


The marketing team at UVC has a list of 400 leads it wants to upload to Salesforce. The team need to avoid creating duplicate records. Which two actions should be taken to meet this requirement? (Choose 2 answers)


UVC 的行銷團隊有一份包含 400 筆潛在客戶的清單想要上傳到 Salesforce。團隊需要避免建立重複的記錄。應採取哪兩個措施來滿足此需求？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Utilize a Lead Matching Rule and corresponding Duplicate Rule to block newly created duplicate leads.
     

利用「潛在客戶比對規則」和相應的「重複規則」來阻止新建立的重複潛在客戶。

B. Upload the lead list using the import wizard and select a Matching type to prevent duplicate lead creation.
     

使用「匯入精靈」上傳潛在客戶清單，並選擇一個「比對類型」以防止建立重複的潛在客戶。

C. Use Data Loader's update function to import lead and match to existing records based on e-mail address.
     

使用 Data Loader 的更新功能匯入潛在客戶，並根據電子郵件地址與現有記錄進行比對。

D. Enable Duplicate Matching in the Data Management section in Setup and activate the Lead-to_Lead scenario.
     

在「設定」的「資料管理」部分啟用「重複比對」，並啟動「潛在客戶對潛在客戶」的情境。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, B

詳解 (Explanation):
The best actions to take to avoid creating duplicate leads when uploading a list of 400 leads are to utilize a Lead Matching Rule and corresponding Duplicate Rule to block newly created duplicate leads, and to upload the lead list using the import wizard and select a Matching type to prevent duplicate lead creation. The Lead Matching Rule defines the criteria for identifying duplicate leads, and the Duplicate Rule defines the actions to take when a duplicate is detected. The import wizard allows users to choose a Matching type based on the Lead Matching Rule and block or allow duplicates.
為了避免在匯入 400 筆潛在客戶時產生重複，最好的做法是：1. 使用「潛在客戶比對規則」和對應的「重複規則」來阻止重複記錄的產生。2. 使用「匯入精靈」並選擇一個「比對類型」來防止重複。「比對規則」定義了如何識別重複，「重複規則」定義了偵測到重複時應採取的行動。「匯入精靈」則允許使用者根據比對規則來選擇比對方式，並阻止重複記錄的建立。

【第十四題 / NO. 14】


Universal Containers has Public Read/Write as the Account organization-wide default (OWD) setting. Visitors to the customer community site report that they can see all of the company's account records. How should an app builder configure Account sharing so that community users only see their own Account?


Universal Containers 公司的「帳戶」物件全組織預設 (OWD) 設定為「公開讀取/寫入」。客戶社群網站的訪客回報說，他們可以看到公司所有的帳戶記錄。應用程式建構者應如何設定帳戶共用，讓社群使用者只能看到他們自己的帳戶？


A. Create an account record type for external accounts.
     

為外部帳戶建立一個帳戶記錄類型。

B. Define an owner-based sharing rule for external accounts.
     

為外部帳戶定義一個基於負責人的共用規則。

C. Define a permission set for external accounts.
     

為外部帳戶定義一個權限集。

D. Set the account external OWD to private.
     

將帳戶的「外部」全組織預設設定為「私人」。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
The best way to configure Account sharing so that community users only see their own Account is to set the account external OWD to private. This will restrict the access to Account records for external users.
讓社群使用者只能看到自己帳戶的最佳方法，是將帳戶的「外部全組織預設 (external OWD)」設定為「私人 (Private)」。 Salesforce 允許您為內部使用者和外部使用者（如社群使用者）設定不同的 OWD。即使內部 OWD 是公開的，將外部 OWD 設定為私人將會限制外部使用者的記錄存取權限。

【第十五題 / NO. 15】


Cloud Kicks's management team frequently travels and wants to approve requests from their team on the go via Chatter. Where would an app builder enable this ability?


Cloud Kicks 的管理團隊經常出差，並希望能夠透過 Chatter隨時隨地批准團隊的請求。應用程式建構者應該在哪裡啟用此功能？


A. Chatter Feed Tracking
     

Chatter 動態追蹤

B. Object Settings
     

物件設定

C. Chatter Settings
     

Chatter 設定

D. Approval Process Settings
     

批准流程設定

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder would enable this ability in Chatter Settings. Chatter Settings is a setup menu that allows an app builder to configure various aspects of Chatter functionality. One of the options in Chatter Settings is Enable Approvals via Chatter, which allows users to approve or reject requests from their team via Chatter posts or comments.
應用程式建構者應在「Chatter 設定 (Chatter Settings)」中啟用此功能。這是一個設定選單，允許建構者配置 Chatter 的各種功能。其中一個選項是「透過 Chatter 啟用批准 (Enable Approvals via Chatter)」，它允許使用者透過 Chatter 貼文或留言來批准或拒絕團隊的請求。

【第十七題 / NO. 17】


Universal containers (UC) want to delete data in several fields for 5000 lead records. UC export the selected record IDs and fields that need to have data deleted in a csv file. Which two steps should an app builder suggest to meet these requirements? (Choose 2 answers)


Universal Containers (UC) 想要刪除 5000 筆潛在客戶記錄中數個欄位的資料（即清空欄位值）。UC 會將選定的記錄 ID 和需要刪除資料的欄位匯出成一個 CSV 檔案。應用程式建構者應該建議哪兩個步驟來滿足這些需求？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Select the correct record type
     

選擇正確的記錄類型。

B. Use import Wizard to update leads using the CSV file
     

使用「匯入精靈」透過 CSV 檔案來更新潛在客戶。

C. Select insert null values in settings.
     

在設定中選擇「插入 Null 值」。

D. Use Data Loader to update leads using the CSV file
     

使用 Data Loader 透過 CSV 檔案來更新潛在客戶。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C, D

詳解 (Explanation):
The two steps that should be suggested are to select insert null values in settings and to use Data Loader to update leads using the CSV file. Selecting insert null values in settings will allow Data Loader to overwrite existing values with null values. Data Loader is a tool that can import, export, update, or delete large amounts of data. (Note: Import Wizard has a limit of 50,000 records, but Data Loader is generally preferred for this type of mass update operation).
建議的兩個步驟是：在設定中選擇「插入 Null 值」，並使用 Data Loader 來更新潛在客戶。勾選「插入 Null 值」這個設定會允許 Data Loader 將現有的欄位值用空值 (null) 覆寫，從而達到清空資料的目的。對於 5000 筆這樣的大量資料操作，Data Loader 是比匯入精靈更適合的工具。

【第十八題 / NO. 18】


An app builder is preparing to deploy a new app from the sandbox to production using change sets. What two considerations should an app builder keep in mind during this process? (Choose 2 answers)


一位應用程式建構者正準備使用變更集將一個新的應用程式從沙箱部署到生產環境。在此過程中，建構者應記住哪兩項考量因素？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Salesforce Connect automatically establishes a link between environments.
     

Salesforce Connect 會自動在環境之間建立連結。

B. Change sets do not include all components and may have to perform some changes manually.
    ˆ

變更集不包含所有元件，可能需要手動執行一些變更。

C. Users should be logged out of production when receiving inbound change sets.
     

在接收傳入的變更集時，使用者應該登出生產環境。

D. Transactions will revert if the deployment errors.
   ˆ

如果部署出錯，交易將會還原。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C (註：根據題庫文件提供的答案。在實務上 D 也是一個正確的考量，因為 Salesforce 部署是交易式的，失敗會自動回復。但 C 作為最佳實踐，是為了避免部署過程中發生衝突。)

詳解 (Explanation):
The two considerations that an app builder should keep in mind are: Change sets do not include all components and may have to perform some changes manually. Change sets do not support all types of components, such as reports, dashboards, email templates, etc. Users should be logged out of production when receiving inbound change sets. This is a best practice to avoid any errors or conflicts that may occur when deploying changes to production.
建構者應記住的兩個考量是：1. 變更集不包含所有元件，可能需要手動執行一些變更。變更集不支援所有類型的元件，例如報告、儀表板、電子郵件範本等。 2. 在接收傳入的變更集時，使用者應登出生產環境。這是一個最佳實踐，以避免在部署變更到生產環境時可能發生的任何錯誤或衝突。

【第十九題 / NO. 19】


Northern Trail Outfitters uses a custom object to track travel requests. Rangers want to have automatic posts on a record whenever a travel request has been approved. Which feature should be used to accomplish this?


Northern Trail Outfitters 公司使用一個自訂物件來追蹤差旅請求。Rangers 希望每當差旅請求被批准時，記錄上都能有自動的貼文。應該使用哪個功能來完成這項任務？


A. Auto-response rule
     

自動回應規則

B. Workflow rule
     

工作流程規則

C. Feed tracking
     

動態追蹤

D. Feed quick action
     

動態快速動作

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
To have automatic posts on a record whenever a travel request has been approved, feed tracking should be used. Feed tracking enables field updates to be displayed in the Chatter feed of a record or a user profile. Feed tracking can be enabled for standard or custom objects and selected fields.
若要在差旅請求被批准時自動在記錄上發布貼文，應使用「動態追蹤 (Feed tracking)」。動態追蹤能讓欄位的更新顯示在記錄或使用者設定檔的 Chatter 動態中。當「批准狀態」這個欄位的值發生變化時（例如，從「待處理」變為「已批准」），啟用該欄位的動態追蹤就會自動產生一則貼文。

Cloud Kicks 的一位銷售經理希望團隊能花更多時間在外面跑業務，而不是手動輸入他們收集到的名片上的資訊。應用程式建構者應該做什麼來幫助達成這個目標，同時又不犧牲資料品質？


A. Research and evaluate data enrichment products on the AppExchange to automate data entry.

B. Post daily to the Chatter feed any relevant fields that need to be populated.
     

每天在 Chatter 動態上發布任何需要填入的相關欄位。

C. Use Flow to create a data entry wizard to automate data entry.
     

使用 Flow 建立一個資料輸入精靈來自動化資料輸入。

D. Use a combination of workflow rules and formula fields to populate key fields for the sales user.
     

使用工作流程規則和公式欄位的組合來為銷售使用者填入關鍵欄位。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

The best way to help the sales manager achieve their goal of reducing manual data entry from business cards is to research and evaluate data enrichment products on the AppExchange that can automate data entry. Data enrichment products can scan business cards, extract relevant information, and populate fields in Salesforce records. This can save time, improve data quality, and enhance productivity.
幫助銷售經理達成減少從名片手動輸入資料這個目標的最佳方法，是在 AppExchange 上研究和評估能夠自動化資料輸入的「資料豐富化產品」。這類產品可以掃描名片，提取相關資訊，並填入 Salesforce 記錄中的欄位。這可以節省時間、提高資料品質並提升生產力。

【第二十一題 / NO. 21】


When a deal is closed- won, it has to be approved by the owner's manager prior to being added to the leaderboard for a quarterly sales competition. An opportunity is won on the last day of the quarter and the manager is on vacation.
What is recommended to ensure all of the appropriate deals are reviewed and the leaderboard is up to date?


當一筆交易「結案成交 (Closed-Won)」時，必須先由負責人的經理批准，然後才能被加入季度銷售競賽的排行榜。現在有一筆機會在季度的最後一天成交了，但經理正在休假。
建議採取什麼措施來確保所有適當的交易都得到審核，並且排行榜能及時更新？


A. Forward the approval request to the manager's assistant.
     

將批准請求轉發給經理的助理。

B. Set up a delegated approver for the manager
     

為經理設定一個代理批准人。

C. Have the manager log on and reassign the approval request
     

讓經理登入並重新指派批准請求。

D. Use Process Builder to assign a delegated approver.
     

使用 Process Builder 來指派一個代理批准人。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
Set up a delegated approver for the manager is the recommended solution. According to the Salesforce documentation, "A delegated approver can approve records that are submitted for approval by users below them in the role hierarchy."

推薦的解決方案是為經理設定「代理批准人 (delegated approver)」。根據 Salesforce 文件，「代理批准人」可以批准由其角色層級結構中下屬使用者提交以供批准的記錄。 這樣即使原批准人不在，也能由代理人及時處理審批，確保流程順暢。

【第二十二題 / NO. 22】


An app builder wants to create a formula field on an Account to include data from related Contacts but is unable to find the relationship in the formula editor.
What is a limitation of formulas that could be causing the issue?


一位應用程式建構者想在「帳戶 (Account)」上建立一個公式欄位，以包含來自相關「連絡人 (Contacts)」的資料，但在公式編輯器中找不到這個關係。
這可能是由公式的哪個限制所導致的？


A. Unable to reference the child records.
     

無法引用子記錄。

B. A master-detail relationship should be created.
     

應該建立一個主從式關係。

C. Formula field limit reached on the Account object.
     

「帳戶」物件上的公式欄位已達到數量限制。

D. More than 5,000 characters in the formula.
     

公式中的字元超過 5,000 個。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
Formulas cannot reference child records, only parent records. This is a limitation of formulas that could be causing the issue. To include data from related child records, the app builder could use roll-up summary fields or Apex triggers instead.

公式欄位不能從父物件引用子物件的記錄，只能從子物件引用父物件的記錄。這是一個可能導致此問題的公式限制。在本例中，Account 是父，Contact 是子，所以無法在 Account 的公式欄位中直接引用 Contact 的資料。若要包含來自相關子記錄的資料，建構者應改用總計欄位 (roll-up summary fields，需要主從式關係) 或 Apex 觸發器。

【第二十三題 / NO. 23】


What should an app builder consider when choosing a template for a new Lightning record page?

範本在初次儲存後無法更改。

C. A Page structure will automatically adapt to the device being used to view the record page.
     

頁面結構將會自動適應正在用於檢視記錄頁面的裝置。

D. Select a new template for each type of device users use to view the record page.
     

為使用者用來檢視記錄頁面的每種類型的裝置選擇一個新的範本。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
A template for a new Lightning record page determines how the page is divided into regions. The template is responsive and will automatically adapt to the device being used to view the record page.

Lightning 記錄頁面的範本決定了頁面如何劃分為不同的區域。 這些範本是響應式的 (responsive)，會自動適應正在檢視頁面的裝置（例如桌面電腦、平板或手機），以提供最佳的觀看體驗。

【第二十四題 / NO. 24】


An app builder wants to show Groups as the last navigation menu item in the mobile app. However, the app builder is unable to select Groups as one of the items on the drop-down menu.
What could cause this?


一位應用程式建構者希望將「群組 (Groups)」顯示為行動應用程式中導覽功能表的最後一個項目。然而，建構者無法在下拉選單中選擇「群組」作為項目之一。
這可能是什麼原因造成的？


A. Groups is available in the recent section of the navigation menu.
     

「群組」在導覽功能表的「最近」部分中可用。

B. Groups is included m the Smart Search items but unavailable on the navigation menu.
     

「群組」包含在「智慧搜尋」項目中，但在導覽功能表中不可用。

C. Groups is unavailable in the selected list for the navigation menu.
     

「群組」在導覽功能表的已選清單中不可用。

D. Groups is available in the Chatter section of the navigation menu.
     

「群組」在導覽功能表的 Chatter 部分中可用。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
Groups is available in the Chatter section of the navigation menu, not in the selected list for the navigation menu. According to the Salesforce documentation, "Groups appear in Chatter, not in Navigation Menu."

在設定行動應用程式的導覽功能表時，「群組」本身並不是一個可以獨立加入的項目。它被歸類在「Chatter」項目之下。因此，要讓使用者存取群組，應將「Chatter」項目加入導覽功能表。

【第二十五題 / NO. 25】


Cloud Kicks has five years of sales data and would like to track when customers made their first purchase.
How should an app builder use a roll-up summary to meet the requirements?


Cloud Kicks 公司擁有五年的銷售資料，並希望追蹤客戶首次購買的時間。
應用程式建構者應如何使用總計欄位來滿足此需求？


A. Create a new roll-up summary field called First Order Date, using Type MIN on the Opportunity Close Date with a filter where IsWon = TRU

E.
     

建立一個名為「首次訂單日期」的總計欄位，對「機會結束日期」使用 MIN (最小值) 類型，並設定篩選條件為 IsWon = TRUE。

B. Create a new date field called First Order Date, create a new Workflow to set the date, and roll up the value with a filter where IsWon = TRU

E.
     

建立一個名為「首次訂單日期」的日期欄位，建立一個新的工作流程來設定日期，並使用篩選條件 IsWon = TRUE 來匯總該值。

C. Create a new roll-up summary field called First Order Date, using Type SUM on Opportunity Close Date.
     

建立一個名為「首次訂單日期」的總計欄位，對「機會結束日期」使用 SUM (加總) 類型。

D. Create a new date field called First Order Date, then create a roll-up summary to update the field using Type MIN.
     

建立一個名為「首次訂單日期」的日期欄位，然後建立一個總計欄位以使用 MIN (最小值) 類型來更新該欄位。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should create a new roll-up summary field called First Order Date, using Type MIN on the Opportunity Close Date with a filter where IsWon = TRU

E. A roll-up summary field calculates values from related records. In this case, the app builder can create a roll-up summary field on the Account object that calculates the minimum (earliest) value of the Opportunity Close Date field from the related opportunities where IsWon = TRU

E. This will show when customers made their first purchase.

為了找到「首次」購買日期，我們需要找到所有「已成交 (IsWon = TRUE)」的機會中，最早的「結束日期」。總計欄位 (Roll-up summary field) 正好可以滿足此需求。我們可以在 Account 物件上建立一個總計欄位，設定它匯總相關 Opportunity 物件的資料，匯總類型選擇「MIN (最小值)」，並篩選出 IsWon = TRUE 的機會，這樣就能得到最早的成交日期。


【第二十六題 / NO. 26】


An app builder at DreamHouse Realty created a custom object which has fields containing data from two different objects via related lookups.
What is needed to create "with" or "without" reports on the new custom object?


DreamHouse Realty 的一位應用程式建構者建立了一個自訂物件，該物件的欄位透過相關查詢 (related lookups) 包含了來自另外兩個不同物件的資料。
若要在此新自訂物件上建立「包含 (with)」或「不包含 (without)」類型的報告，需要什麼？


A. Row-Level Formula
     

資料列層級公式

B. Report Bucket Field
     

報告分類欄位

C. Report Filters
     

報告篩選器

D. Custom Report Type
     

自訂報告類型

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
To create "with" or "without" reports on the new custom object, a custom report type is needed. A custom report type defines the relationship between one or more standard or custom objects for reporting purposes. It allows users to select which fields they want to display in their reports and filter by related objects.

要建立「包含」或「不包含」特定關聯物件的報告（例如，「A 物件包含相關的 B 物件」或「A 物件不包含相關的 C 物件」），需要建立一個「自訂報告類型 (Custom Report Type)」。自訂報告類型可以定義報告中物件之間的關係，讓您可以報告一個主要物件與其相關或不相關的其他物件的資料。

【第二十七題 / NO. 27】


Ursa Major Solar wants to provide sales console users with an Incredible experience, with the most-used components easily accessible at all times.
What solution can enable reps to see and access these components from anywhere within the app without leaving the pages where the team is working?


Ursa Major Solar 公司希望為銷售主控台 (sales console) 的使用者提供絕佳的體驗，讓最常用的元件能隨時輕鬆存取。
什麼解決方案能讓銷售代表在應用程式內的任何地方都能看到並存取這些元件，而無需離開他們正在工作的頁面？


A. Favorites
     

我的最愛

B. Home page
     

首頁

C. Global actions
     

全域動作

D. Utility bar
     

公用程式列

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
The best solution to enable reps to see and access the most-used components from anywhere within the app without leaving the page they are working on is Utility bar. This is a footer that can be added to any Lightning app and can contain tools such as history, notes, or softphone.

最好的解決方案是「公用程式列 (Utility bar)」。這是一個可以新增到任何 Lightning 應用程式頁尾的固定工具列，可以包含像是歷史記錄、筆記或軟體電話等工具。 它讓使用者無論在哪個頁面工作，都能隨時存取這些常用元件。

【第二十八題 / NO. 28】


An app builder has downloaded a component from the AppExchange successfully; however, they are unable to add it to the Lightning home page.
Which two reasons can be preventing the app builder from being able to add the custom component? (Choose 2 answers)


一位應用程式建構者已成功從 AppExchange 下載了一個元件；然而，他們無法將其新增到 Lightning 首頁上。
哪兩個原因可能會阻止建構者新增這個自訂元件？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. My Domain must be deployed to add custom components to the page with the App Builder.
     

必須部署「我的網域 (My Domain)」，才能使用 App Builder 將自訂元件新增到頁面。

B. A custom tab must be created to add custom components to the page with the App Builder.
     

必須建立一個自訂索引標籤，才能使用 App Builder 將自訂元件新增到頁面。

C. The component requires a developer permission to add it to the page with the App Builder.
     

該元件需要開發人員權限才能使用 App Builder 將其新增到頁面。

D. The component is tagged for record pages instead of home pages and is not showing up in the App Builder.
     

該元件被標記為用於「記錄頁面」而非「首頁」，因此未顯示在 App Builder 中。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, D

詳解 (Explanation):
Two reasons that can prevent an app builder from adding a custom component to the Lightning home page are if My Domain is not deployed, or if the component is tagged for record pages instead of home pages. My Domain must be deployed to add custom components to the page with the App Builder, as it enables Lightning components and other features. The component must be tagged for home pages in its configuration file, otherwise it will not show up in the App Builder for home pages.

有兩個可能的原因：1. 未部署「我的網域 (My Domain)」：要使用自訂 Lightning 元件，必須先在組織中設定並部署 My Domain。 2. 元件用途標記錯誤：Lightning 元件在其設定檔中會定義它適用於哪些頁面類型（如首頁、記錄頁面、應用程式頁面）。如果這個元件被標記為只能用於「記錄頁面」，那麼在編輯「首頁」時，它就不會出現在可選元件清單中。

【第二十九題 / NO. 29】


Ursa Major Solar (UMS) is looking to hire some new employees. UMS wants to allow the same applicant to apply for multiple open positions using a single application.
What should an app builder recommend to meet these requirements?


Ursa Major Solar (UMS) 正在招聘新員工。UMS 希望允許同一位申請人使用單一申請資料來應徵多個開放職位。
應用程式建構者應推薦什麼方案來滿足這些需求？
(註：此題的選項與答案可能存在邏輯上的混淆，但我們以題庫提供的答案為主來解釋。此情境是典型的多對多關係：一個申請人(Applicant)可以申請多個職位(Open Position)，一個職位也可以被多個申請人申請。這需要一個稱為「申請(Application)」的連接物件。)


A. Create a master-detail relationship on Open_Position__c to Application__c
     

在 Open_Position__c 上建立一個到 Application__c 的主從式關係。

B. Create a master-detail relationship held on Applicant__c to Application__c
     

在 Applicant__c 上建立一個到 Application__c 的主從式關係。

C. Create a master-detail relationship field on Application__c to Open_Position__c
     

在 Application__c 上建立一個到 Open_Position__c 的主從式關係欄位。

D. Create a master-detail relationship field on Applicant__c to Application__c
     

在 Applicant__c 上建立一個到 Application__c 的主從式關係欄位。
(註：選項 B 和 D 的描述幾乎相同。)

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D (根據題庫)

詳解 (Explanation):
Create a master-detail relationship field on Applicant_c to Application_c is what the app builder should recommend to meet the requirements of allowing the same applicant to apply for multiple open positions using a single application. This will create a many-to-many relationship between Applicant_c and Open_Position_c using Application_c as a junction object.
(中文詳解 - 基於正確的多對多模型)
為了實現多對多關係，需要一個「連接物件 (Junction Object)」，在此情境中即為 Application__c。這個連接物件應該分別與 Applicant__c 和 Open_Position__c 建立主從式關係。也就是說，Application__c 上會有兩個 Master-Detail 欄位，一個指向 Applicant__c，另一個指向 Open_Position__c。雖然題庫提供的選項和答案 (D) 的描述不夠精確，但其核心思想是利用 Application__c 作為連接物件來建立多對多關係。

【第三十題 / NO. 30】


Universal Containers wants sales reps to get permission from their managers before deleting Opportunities.
What can be used to meet these requirements?


Universal Containers 公司希望銷售代表在刪除「機會 (Opportunities)」之前，必須先獲得其經理的許可。
可以使用什麼來滿足這些需求？


A. Process Builder with Submit for Approval action.
     

帶有「提交以供批准」動作的 Process Builder。

B. Approval Process with a triggered Flow process.
     

帶有觸發式 Flow 流程的批准流程。

C. Approval Process with Time-Dependent Workflow action.
     

帶有時間相依工作流程動作的批准流程。

D. Two-step Approval Process.
     

兩步驟批准流程。
(註：此題答案在實務上可以有多種解法，但題庫提供的答案可能基於特定的邏輯。)

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D (根據題庫)

詳解 (Explanation):
The feature that can be used to meet these requirements is two-step approval process. An approval process defines the steps and criteria for approving records. A two-step approval process requires two levels of approval before a record can be deleted. The app builder can configure an approval process for opportunities that requires sales reps to submit their delete requests for approval from their managers.

雖然題目只要求經理批准，但「批准流程 (Approval Process)」是處理此類需求的核心功能。一個批准流程定義了批准記錄的步驟和標準。建構者可以設定一個批准流程，當記錄被提交刪除時（可以透過自訂按鈕+Flow來觸發），需要先由經理批准。 題庫的答案 D「兩步驟批准流程」可能是一個寬泛的說法，意指使用批准流程這個機制，其中至少包含一個步驟（提交給經理）。在實務上，更精確的解法是選項 A 的概念，即透過自動化（如 Flow 或 Apex Trigger）在刪除前觸發一個「提交以供批准」的動作，來啟動一個批准流程。
