【第三十三題 / NO. 33】


An app builder at Ursa Major Solar has been working on a new custom app in a sandbox that has been upgraded to the next major Salesforce version, and their production instance is still on the current Salesforce version. The development is complete and they are ready to deploy a change set.
What should the app builder consider when planning the deployment?


Ursa Major Solar 的一位應用程式建構者在一個沙箱中開發新的自訂應用程式，該沙箱已經升級到下一個主要的 Salesforce 版本，而他們的生產環境仍在使用當前的 Salesforce 版本。開發工作已完成，他們準備部署一個變更集。
在規劃部署時，建構者應該考慮什麼？


A. It will fail if there is a feature only available in the next version.
     

如果包含只有在下一個版本中才有的功能，部署將會失敗。

B. The change set components will be upgraded to the next version in production.
     

變更集中的元件將在生產環境中升級到下一個版本。

C. The change set will be automatically deployed when production is upgraded.
     

當生產環境升級時，變更集將被自動部署。

D. The deployment is not possible due to different versions.
     

由於版本不同，部署是不可能的。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
It will fail if there is a feature only available in the next version. According to the Salesforce documentation, "If your sandbox is on a newer version than your production org, you can't deploy any components that are new in the sandbox version."

部署將會失敗，如果變更集中包含了只有在沙箱的新版本中才存在的功能。根據 Salesforce 文件，如果您的沙箱版本高於生產環境版本，您不能部署任何在沙箱版本中新增的元件。 部署是可能的，前提是變更集中不包含任何生產環境不支援的新功能。

【第三十四題 / NO. 34】


A new field has been added to the Applicant object that is part of an unmanaged package. A recruiter ran the Position with or without Applicants report and noticed that the new field was missing as an option to add as a column.
How should an app builder troubleshoot this issue?


一個作為未管理封裝一部分的 Applicant 物件上新增了一個新欄位。一位招聘人員執行「包含或不包含申請人的職位」報告時，注意到這個新欄位沒有出現在可新增為欄位的選項中。
應用程式建構者應如何排解此問題？


A. Adjust the field level security to include in the report type.
     

調整欄位級別安全性以包含在報告類型中。

B. Check Allow Reports for the position and applicant objects.
     

檢查職位和申請人物件的「允許報告」選項。

C. Add the field to the custom report type field layout.
     

將該欄位新增到自訂報告類型的欄位版面配置中。

D. Update the profile with the Manage Public Reports permission.
     

使用「管理公開報告」權限更新設定檔。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should add the field to the custom report type field layout to troubleshoot this issue. A custom report type defines which objects and fields are available for reporting. If a new field is added to an object, it will not be automatically added to the custom report type field layout. The app builder needs to manually add it to make it available as an option to add as a column in reports based on that custom report type.

應用程式建構者應將該欄位新增到「自訂報告類型的欄位版面配置」中。自訂報告類型定義了哪些物件和欄位可用於報告。當一個新欄位被新增到物件後，它不會自動被加入到現有的自訂報告類型中。建構者需要手動編輯該報告類型，並將新的欄位從左側的可用欄位區塊拖曳到右側的版面配置中，這樣它才能在建立報告時被選用。

【第三十五題 / NO. 35】


Universal Containers wants to create a report to show job applications with or without resumes.
What considerations should the app builder be aware of when creating the custom report type?


Universal Containers 公司想要建立一份報告，以顯示「包含」或「不包含」履歷的工作申請。
在建立自訂報告類型時，應用程式建構者應注意哪些考量因素？


A. An app builder is unable to create custom report types for objects they do not have permissions for.
     

應用程式建構者無法為他們沒有權限的物件建立自訂報告類型。

B. Once the report type has been deployed it is unable to be deleted.
     

報告類型一旦部署後就無法刪除。

C. A primary object selection is locked once the custom report type has been saved.
     

主要物件的選擇在自訂報告類型儲存後即被鎖定。

D. When a custom or external object is deleted the report type and reports remain but cause an error when the report is run.
     

當自訂或外部物件被刪除時，報告類型和報告仍然存在，但在執行報告時會導致錯誤。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
The primary object selection is locked once the custom report type has been saved. This means that the app builder cannot change the primary object later. The other options are not true.

一旦自訂報告類型被儲存，其「主要物件 (primary object)」的選擇就會被鎖定，之後無法再更改。 這是建立自訂報告類型時最重要且不可逆的決定之一，因此在儲存前必須仔細確認。

【第三十六題 / NO. 36】


DreamHouse Realty is rethinking its sandbox utilization strategy after acquiring Cloud Kicks. The Salesforce COE already utilizes a partial and a full sandbox, which it refreshes on their own regular schedules. Teams are expanding and have to begin each of their small projects in a sandbox before committing to the larger pool for collaborative testing while still keeping costs down.
What type of sandbox should each team member use?


在收購 Cloud Kicks 之後，DreamHouse Realty 正在重新思考其沙箱使用策略。Salesforce 卓越中心 (COE) 已經在使用一個 Partial Sandbox 和一個 Full Sandbox，並按各自的常規時間表進行重新整理。現在團隊正在擴大，每個小型專案都必須在一個沙箱中開始，然後再提交到更大的池中進行協同測試，同時還要控制成本。
每個團隊成員應該使用哪種類型的沙箱？


A. Full sandbox
     

完整沙箱

B. Developer sandbox
     

開發人員沙箱

C. Developer pro sandbox
     

開發人員專業版沙箱

D. Partial sandbox
     

部分複製沙箱

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The best type of sandbox for each team member to use is a developer sandbox. A developer sandbox is a copy of production that includes only the metadata. It does not include any data. A developer sandbox is ideal for small projects that do not require data testing, such as developing new features or customizations. A developer sandbox is also cheaper than other types of sandboxes.

對於每個團隊成員進行小型專案開發，最適合的沙箱類型是「開發人員沙箱 (Developer sandbox)」。這種沙箱只複製生產環境的設定資料 (metadata)，不包含任何業務資料。它非常適合不需要大量資料進行測試的開發和客製化工作，例如開發新功能。此外，開發人員沙箱是成本最低的選項，並且每天都可以重新整理一次。

【第三十七題 / NO. 37】


Universal Containers uses a private sharing model on Accounts. User A and user B both own Accounts of their own and have both been sent a new account record in an email owned by user C to take a look at. User A is able to open and view the record but user B receives an insufficient privileges error. User A and user B have the same role in the role hierarchy as user C .
What are the three reasons user A has access but user B is unable to access the record? (Choose 3 answers)


Universal Containers 公司的「帳戶」採用私人共用模型。使用者 A 和使用者 B 各自擁有自己的帳戶，他們都收到一封由使用者 C 擁有的新帳戶記錄的電子郵件，讓他們查看。使用者 A 能夠打開並檢視該記錄，但使用者 B 卻收到權限不足的錯誤。使用者 A、B 和 C 在角色層級結構中擔任相同的角色。
使用者 A 有存取權限而使用者 B 沒有的三個可能原因是什麼？(選擇 3 個答案)


A. User A is on the same account team as user C .
     

使用者 A 和使用者 C 在同一個帳戶團隊中。

B. User A and user B have different profiles.
     

使用者 A 和使用者 B 有不同的設定檔。

C. User C has manually shared the record with user A .
     

使用者 C 手動將該記錄與使用者 A 共用。

D. User A was granted an additional permission set.
     

使用者 A 被授予了一個額外的權限集。

E. User A is in a public group that has access via a sharing rule.
     

使用者 A 所在的一個公開群組透過共用規則獲得了存取權限。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C, E

詳解 (Explanation):
The three reasons user A has access but user B is unable to access the record are: 1. User A is on the same account team as user C . 2. User C has manually shared the record with user A . 3. User A is in a public group that has access via a sharing rule. All these are record-level sharing mechanisms that can grant access beyond the role hierarchy. Different profiles (B) or permission sets (D) grant object-level permissions, not specific record access in a private model.

在私人共用模型中，即使角色相同，存取特定記錄的權限也可能不同。以下三種「記錄層級」的共用方式可以解釋這種差異：1. 帳戶團隊 (Account Team)：使用者 A 可能被加入到該帳戶的團隊中，從而獲得存取權限。 2. 手動共用 (Manual Sharing)：記錄的負責人（使用者 C）可以直接手動將該記錄分享給使用者 A。 3. 共用規則 (Sharing Rule)：可能有一條共用規則，將符合特定條件的帳戶分享給某個公開群組，而使用者 A 正好是該群組的成員。 設定檔和權限集主要控制物件級別的權限（例如，能否看到「帳戶」這個物件），而不是單一記錄的存取權。

【第三十八題 / NO. 38】


Due to the complexity of the Universal Containers sandbox release schedule and requirements, it is advised that change sets are used as often as possible to migrate from one environment to another.
Which three common items can an app builder move when using a change set? (Choose 3 answers)


由於 Universal Containers 沙箱發布排程和需求的複雜性，建議盡可能頻繁地使用變更集將變更從一個環境遷移到另一個環境。
使用變更集時，應用程式建構者可以移動哪三個常見項目？(選擇 3 個答案)


A. Web-to-lead
     

網站產生潛在客戶

B. Standard fields
     

標準欄位

C. Custom object
     

自訂物件

D. Apex class
     

Apex 類別

E. Custom field
     

自訂欄位

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C, D, E

詳解 (Explanation):
The common items that can be moved using a change set are custom object, Apex class, and custom field. These are metadata components that can be deployed from one environment to another using change sets. Web-to-lead settings and standard fields are not metadata components that can be moved using change sets.

可以使用變更集移動的常見項目是「自訂物件」、「Apex 類別」和「自訂欄位」。這些都屬於可以從一個環境部署到另一個環境的「設定資料 (metadata)」元件。像「網站產生潛在客戶」這類的設定或「標準欄位」則不屬於可以透過變更集移動的元件類型。

【第三十九題 / NO. 39】


Cloud Kicks (CK) switched to Lightning Experience and started using Chatter across its global workforce to support its fast-paced sales cycle. CK loves Chatter but struggle with gathering feedback from core team members, including understanding who is available to respond.
Which two ways could CK use Chatter to solve this problem? (Choose 2 answers)


Cloud Kicks (CK) 切換到 Lightning Experience 後，開始在其全球員工中使用 Chatter 來支援其快節奏的銷售週期。CK 很喜歡 Chatter，但在收集核心團隊成員的回饋方面遇到了困難，包括了解誰有空可以回應。
CK 可以使用 Chatter 的哪兩種方式來解決這個問題？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Streams
     

摘要

B. Polls
     

投票

C. Out of Office
     

外出

D. Topics
     

主題

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C

詳解 (Explanation):
Polls and Out of Office are two ways that CK can use Chatter to gather feedback and understand availability. Polls allow users to create surveys and collect opinions from other users. Out of Office lets users set a status message and an end date to inform others when they are away or busy.

「投票 (Polls)」和「外出 (Out of Office)」是 CK 可以用來收集回饋和了解可用性的兩種 Chatter 功能。 「投票」允許使用者建立調查並收集其他使用者的意見，這有助於快速收集回饋。「外出」功能讓使用者可以設定狀態訊息和結束日期，告知他人他們何時不在或忙碌，這有助於了解誰有空可以回應。

【第四十題 / NO. 40】


Universal Containers uses the Asset object to track products that are installed at customer locations. A new object, Asset Inventory, has been created to capture details about the asset.
Which approach should the app builder take to show Asset Inventory as a related list on Asset?


Universal Containers 公司使用「資產 (Asset)」物件來追蹤安裝在客戶地點的產品。現在建立了一個新物件「資產庫存 (Asset Inventory)」，用來擷取關於資產的詳細資訊。
應用程式建構者應採取何種方法，將「資產庫存」顯示為「資產」上的相關清單？


A. Create a roll-up on Asset. Add the Asset Inventory related list to the Asset page layout.
     

在「資產」上建立一個總計。將「資產庫存」相關清單新增到「資產」頁面版面配置中。

B. Create a junction object to relate Asset Inventory and Asset. Add the Asset Inventory related list to the Asset page layout.
     

建立一個連接物件來關聯「資產庫存」和「資產」。將「資產庫存」相關清單新增到「資產」頁面版面配置中。

C. Create a lookup relationship on Asset Inventory to Asset. Add the Asset Inventory related list to the Asset page layout.
     

在「資產庫存」上建立一個到「資產」的查詢關係。將「資產庫存」相關清單新增到「資產」頁面版面配置中。

D. Create a master-detail relationship on Asset-to-Asset Inventory. Add the Asset Inventory related list to the Asset page layout.
     

在「資產」到「資產庫存」上建立一個主從式關係。將「資產庫存」相關清單新增到「資產」頁面版面配置中。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
The best way to show Asset Inventory as a related list on Asset is to create a lookup relationship on Asset Inventory to Asset. This will allow one-to-many relationship between Asset and Asset Inventory, and display the related records on the Asset page layout.

要將「資產庫存」顯示為「資產」的相關清單，最好的方法是在「資產庫存」物件上建立一個指向「資產」物件的「查詢關係 (lookup relationship)」。這樣就在「資產」（父）和「資產庫存」（子）之間建立了一對多的關係，並允許您將子物件的相關清單顯示在父物件的頁面版面配置上。

【第四十一題 / NO. 41】


An App Builder has been asked to integrate Salesforce with an external web service. The web service must be notified every time an Opportunity is Won. Which two can satisfy this requirement? (Choose 2 answers)


一位應用程式建構者被要求將 Salesforce 與一個外部 Web 服務整合。每當一個「機會 (Opportunity)」成交 (Won) 時，都必須通知該 Web 服務。哪兩種方式可以滿足此需求？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Use a workflow rule and an outbound message
     

使用工作流程規則和傳出訊息

B. Use a flow and an outbound message
     

使用 Flow 和傳出訊息

C. Use a process and Apex Code
     

使用 Process Builder 和 Apex 程式碼

D. Use a process and an outbound message
     

使用 Process Builder 和傳出訊息

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C

詳解 (Explanation):
Workflow rule and an outbound message or Process Builder and Apex Code are two ways to integrate Salesforce with an external web service. Workflow rule can define criteria and actions for triggering an outbound message, which is an XML message sent to a designated endpoint URL. Process Builder can invoke Apex Code, which is a programming language that can make callouts to external web services using HTTP requests. (Note: Process Builder can also trigger an outbound message, making option D also viable in practice. However, the provided answer is A and C).

1. 工作流程規則與傳出訊息 (Workflow rule and an outbound message)：這是 Salesforce 傳統的、無須編寫程式碼的宣告式方法，用於在滿足特定條件時向指定的外部端點 URL 發送一個安全的 XML 訊息。
2. Process Builder 與 Apex 程式碼 (Process Builder and Apex Code)：Process Builder 可以觸發一個 Apex 類別。在 Apex 程式碼中，開發人員可以編寫邏輯來呼叫 (callout) 外部的 Web 服務。
(註：雖然 Process Builder 也可以觸發傳出訊息，但題庫提供的答案組合是 A 和 C。)

【第四十二題 / NO. 42】


Cloud Kicks (CK) tracks orders against inventory, ensuring its ability to fulfill order requests. CK created a junction object called Request_Inventory__c to enable many-to-many relationships with the Inventory and Order objects.
What does the app builder need to provide to ensure users can view Request_Inventory__c records?


Cloud Kicks (CK) 根據庫存追蹤訂單，以確保能夠履行訂單請求。CK 建立了一個名為 Request_Inventory__c 的連接物件，以實現與「庫存 (Inventory)」和「訂單 (Order)」物件之間的多對多關係。
應用程式建構者需要提供什麼，才能確保使用者可以檢視 Request_Inventory__c 的記錄？


A. Read access to both master objects.
     

對兩個主物件的讀取權限。

B. Apex-based sharing on the first master object.
     

在第一個主物件上基於 Apex 的共用。

C. Sharing rules on Request Inventory object.
     

在「請求庫存」物件上的共用規則。

D. Read access to the first master object.
     

對第一個主物件的讀取權限。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
To view a junction object record, a user must have at least read access to both master objects. This is because the junction object inherits the sharing and security settings from both master objects.

要檢視一個連接物件的記錄，使用者必須至少對其兩個主物件都擁有讀取權限。這是因為連接物件的共用和安全性設定是繼承自它的兩個主物件。如果使用者對其中任何一個主物件的記錄沒有讀取權限，他們就無法看到與之關聯的連接物件記錄。

【第四十三題 / NO. 43】


Cloud Kicks (CK) tracks the support level of its customers on the account record page. CK wants to show a text notification on a case record page when the related account is a platinum-level customer.
How could an app builder meet this requirement?


Cloud Kicks (CK) 在帳戶記錄頁面上追蹤客戶的支援等級。CK 希望當相關帳戶是白金級客戶時，在個案記錄頁面上顯示一則文字通知。
應用程式建構者應如何滿足此需求？


A. Add a rich text area to the Case Lighting page > Set the component visibility of the rich text area to show when the account support level is platinum.
     

將一個 RTF 區域新增到個案 Lightning 頁面 > 設定該 RTF 區域的元件可見度，使其在帳戶支援等級為白金時顯示。

B. Create a text-only Visualforce page > Drag the Visualforce component into the Case page layout > Set its visibility to show when the account support level is platinum.
     

建立一個純文字的 Visualforce 頁面 > 將 Visualforce 元件拖曳到個案頁面版面配置中 > 設定其可見度，使其在帳戶支援等級為白金時顯示。

C. Create a text-only Visualforce page > Clone the case page layout > Drag the Visualforce component into the page, and assign the layout to platinum cases.
     

建立一個純文字的 Visualforce 頁面 > 複製個案頁面版面配置 > 將 Visualforce 元件拖曳到頁面中，並將該版面配置指派給白金級個案。

D. Clone the Case Lightning page > Add a rich text area to the the new page, and assign this page to platinum accounts.
     

複製個案 Lightning 頁面 > 將一個 RTF 區域新增到新頁面中，並將此頁面指派給白金級帳戶。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B (註：在目前的 Lightning Experience 中，選項 A 是更現代且更簡單的作法。但此題庫可能較舊，答案 B 在當時是可行方案。)

詳解 (Explanation):
A text-only Visualforce page can be used to show a text notification on a case record page based on a condition. The Visualforce component can be dragged into the Case Lightning page and its visibility can be set to show when the account support level is platinum. This is the simplest and most flexible way to meet the requirement.

可以使用一個純文字的 Visualforce 頁面，根據條件在個案記錄頁面上顯示文字通知。將這個 Visualforce 元件拖曳到個案的 Lightning 頁面上，並設定其「元件可見度 (Component Visibility)」，使其僅在帳戶支援等級為白金時才顯示。這是在舊版中實現條件式顯示的一種方法。
(現代作法)：更推薦的做法是直接在 Lightning 頁面上新增一個「RTF (Rich Text)」元件，在其中輸入通知文字，然後設定該元件的可見度篩選條件 (例如：相關帳戶 > 支援等級 = 白金)。這完全是宣告式操作，無需 Visualforce。

【第四十四題 / NO. 44】


Ursa Major Solar's service department gets requests for several types of services, such as installation, repair, and maintenance. Service managers need to be able to tell when maintenance was last done on on asset to help determine if they are meeting contract agreements, but the last maintenance date can be difficult to determine when there are many work orders related to the asset. They think it would be helpful to have a field auto-populated on the Asset record when a maintenance work order gets closed.
What tool should an app builder recommend to help meet this requirement?


Ursa Major Solar 的服務部門會收到多種類型的服務請求，如安裝、維修和保養。服務經理需要能夠知道資產上次進行保養的時間，以幫助判斷是否符合合約協議，但當資產有許多相關工單時，很難確定上次保養日期。他們認為，如果當保養工單結案時，能自動在資產記錄上填入一個欄位，將會很有幫助。
應用程式建構者應推薦使用哪種工具來滿足此需求？


A. Visualforce

B. Roll-up Summary
     

總計

C. Apex Trigger
    ˆ

Apex 觸發器

D. Flow


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
A flow is an application that automates a business process. You can use flows to update fields on related records when a certain event occurs, such as closing a work order. In this case, a flow can be used to update the last maintenance date field on the Asset record when a maintenance work order gets closed. (Note: A roll-up summary can only work with a Master-Detail relationship, which may not exist between Asset and Work Order).

Flow 是一個可以自動化業務流程的應用程式。您可以使用 Flow 在特定事件發生時（例如工單結案）更新相關記錄上的欄位。在這個情境中，可以建立一個由「工單」記錄觸發的 Flow，當工單狀態變為「已結案」且類型為「保養」時，Flow 會自動將該工單的結案日期更新到相關「資產」記錄的「上次保養日期」欄位中。 (註：總計欄位需要主從式關係，而資產和工單之間通常不是主從式關係，因此不適用)。

【第四十五題 / NO. 45】


At Universal Containers, the Account object has a Master-Detail relationship with an Invoice custom object. The App Builder would like to change to a lookup field, but is not able to do so.
What could be causing this?


在 Universal Containers，帳戶物件與一個自訂的發票物件之間存在主從式關係。應用程式建構者想要將其更改為查詢欄位，但無法這麼做。
可能的原因是什麼？


A. The invoice must have at least one Master-Detail field for reporting.
     

發票物件必須至少有一個主從式欄位用於報告。

B. The Account record includes Invoice roll-up summary fields.
     

帳戶記錄上包含了發票的總計欄位。

C. The Invoice records have existing values in the Account.
     

發票記錄在帳戶欄位中已存在值。

D. The Account is included in the workflow on the Invoice object.
     

帳戶被包含在發票物件的工作流程中。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The Account record includes Invoice roll-up summary fields. This is correct because roll-up summary fields are only available on the master object in a master-detail relationship, and changing the field type to lookup would delete the roll-up summary fields. You must delete the roll-up summary fields before you can convert the relationship type.

正確答案是帳戶記錄上包含了發票的總計欄位。總計欄位 (roll-up summary fields) 是主從式關係獨有的功能，它們只能存在於主物件上。如果要將主從式關係轉換為查詢關係，必須先手動刪除主物件上所有引用該從物件的總計欄位。

【第四十六題 / NO. 46】


At Universal Containers, the VP of Service has requested a visual indicator flag on each case, based on the case priority. High-priority cases should be flagged red, medium-priority should be flagged yellow, and low-priority cases should be flagged green.
Which formula would accomplish this requirement? (Choose 2 answers)


Universal Containers 的服務副總要求在每個個案上根據其優先順序顯示一個視覺指示旗幟。高優先順序的個案應標記為紅色，中優先順序為黃色，低優先順序為綠色。
哪個公式可以完成此需求？(選擇 2 個答案)
(註：選項中圖片路徑為範例)


A. CASE (Priority, "Low", "img/samples/flag_green.gif", "Medium", "img/samples/flag_yellow.gif", "High", "img/samples/flag_red.gif", "/s.gif")

B. IMAGE (IF(ISPICKVAL (Priority, "Low"), "img/samples/flag_green.gif", IF (ISPICKVAL (Priority, "Medium"), "img/samples/flag_yellow.gif", IF(ISPICKVAL (Priority, "High"), "img/samples/flag_red.gif"))), "Priority Flag")

C. IF (ISPICKVAL(Priority, "Low"), "img/samples/flag_green.gif", IF (ISPICKVAL (Priority, "Medium"), "img/samples/flag_yellow.gif", IF (ISPICKVAL (Priority, "High"), "img/samples/flag_red.gif", "/s.gif"))

D. IMAGE (CASE(Priority, "Low", "img/samples/flag_green.gif", "Medium", "img/samples/flag_yellow.gif", "High", "img/samples/flag_red.gif", "Priority Flag")
(註：選項D的公式缺少了最後一個 else_result 參數，語法不完整)


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, D (根據題庫，儘管 D 語法有誤)

詳解 (Explanation):
The formula for creating a visual indicator flag on each case based on the case priority should use the IMAGE and CASE functions. The IMAGE function returns an image for a given URL, and the CASE function evaluates an expression and returns a value based on that expression. Option A and D use these functions correctly, while option B and C do not. (Note: Option A is missing the IMAGE() wrapper to actually display the image, and Option D is missing a parameter in the CASE function. However, the logic of using CASE is correct. The most complete answer is B, but we follow the provided answer key).

為了顯示圖片，必須使用 IMAGE() 函數。為了根據選項清單 (picklist) 的值來選擇不同的圖片路徑，使用 CASE() 函數比巢狀的 IF() 函數更簡潔。
選項 A：使用了 CASE 函數來返回圖片路徑，但缺少了外層的 IMAGE() 函數來將路徑轉換為圖片。
選項 B：使用了 IMAGE() 和巢狀的 IF()，語法和邏輯完全正確。
選項 C：使用了巢狀的 IF()，但缺少了外層的 IMAGE() 函數。
選項 D：使用了 IMAGE() 和 CASE()，但 CASE 函數的語法不完整，缺少了最後一個「其他情況 (else_result)」的參數。
儘管選項 B 是語法最完整的，但題庫答案為 A 和 D，可能是因為它們展示了 CASE 函數的用法。一個完全正確的寫法應該是：
IMAGE(CASE(Priority, "Low", "/img/samples/flag_green.gif", "Medium", "/img/samples/flag_yellow.gif", "High", "/img/samples/flag_red.gif", "/s.gif"), "Priority Flag")

【第四十七題 / NO. 47】


Cloud Kicks wants to display the number of opportunities that are Closed Won with a Close Date within the last year on the Account detail page.
Which tool should an app builder use to implement this?


Cloud Kicks 希望在帳戶詳細資料頁面上，顯示在過去一年內結束日期且狀態為「結案成交 (Closed Won)」的機會數量。
應用程式建構者應該使用哪種工具來實現此功能？


A. Process Builder

B. Activity Timeline
     

活動時間軸

C. Roll-Up Summary Field
     

總計欄位

D. Workflow Rule
     

工作流程規則

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
A roll-up summary field is a field that calculates values from related records. A roll-up summary field can be used to display the number of opportunities that are closed won with a close date within the last year on the account detail page by using a filter criteria on the field.

總計欄位 (Roll-Up Summary Field) 是專門用來從相關的子記錄中計算值的。我們可以在「帳戶」物件上建立一個總計欄位，讓它計算相關「機會」的數量 (COUNT)，並設定篩選條件為：1. 狀態等於「結案成交」；2. 結束日期在「去年」。這樣就能滿足所有需求。

【第四十八題 / NO. 48】


Cloud Kicks asked the app builder to insert a list of 25,000 records using deduplication for the Race_Track__c customobject.
Which tool should be used?


Cloud Kicks 要求應用程式建構者為 Race_Track__c 自訂物件插入一個包含 25,000 筆記錄的清單，並使用重複資料刪除功能。
應該使用哪種工具？


A. Import Wizard
     

匯入精靈

B. Lightning Object Creator
     

Lightning 物件建立器

C. Data Loader

D. Schema Builder
     

結構描述產生器

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
To insert a list of 25,000 records using deduplication for the Race_Track__c custom object, an app builder should use Data Loader. Data Loader is a tool that allows users to insert, update, delete, or export large amounts of data in Salesforce. Data Loader can also perform deduplication by matching records based on external ID fields or Salesforce record IDs. (Note: Import Wizard has a limit of 50,000 records, but Data Loader is more powerful for these operations).

對於 25,000 筆記錄的資料操作，應使用 Data Loader。Data Loader 是一個用戶端應用程式，可以處理大量的資料匯入、匯出、更新和刪除。它支援透過外部 ID (External ID) 或 Salesforce 記錄 ID 進行匹配，從而實現重複資料刪除 (deduplication) 的功能。 雖然「匯入精靈」支援最多 50,000 筆記錄，但 Data Loader 在處理大量資料和重複資料刪除方面功能更強大，是更適合的工具。

【第四十九題 / NO. 49】


Cloud Kicks works on an annual subscription model. When a sales rep marks an opportunity as closed won, a new opportunity should automatically be created for the renewal. The contracts team works outside of Salesforce but also needs to be notified about closed deals in order to initiate the contract process with the customer.
Which automation solution would meet these requirements?


Cloud Kicks 採用年度訂閱模式。當銷售代表將一個機會標記為「結案成交 (closed won)」時，應自動為續約建立一個新的機會。合約團隊在 Salesforce 外部工作，但也需要收到關於已成交交易的通知，以便與客戶啟動合約流程。
哪種自動化解決方案可以滿足這些需求？


A. Approval Process
     

批准流程

B. Validation Rule
     

驗證規則

C. Process Builder

D. Workflow Rule
     

工作流程規則

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C (註：Process Builder 即將退役，現在的最佳實踐是使用 Flow。但根據此題庫，答案是 Process Builder。)

詳解 (Explanation):
The automation solution that would meet these requirements is Process Builder. Process Builder is a tool that can create and update records, send email alerts, submit records for approval, invoke flows, call Apex classes, and post to Chatter. In this case, it can both create a new opportunity record and send an email alert to the contracts team. A workflow rule can't create a new record.

Process Builder 是能夠滿足所有需求的自動化工具。它可以在一個流程中執行多個動作。當機會被標記為「結案成交」時，Process Builder 可以：
建立記錄 (Create a Record)：自動建立一個新的續約機會。
傳送電子郵件警示 (Send an Email Alert)：向合約團隊發送通知。
工作流程規則 (Workflow Rule) 無法建立新的記錄，因此不適用於此情境。

【第五十題 / NO. 50】


Cloud Kicks wants to make sure that users without the Marketing role are unable to update the Contact Retail_Opt_In__c picklist field to Yes.
What validation rule would an app builder use to prevent other users from making this update?


Cloud Kicks 希望確保沒有「行銷 (Marketing)」角色的使用者無法將連絡人的 Retail_Opt_In__c 選項清單欄位更新為「是 (Yes)」。
應用程式建構者應該使用哪條驗證規則來阻止其他使用者進行此更新？


A. AND($UserRole.Name != 'Marketing', ISCHANGED(Retail_Opt_In__c), ISPICKVAL(Retail_Opt_In__c, "Yes"))

B. AND($UserRole.Name != 'Marketing', Retail_Opt_In__c = "Yes")

C. AND($UserRole.Name = 'Marketing', ISPICKVAL(Retail_Opt_In__c, "Yes"))

D. AND($UserRole.Name = 'Marketing', Retail_Opt_In__c = "Yes")


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The validation rule should check if the user role is not Marketing, and if the Retail_Opt_In__c field has been changed to Yes. The ISCHANGED function returns true if the field value has been changed, and the ISPICKVAL function returns true if the field value matches a specified picklist value.

這條驗證規則的目的是在滿足所有以下條件時觸發錯誤：
$UserRole.Name != 'Marketing'：目前使用者的角色不是「行銷」。
ISCHANGED(Retail_Opt_In__c)：Retail_Opt_In__c 這個欄位的值正在被變更。
ISPICKVAL(Retail_Opt_In__c, "Yes")：Retail_Opt_In__c 欄位的新值是「是 (Yes)」。
只有當這三個條件同時成立時，驗證規則才會阻止儲存，這完全符合題目的要求。

【第五十一題 / NO. 51】


An App Builder wants to deploy a new version of an auto launched flow to production in an active state so that the new functionality Is immediately available to users. What should the App Builder take into consideration when planning the deployment?


一位應用程式建構者想要部署一個新版本的自動啟動流程 (auto-launched flow) 到生產環境，並使其處於啟用狀態，以便新功能能立即對使用者可用。在規劃部署時，建構者應考慮什麼？


A. Verify there is an Apex test that provides test coverage for the Flow.
     

驗證是否有一個為 Flow 提供測試覆蓋率的 Apex 測試。

B. Grant user access to the Flow.
     

授予使用者對 Flow 的存取權限。

C. Manually activate the Flow after deployment
     

部署後手動啟動 Flow。

D. Include the Process Builder calling the Flow In the deployment
     

在部署中包含呼叫該 Flow 的 Process Builder。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should verify that there is an Apex test that provides test coverage for the Flow. An Apex test is a unit test that verifies the functionality and quality of Apex code. Apex tests are required to deploy any change that contains Apex code or references Apex code, such as an auto launched flow. The app builder should ensure that there is an Apex test that covers at least 75% of the Flow logic before deploying it to production in an active state.

建構者應驗證是否有一個為 Flow 提供測試覆蓋率的 Apex 測試。 在部署包含 Apex 程式碼或被 Apex 程式碼引用的變更時，Apex 測試是必需的。 由於自動啟動流程可以被 Apex 觸發，Salesforce 在部署時會將其視為需要測試覆蓋率的元件，以確保其邏輯的穩定性，尤其是當您希望它一經部署就立即處於「啟用」狀態時。

【第五十二題 / NO. 52】


Universal Containers is expecting impacts to operations due to increased demand. The executive team will be reaching out to current customers and want to see the number of open cases for the account and parent account.
Which two tools could an app builder combine to display the number of open cases on the account page? (Choose 2 answers)


由於需求增加，Universal Containers 預計營運將受到影響。高階主管團隊將聯繫現有客戶，並希望看到該帳戶及其父帳戶的未結案個案數量。
應用程式建構者可以結合哪兩種工具來在帳戶頁面上顯示未結案個案的數量？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Flow

B. Workflow
     

工作流程

C. Approval Process
     

批准流程

D. Process Builder


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, D (註：現在建議直接使用 Flow 完成，但根據題庫，此為舊有作法)

詳解 (Explanation):
The two tools that an app builder could combine to display the number of open cases on the account page are Flow and Process Builder. Flow is a tool that allows the app builder to create a declarative automation that can query, manipulate, and display data from multiple objects. Process Builder is a tool that allows the app builder to create a trigger-based automation that can invoke a Flow when a record is created or updated.

可以結合使用 Flow 和 Process Builder。 Flow 具有查詢和操作多個物件資料的能力，可以用來計算帳戶及其父帳戶的未結案個案數量。 Process Builder 則可以作為一個觸發器，在記錄建立或更新時，呼叫該 Flow 來執行計算和更新欄位的動作。

【第五十三題 / NO. 53】


What are two capabilities of Schema Builder? (Choose 2 answers)


結構描述產生器 (Schema Builder) 的兩個功能是什麼？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Editing custom settings
     

編輯自訂設定

B. Creating a new record type
     

建立一個新的記錄類型

C. Showing selected objects on a page
     

在頁面上顯示選定的物件

D. Viewing page layouts in a new window
     

在新視窗中檢視頁面版面配置

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C (註：題庫答案 A 有誤，Schema Builder 無法編輯自訂設定，但此處依題庫提供答案)

詳解 (Explanation):
Schema Builder is a tool that allows app builders to view and modify the data model of their Salesforce org. Some of the capabilities of Schema Builder are: Showing selected objects on a page; Editing custom settings. Schema Builder cannot be used to create a new record type or view page layouts in a new window.

結構描述產生器是一個視覺化工具，用於查看和修改資料模型。其功能包括：
在頁面上顯示選定的物件：使用者可以選擇他們想要查看的物件，並在畫布上以圖形方式看到它們及其關係。
* 編輯自訂設定：根據題庫文件，這也是一項功能（但在實際的 Salesforce 平台中，這項操作通常在「設定」中完成，而非 Schema Builder）。
Schema Builder 無法用於建立記錄類型或檢視頁面版面配置。

【第五十四題 / NO. 54】


An app builder wants to create a report to compare the number of support cases in each status (New, In-progress, or Closed) and by priority (Critical, High, Medium, or Low).
What solution should be used for the report?


一位應用程式建構者想要建立一份報告，以比較每個狀態（新增、處理中或已結案）和每個優先順序（嚴重、高、中或低）的支援個案數量。
應該使用哪種解決方案來製作此報告？


A. Grouping
     

群組

B. Bucket Columns
     

分類欄

C. Custom Report Type
     

自訂報告類型

D. Filters
     

篩選器

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The best solution to create a report to compare the number of support cases in each status and by priority is to use grouping. Grouping allows the app builder to summarize data by one or more fields, such as status and priority, and display them in rows and columns. This requires a Summary or Matrix report format.

比較每個狀態和優先順序的個案數量，最好的解決方案是使用「群組 (Grouping)」。 透過將報告的資料列按「狀態」進行第一層群組，再按「優先順序」進行第二層群組，就可以清楚地看到每個組合下的個案數量。這通常會使用「摘要 (Summary)」或「矩陣 (Matrix)」報告格式來實現。

【第五十五題 / NO. 55】


Universal Containers uses a custom picklist called Account_Region__c on the Account object. The vice president of sales has asked that the value of this field is visible on Opportunities.
How should an app builder create this solution?


Universal Containers 公司在「帳戶 (Account)」物件上使用一個名為 Account_Region__c 的自訂選項清單。銷售副總要求在「機會 (Opportunities)」上也能看到此欄位的值。
應用程式建構者應如何建立此解決方案？


A. Lookup field
     

查詢欄位

B. Field-level security
     

欄位級別安全性

C. Field history tacking
     

欄位歷史追蹤

D. Cross-object formula field
     

跨物件公式欄位

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
A cross-object formula field is a formula field that references fields from another object. This can be used to display the value of the Account_Region__c field on Opportunities, as long as there is a relationship between the two objects.

應使用「跨物件公式欄位 (Cross-object formula field)」。 由於「機會」物件上已經有一個指向「帳戶」的標準查詢關係，因此可以在「機會」物件上建立一個公式欄位，直接引用其相關帳戶的 Account_Region__c 欄位值 (例如，公式可以是 Account.Account_Region__c)。這樣就可以在機會記錄上即時顯示帳戶的區域資訊。

【第五十六題 / NO. 56】


Ursa Major Solar wants to convert the relationship between Galaxy and Star from a lookup relationship to a master-detail relationship so each Galaxy record can be equipped with a roll-up summary count of Star records.
Which two considerations should be made? (Choose 2 answers)


Ursa Major Solar 公司希望將 Galaxy 和 Star 物件之間的關係從查詢關係轉換為主從式關係，以便每個 Galaxy 記錄都能配備一個計算 Star 記錄數量的總計欄位。
應該考慮哪兩項因素？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. The Star records are all required to have an existing value in their Galaxy field.
     

所有的 Star 記錄都必須在其 Galaxy 欄位中擁有一個現有的值。

B. The Galaxy object has fewer than two existing master-detail relationships.
     

Galaxy 物件上現有的主從式關係少於兩個。

C. The Galaxy object is required to contain existing roll-up summary fields.
     

Galaxy 物件必須包含現有的總計欄位。

D. The Star object has fewer than two existing master-detail relationships.
     

Star 物件上現有的主從式關係少於兩個。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, B

詳解 (Explanation):
The two considerations that should be made are: 1. The Star records are all required to have an existing value in their Galaxy field. This is a prerequisite for converting a lookup relationship to a master-detail relationship. 2. The Galaxy object has fewer than two existing master-detail relationships. This is another prerequisite... An object can have up to two master-detail relationships with other objects.

將查詢關係轉換為主從式關係有兩個關鍵先決條件：
1. 子物件 (Star) 上的查詢欄位 (Galaxy field) 在所有記錄中都必須有值。主從式關係要求每個子記錄都必須有一個父記錄，因此不允許該欄位為空。
2. 父物件 (Galaxy) 上現有的主從式關係數量必須少於兩個。一個物件最多只能作為兩個主從式關係中的「主 (Master)」。

【第五十七題 / NO. 57】


A new custom object is being created with a private sharing setting. The business wants to share individual records with specific people or group of people on a case-by-case basis.
What options does the business user have to manually share individual records? (Choose 3 answers)


一個新的自訂物件正在被建立，其共用設定為「私人 (Private)」。業務部門希望能夠根據個案情況，將單筆記錄與特定的人或人群共用。
業務使用者有哪些選項可以手動共用單筆記錄？(選擇 3 個答案)


A. Public Groups
     

公開群組

B. Permission Sets
     

權限集

C. Roles
   ˆ

角色

D. Profiles
     

設定檔

E. Users
     

使用者

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C, E

詳解 (Explanation):
To manually share individual records with specific people or group of people on a case by case basis, users can use public groups, roles, or users. Public groups are collections of users, roles, or other groups. Roles define the level of access... based on their position in the hierarchy. Users are individual people who log in to Salesforce.

當一個物件的 OWD 為「私人」時，記錄的負責人可以透過「共用 (Sharing)」按鈕手動將該筆記錄的存取權限授予其他人。可以授予存取權的對象包括：
使用者 (Users)：直接分享給某個特定的使用者。
公開群組 (Public Groups)：分享給一個預先定義好的使用者群組。
角色 (Roles)：分享給擔任某個角色的所有使用者（以及該角色之下的所有角色）。
權限集 (Permission Sets) 和設定檔 (Profiles) 控制的是物件級別的權限，而不是單筆記錄的存取權。

【第五十八題 / NO. 58】


The Director of customer service wants to receive a notification when a case stays in the "new" status for more than four business hours.
Which two automation processes should be used to accomplish this? (Choose 2 answers)


客戶服務總監希望當一個個案在「新增」狀態下停留超過四個工作小時後，能收到一則通知。
應該使用哪兩個自動化流程來完成此任務？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Escalation rules
     

呈報規則

B. Flow Builder

C. Process Builder

D. Scheduled Apex
     

已排程的 Apex

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C (註：現在建議使用 Flow 取代 Process Builder)

詳解 (Explanation):
Escalation rules and Process Builder are two automation processes that can be used to send a notification. Escalation rules can define criteria and actions for escalating cases based on time or other factors. Process Builder can create a time-based action that triggers an email alert when the case status is "new" for more than four business hours.

有兩種宣告式工具可以實現基於時間的自動化：
呈報規則 (Escalation Rules)：這是專為「個案 (Case)」物件設計的功能，其核心目的就是在個案滿足特定條件（如狀態為 "New"）並經過一段時間後，自動執行某些動作（如通知特定使用者、重新指派負責人等）。這完全符合題目要求。
Process Builder：可以建立一個基於時間的動作。當個案建立且狀態為 "New" 時，可以設定一個排程動作，在 4 小時後觸發一個電子郵件警示。

【第五十九題 / NO. 59】


DreamHouse Realty (DR) is expanding into subsidized housing by partnering with local government entitles. DR uses Sales Cloud and has enabled field history tracking on the Opportunity object. Due to increased Information requirements, the App Dev team is changing Text Area (Long) fields to Rich Text fields to allow for up to 1,000 characters and better descriptions.
Which two considerations should be made by the team? (Choose 2 answers)


DreamHouse Realty (DR) 正在透過與地方政府實體合作，擴展到補貼性住房領域。DR 使用 Sales Cloud，並已在「機會」物件上啟用欄位歷史追蹤。由於資訊需求的增加，應用程式開發團隊正在將「長文字區域 (Text Area (Long))」欄位更改為「RTF (Rich Text)」欄位，以允許最多 1,000 個字元和更好的描述。
團隊應該考慮哪兩項因素？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Rich text field values of all lengths are displayed fully in reports.
     

所有長度的 RTF 欄位值都會在報告中完整顯示。

B. Data loss may occur when changing custom field types.
     

更改自訂欄位類型時可能會發生資料遺失。

C. Field History Tracking records value changes of 255 characters or less.
     

欄位歷史追蹤只記錄 255 個字元或更少的數值變更。

D. Audit Trail is available through REST API extracts.
     

稽核軌跡可透過 REST API 提取獲得。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C

詳解 (Explanation):
Changing custom field types may result in data loss if the new field type is incompatible with the old one. Field history tracking records value changes of 255 characters or less. If a rich text field value exceeds this limit, only the first 255 characters are tracked.

更改欄位類型時需要考慮以下兩點：
1. 可能發生資料遺失：在轉換欄位類型時，尤其是在從容量較大的類型（長文字）轉換為其他類型時，總是有資料遺失的風險。在進行任何轉換前，都應先備份資料。
2. 欄位歷史追蹤的限制：對於長文字區域或 RTF 欄位，欄位歷史追蹤只會記錄前 255 個字元的變更。如果變更發生在 255 個字元之後，將不會被追蹤到。

【第六十題 / NO. 60】


Cloud Kicks has a shipment date on each shipment that is sent out. Dispatchers need more details on the day and time the shipment was sent out. The app builder needs to change the current field type that is used from Date to Date/Time.
What should the app builder be aware of when it comes to data already in the system?


Cloud Kicks 在每次出貨時都有一個出貨日期。調度員需要關於出貨日期和時間的更多詳細資訊。應用程式建構者需要將目前使用的欄位類型從「日期 (Date)」更改為「日期/時間 (Date/Time)」。
關於系統中已有的資料，建構者應該注意什麼？


A. The change will be instant
     

變更將是即時的。

B. Historical data will be updated to 12:00 timestamp.
     

歷史資料將被更新為 12:00 的時間戳。

C. The field name will change.
     

欄位名稱將會改變。

D. Data loss will be experienced.
     

將會發生資料遺失。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
Historical data will be updated to 12:00 timestamp when changing a Date field to Date/Time field. According to the Salesforce documentation, "When you convert a Date field to Date/Time, Salesforce appends '12:00' to existing data in your records."

當您將一個「日期」欄位轉換為「日期/時間」欄位時，Salesforce 會自動為所有現有記錄的該欄位值附加一個預設的時間。這個預設時間是 00:00 GMT (格林威治標準時間)，在許多時區中會顯示為 12:00 AM 或其他時間。因此，所有歷史資料都會被更新，並附帶一個時間戳。

【第六十一題 / NO. 61】


Cloud Kicks is redefining its entire business process to convert the Manager Notes field from a long text area field. The goal is to encourage managers to be more concise in their comments and stay at 255 characters or less. There is preexisting information in the Manager Notes field that often is well beyond the character limit.
What would happen to any existing information if the app builder tries to convert a preexisting long text area field to text area?


Cloud Kicks 正在重新定義其整個業務流程，要將「經理備註」欄位從「長文字區域 (long text area)」轉換。目標是鼓勵經理們的評論更簡潔，並保持在 255 個字元或更少。 「經理備註」欄位中已有的資訊通常遠超過這個字元限制。
如果應用程式建構者嘗試將一個已有的長文字區域欄位轉換為文字區域，現有的資訊會發生什麼情況？
(註：文字區域 (Text Area) 預設長度為 255 字元)


A. Preexisting information will truncate to the first 255 characters.
     

已有的資訊將被截斷為前 255 個字元。

B. Preexisting information in the field will be completely lost.
     

欄位中已有的資訊將完全遺失。

C. Preexisting information will remain even if it was over 255 characters.
     

已有的資訊將會保留，即使它超過了 255 個字元。

D. Preexisting information will cause an error message to pop up.
     

已有的資訊將導致彈出錯誤訊息。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C (註：題庫文件給出的答案 C 和 A 存在衝突 (NO.61 vs NO.193)。根據 Salesforce 官方文件，從 long text area 轉換為 text(255) 會截斷 (truncate) 資料，因此 A 才是正確的行為。但此處我們依據題庫 NO.61 的答案。)

詳解 (Explanation):
Preexisting information will remain even if it was over 255 characters if the app builder tries to convert a preexisting long text area field to text area. However, users will not be able to edit or save records with more than 255 characters in that field until they reduce the number of characters.

根據此題庫的解釋，如果應用程式建構者嘗試將一個已有的長文字區域欄位轉換為文字區域，已有的資訊將會保留，即使它超過了 255 個字元。然而，使用者將無法編輯或儲存該欄位中超過 255 個字元的記錄，直到他們減少字元數為止。

【第六十二題 / NO. 62】


At Universal Containers, each admin and developer use a separate developer pro sandbox. Configuration and code are then migrated to a partial data sandbox for combination and initial testing. Once approved the configuration and code are then migrated to a full sandbox for final load and regression testing before going to production.
When should the full sandbox be refreshed?


在 Universal Containers，每個管理員和開發人員都使用一個獨立的 Developer Pro 沙箱。然後，設定和程式碼會被遷移到一個 Partial Data 沙箱中進行整合和初步測試。一旦批准，設定和程式碼會再遷移到一個 Full Sandbox 中進行最終的負載和迴歸測試，然後才上線到生產環境。
Full Sandbox 應該在什麼時候重新整理？


A. After user acceptance testing is complete.
     

使用者驗收測試 (UAT) 完成後。

B. After each push from the partial data sandbox.
     

每次從 Partial Data 沙箱推送後。

C. After each major release to production.
     

每次對生產環境進行重大發布後。

D. After a new user is added to production.
     

在生產環境中新增一個新使用者後。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
The full sandbox should be refreshed after each major release to production. This way, the full sandbox will have the most updated data and metadata from the production org, and can be used for final load and regression testing before the next release.

Full Sandbox 應在每次對生產環境進行重大發布後重新整理。這樣做可以確保 Full Sandbox 擁有來自生產環境最新的資料和設定資料 (metadata)，從而為下一個發布週期的最終負載和迴歸測試提供一個與生產環境最接近的基準環境。

【第六十三題 / NO. 63】


An app builder at Cloud Kicks created a custom object and related fields in the schema builder.
What next steps should the app builder take to ensure users can access the new object and fields?


Cloud Kicks 的一位應用程式建構者在結構描述產生器 (Schema Builder) 中建立了一個自訂物件及相關欄位。
為了確保使用者可以存取這個新的物件和欄位，建構者下一步應該做什麼？


A. Create a permission set for access to the object and fields.
     

建立一個權限集來存取該物件和欄位。

B. Allow reporting for the object and fields.
     

允許對該物件和欄位進行報告。

C. Assign data types to the fields on the object.
     

為物件上的欄位指派資料類型。

D. Add the fields to the page layout on the object.
     

將欄位新增到物件的頁面版面配置上。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should add the fields to the page layout on the object to ensure users can access the new object and fields. The page layout determines which fields are visible and editable on the record detail page. (Note: Other steps like assigning permissions via profiles/permission sets and creating a tab are also necessary for full access, but making fields visible on the UI is a primary next step).

建構者下一步應將欄位新增到物件的頁面版面配置上。僅僅建立欄位並不足以讓使用者在介面上看到或編輯它們。頁面版面配置 (Page Layout) 決定了在記錄詳細資料頁面上哪些欄位是可見和可編輯的。 (註：要讓使用者完整存取，還需要透過設定檔/權限集授予權限，並建立索引標籤等，但將欄位放在版面配置上是讓使用者能看到資料的首要步驟)。

【第六十四題 / NO. 64】


A new app builder on the Cloud Kicks team is getting familiar with relationships in the data model.
What functionality would present the app builder a comprehensive view of all relationships in one place?


Cloud Kicks 團隊的一位新應用程式建構者正在熟悉資料模型中的關係。
什麼功能可以為建構者提供一個在單一位置查看所有關係的全面視圖？


A. Schema Builder
     

結構描述產生器

B. Lightning Object Creator
     

Lightning 物件建立器

C. Object Manager
     

物件管理員

D. Lightning Record Page
     

Lightning 記錄頁面

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
Schema Builder is a tool that presents a comprehensive view of all relationships in one place. It allows app builders to see how objects are connected and create new relationships.

結構描述產生器 (Schema Builder) 是一個視覺化工具，它可以在一個畫布上展示所選物件及其欄位和彼此之間的關係（如查詢、主從式）。這使得建構者可以宏觀地、全面地理解資料模型中各物件是如何連接的。

【第六十五題 / NO. 65】


Universal Containers (UC) has large data volumes and is nearing data storage limits. The planned solution is to archive historical data to reduce data storage in Salesforce however, UC would still like to use reports, queries, and lookups on the archived information.
Which two options could meet this requirement? (Choose 2 answers)


Universal Containers (UC) 的資料量很大，且已接近資料儲存上限。計劃的解決方案是封存歷史資料以減少 Salesforce 中的資料儲存量，然而，UC 仍希望能夠對封存的資訊使用報告、查詢和查找功能。
哪兩個選項可以滿足此需求？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Big objects
     

大物件

B. Custom objects
     

自訂物件

C. Related objects
     

相關物件

D. External objects
     

外部物件

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, D

詳解 (Explanation):
Big objects and external objects can be used to archive historical data and reduce data storage in Salesforce, while still allowing users to access the archived data using reports, queries, and lookups. Big objects store data within Salesforce, while external objects store data outside Salesforce and integrate it with Salesforce using an external data source.

大物件 (Big Objects)：專為在 Salesforce 平台上儲存和管理海量資料而設計，適合封存用途，並且可以透過 Async SOQL 進行查詢。
外部物件 (External Objects)：允許您將 Salesforce 連接到儲存在外部系統的資料，而無需將資料實際匯入 Salesforce。這樣可以即時存取外部的封存資料，同時不佔用 Salesforce 的儲存空間。

【第六十六題 / NO. 66】


Universal Containers would like to collaborate with its customers within Salesforce, and has decided to enable the "Allow Customer Invitations" Chatter setting.
What permission is granted to Customers when invited to a Chatter Group?


Universal Containers 希望在 Salesforce 內與其客戶進行協作，並已決定啟用「允許客戶邀請」的 Chatter 設定。
當客戶被邀請加入 Chatter 群組時，他們會被授予什麼權限？


A. The ability to invite members to groups of which they are a member
     

邀請成員加入他們所屬群組的能力。

B. The ability to @mention accounts of which they are a contact.
     

@提及他們作為連絡人的帳戶的能力。

C. The ability to request access to public groups
     

請求存取公開群組的能力。

D. The ability to interact with members of their groups
     

與他們群組內的成員互動的能力。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
Customers who are invited to Chatter groups can only interact with members of their groups. They cannot invite other members, @mention accounts, or request access to public groups.

當外部使用者（客戶）被邀請加入 Chatter 群組時，他們的主要權限是在該群組的範圍內進行互動，例如查看貼文、發表評論、按讚等。他們的功能受到限制，不能像內部使用者那樣邀請新成員或存取群組外的資源。

【第六十七題 / NO. 67】


Universal Containers has the Account object's Organization-Wide Default set to Private. The marketing team owns Accounts; however, they also need to be able to see the sales team's Accounts. Both the sales and marketing teams are in completely different branches of the role hierarchy.
What feature should be used to enable marketing to see sales-owned accounts?


Universal Containers 公司的「帳戶」物件全組織預設 (OWD) 設定為「私人」。行銷團隊擁有自己的帳戶；然而，他們也需要能夠看到銷售團隊的帳戶。銷售和行銷團隊在角色層級結構中處於完全不同的分支。
應該使用什麼功能來讓行銷團隊看到銷售團隊擁有的帳戶？


A. Public Group
     

公開群組

B. Flow

C. Workflow
     

工作流程

D. Sharing Rules
     

共用規則

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
Sharing rules can be used to extend access to records owned by certain users or roles to other users or roles. In this case, a sharing rule can grant read-only or read/write access to sales-owned accounts to the marketing team.

應使用「共用規則 (Sharing Rules)」。當 OWD 為「私人」且需要跨角色層級分支擴展存取權限時，共用規則是標準的解決方案。可以建立一條基於負責人 (owner-based) 的共用規則，將「銷售團隊角色」擁有的所有帳戶記錄，分享給「行銷團隊角色」的使用者。

【第六十八題 / NO. 68】


The VP of Sales wants a Chatter post to the All-Sales private group when an opportunity goes to the closed won stage.
What two tools should the app builder use to automate this process? (Choose 2 answers)


銷售副總希望當一個機會進入「結案成交 (closed won)」階段時，能自動在「All-Sales」這個私人 Chatter 群組中發布一則貼文。
應用程式建構者應該使用哪兩種工具來自動化此流程？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Flow

B. Process Builder

C. Big Deal Alert
     

大額交易警示

D. Workflow
     

工作流程

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, D (註：此答案來自舊版題庫，現在的最佳實踐是統一使用 Flow。Process Builder 和 Workflow 都是舊的自動化工具。)

詳解 (Explanation):
Process Builder: This is a type of automation tool that can execute actions based on certain criteria...and then execute an action that posts a message to a Chatter group. Workflow: This is another type of automation tool...the workflow can...execute an action that posts a message to a Chatter group. (Note: The correct tool today would be Flow, as both Workflow Rules and Process Builder are being retired. However, according to this exam material, both are considered correct).

根據此題庫的內容，Process Builder 和 Workflow Rules 都是可行的選項，因為它們都支援「發布到 Chatter (Post to Chatter)」這個動作。
Process Builder：可以設定觸發條件為「當機會階段變為結案成交時」，然後執行「發布到 Chatter」的動作，並指定發布到「All-Sales」群組。
Workflow：同樣可以設定觸發條件，並執行「發布到 Chatter」的外送動作。
在目前的 Salesforce 版本中，Flow 是唯一推薦使用的工具，因為它可以完成上述所有功能且更為強大。

【第六十九題 / NO. 69】


Universal Containers (UC) has a time-sensitive need for a custom component to be built in 4 weeks; UC developers require additional enablement to complete the work and are backlogged by several months.
Which option should an app builder suggest to meet this requirement?


Universal Containers (UC) 有一個時間緊迫的需求，需要在 4 週內建立一個自訂元件；然而，UC 的開發人員需要額外的培訓才能完成這項工作，而且他們的工作排程已經排到了幾個月後。
應用程式建構者應該建議哪個選項來滿足此需求？


A. Use an AppExchange solution.

使用一個 Bolt 解決方案。

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
An AppExchange solution is a pre-built application or component that can be installed from the Salesforce AppExchange. AppExchange solutions can help you meet your business needs quickly and efficiently, without requiring much development effort or expertise.

在時間緊迫且內部開發資源不足的情況下，最快且最有效的解決方案是去 AppExchange 市集尋找預先建置好的應用程式或元件。AppExchange 上的解決方案通常可以立即安裝和使用，大大減少了開發時間和所需的人力。

【第七十題 / NO. 70】


Universal Containers (UC) has created a picklist field called Status on three separate custom objects. UC has a requirement to share the list of values for this field across each object.
Which feature would an app builder use?


Universal Containers (UC) 在三個獨立的自訂物件上都建立了一個名為「狀態 (Status)」的選項清單欄位。UC 有一個需求，是希望這個欄位的選項值列表能在這三個物件之間共用。
應用程式建構者應該使用哪個功能？


A. Field Update
     

欄位更新

B. Global Picklist Value Set
     

全域選項清單值集

C. Dynamic Action
     

動態動作

D. Dependent Picklist
     

相依選項清單

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should use a global picklist value set to share the list of values for the Status field across each object. A global picklist value set is a set of values that can be used by multiple picklist fields on different objects. This can ensure data consistency and reduce maintenance efforts.

應使用「全域選項清單值集 (Global Picklist Value Set)」。這個功能允許您定義一組選項值，然後讓多個不同物件上的選項清單欄位共用這組值。這樣可以確保資料的一致性，並且當需要修改選項時，只需在一個地方更新，所有共用該值集的欄位都會同步更新，從而減少維護工作。

【第七十一題 / NO. 71】


Universal Container wants customers to be able to open cases from a public-facing website.
What should the app builder use to enable visitors to the website?


Universal Container 希望客戶能夠從一個公開的網站上建立個案 (cases)。
應用程式建構者應該使用什麼來讓網站訪客能夠做到這一點？


A. Outbound message
     

傳出訊息

B. Web-to-case
     

網站產生個案

C. Screen flow
     

畫面流程

D. Email-to-case
     

電子郵件產生個案

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should use Web-to-Case to enable visitors to the website to open cases. Web-to-Case is a feature that allows users to create an HTML form that can be embedded into a public-facing website. When visitors fill out and submit the form, a new case is automatically created in Salesforce.

應使用「網站產生個案 (Web-to-Case)」。這個功能可以產生一段 HTML 表單程式碼，您可以將其嵌入到您的公開網站中。當網站訪客填寫並提交這個表單時，Salesforce 會自動根據表單內容建立一筆新的個案記錄。

【第七十二題 / NO. 72】


Accounts at Universal Containers are currently readable by all users but editable only by their owners. Management wants to designate some Accounts as VIP Accounts. Only Account owners should have read access to these VIP accounts.
Which two actions should an app builder take to meet the requirements? (Choose 2 answers)


在 Universal Containers，帳戶目前對所有使用者都是可讀的，但只能由其負責人編輯。管理層希望將某些帳戶指定為 VIP 帳戶。對於這些 VIP 帳戶，只有帳戶負責人應該擁有讀取權限。
應用程式建構者應採取哪兩個行動來滿足需求？(選擇 2 個答案)
(註：此題的答案組合在邏輯上是矛盾的，但我們依據題庫答案進行解釋。)


A. Implement a sharing rule.
     

實作一個共用規則。

B. Configure a permission set.
     

設定一個權限集。

C. Set up an Account Team.
     

設定一個帳戶團隊。

D. Change organization-wide defaults.
     

更改全組織預設值。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, D (根據題庫)

詳解 (Explanation):
Change organization-wide defaults. The app builder can change the organization-wide default for accounts from Public Read Only to Private. This way, only the owners can view and edit their own accounts, unless additional access is granted. Implement a sharing rule. The app builder can create a sharing rule that grants read access to all accounts that are NOT VIP accounts to all users. (Note: The logic presented in the original explanation is flawed. A correct approach would be D only, setting OWD to Private. Then, a sharing rule would be needed to open up access for non-VIP accounts, which aligns with the answer choices.)

為了實現「只有負責人能看到 VIP 帳戶」，而其他帳戶保持可見，正確的步驟如下：
1. 更改全組織預設值 (Change OWD)：首先，必須將帳戶物件的 OWD 從「公開唯讀」改為「私人 (Private)」。這是收緊權限的基礎。
2. 實作一個共用規則 (Implement a sharing rule)：OWD 改為私人後，所有非負責人都看不到帳戶了。因此，需要建立一條基於條件的 (criteria-based) 共用規則，將所有非 VIP 的帳戶分享給所有使用者，賦予他們讀取權限。
透過這兩個步驟的組合，可以達到「VIP 帳戶僅負責人可見，非 VIP 帳戶所有人可見」的目標。

【第七十三題 / NO. 73】


An app builder at Universal Containers has been asked to add the Chatter feed to a custom object record page.
Which approach should the app builder use?


Universal Containers 的一位應用程式建構者被要求將 Chatter 動態新增到一個自訂物件的記錄頁面。
建構者應該使用哪種方法？


A. Add the standard Chatter feed component.
     

新增標準的 Chatter 動態元件。

B. Add the standard related list component
     

新增標準的相關清單元件。

C. Add a custom Chatter feed component
     

新增自訂的 Chatter 動態元件。

D. Add the Chatter feed component from the AppExchange.
     

從 AppExchange 新增 Chatter 動態元件。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
Add the standard Chatter feed component is how an app builder can add the Chatter feed to a custom object record page. First, feed tracking must be enabled for the custom object. Then, using the Lightning App Builder, the standard 'Chatter' or 'Chatter Feed' component can be dragged onto the record page layout.

為了在自訂物件的記錄頁面上顯示 Chatter 動態，首先需要為該自訂物件啟用「動態追蹤 (Feed Tracking)」。啟用後，即可在 Lightning 應用程式建構器中編輯該物件的記錄頁面，並從標準元件列表中將「Chatter」或「Chatter 動態 (Chatter Feed)」元件拖曳到頁面上。

【第七十四題 / NO. 74】


Universal containers wants to display the real time stock price for each account on the account record page.

Universal Containers 希望在每個帳戶的記錄頁面上顯示該公司的即時股價。

顯示即時股價這種需要與外部服務整合的功能，最簡單、最快速的方法通常是從 AppExchange 尋找並安裝一個現成的解決方案。市集上通常有專門為此類需求設計的元件，安裝後只需透過 Lightning 應用程式建構器將其拖曳到頁面上即可。

【第七十五題 / NO. 75】


The app builder at Cloud Kicks has created a custom object named Delivery__c to track the details of products shipped to customers.
Which two actions should the app builder take to prevent users in the shipping department from deleting delivery records? (Choose 2 answers)


Cloud Kicks 的應用程式建構者建立了一個名為 Delivery__c 的自訂物件來追蹤運送給客戶的產品詳細資訊。
為了防止貨運部門的使用者刪除運送記錄，建構者應採取哪兩個行動？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Remove the Delete permission from the Shipper profile.
     

從「貨運員」設定檔中移除「刪除」權限。

B. Change the organization-wide default of deliveries to Private.
     

將運送物件的全組織預設值更改為「私人」。

C. Remove the delete button from the Delivery page layout.
     

從「運送」頁面版面配置中移除刪除按鈕。

D. Use a permission set to remove the Delete permission.
     

使用權限集來移除「刪除」權限。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, D

詳解 (Explanation):
Removing the Delete permission from the Shipper profile and using a permission set to remove the Delete permission are both valid ways to prevent users from deleting delivery records. Removing the delete button from the Delivery page layout will not prevent users from deleting records using other methods, such as list views or reports.

防止使用者刪除記錄的根本方法是控制他們的權限。
1. 從設定檔 (Profile) 移除權限：可以直接編輯貨運部門使用者所屬的設定檔，取消勾選 Delivery__c 物件的「刪除 (Delete)」權限。
2. 使用權限集 (Permission Set)：權限集是用來授予額外權限的。雖然無法用權限集來「移除」設定檔已有的權限，但在實務上，一個常見的最佳實踐是建立一個沒有刪除權限的基礎設定檔，然後再用權限集為需要的使用者「新增」刪除權限。反之，如果權限來自權限集，也可以透過移除權限集來拿掉權限。因此，使用權限集是管理權限的有效方式。
僅僅從頁面版面配置移除按鈕是不夠的，因為使用者仍然可以透過清單檢視或其他工具刪除記錄。

【第七十六題 / NO. 76】


Cloud Kicks wants to set up a new opportunity approval process and execute various action items based on the initial submission.
Which three action types should an app builder use in the approval process? (Choose 3 answers)


Cloud Kicks 想要設定一個新的機會批准流程，並根據初始提交執行各種動作項目。
應用程式建構者應在批准流程中使用哪三種動作類型？(選擇 3 個答案)


A. Email Alert
     

電子郵件警示

B. Outbound Message
     

傳出訊息

C. Task
     

工作

D. Invocable Flow
     

可叫用的 Flow

E. Invocable Process Builder
     

可叫用的 Process Builder

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C, D (註：題庫答案為 A, C, D，但 Outbound Message (B) 也是標準的批准動作之一。此處依題庫答案。)

詳解 (Explanation):
Email alert, task, and invocable flow are three action types that can be used in an approval process. Email alert can send an email message to one or more recipients. Task can assign a task to a user or queue. Invocable flow can launch a flow that performs complex logic and actions.

在批准流程中，可以設定四種標準的自動化動作：
工作 (Task)：建立一個工作記錄，指派給特定使用者。
電子郵件警示 (Email Alert)：向指定的收件人發送一封電子郵件。
欄位更新 (Field Update)：更新該記錄上的一個或多個欄位。
傳出訊息 (Outbound Message)：向外部系統發送一個 SOAP 訊息。
此外，還可以呼叫 Flow (D) 來執行更複雜的邏輯。題庫提供的答案 A, C, D 都是批准流程支援的動作類型。

【第七十七題 / NO. 77】


Universal Containers is setting up Salesforce for the first time. Management wants the sales and marketing teams to have different navigation names in the Salesforce1 mobile app.
Which option is available to an app builder to satisfy the requirement?


Universal Containers 正在首次設定 Salesforce。管理層希望銷售團隊和行銷團隊在 Salesforce1 行動應用程式中擁有不同的導覽名稱(項目)。
應用程式建構者可以使用哪個選項來滿足此需求？


A. Create sales and marketing profiles to ensure read access to different objects
     

建立銷售和行銷設定檔，以確保對不同物件的讀取權限。

B. Create roles for sales and marketing and assign a custom homepage layout for each role.
     

為銷售和行銷建立角色，並為每個角色指派一個自訂首頁版面配置。

C. Create mobile navigation menus for both the sales and marketing profiles.
     

為銷售和行銷設定檔建立行動導覽功能表。

D. Create public groups for sales and marketing and create mobile navigation menus for each group.
     

為銷售和行銷建立公開群組，並為每個群組建立行動導覽功能表。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
Create mobile navigation menus for both the sales and marketing profiles. This is correct because mobile navigation menus allow users to customize the items that appear in the navigation bar of the Salesforce mobile app, and they can be assigned to different profiles.

為了讓不同團隊在行動應用程式中看到不同的導覽項目，應該為他們各自的「設定檔 (Profile)」建立並指派不同的「行動導覽功能表 (Mobile Navigation Menus)」。這樣，當銷售設定檔的使用者登入時，他們會看到為銷售設計的導覽列，而行銷設定檔的使用者則會看到為行銷設計的導覽列。

【第七十八題 / NO. 78】


The services manager wants to make sure the team enters case priority consistently.
What feature can an app builder use to accomplish this?


服務經理希望確保團隊在輸入個案優先順序時能夠保持一致。
應用程式建構者可以使用哪個功能來達成此目標？


A. Path
     

路徑

B. Flow

C. Next Best Action
     

下一個最佳動作

D. In-App Guidance
     

應用程式內指引

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The best feature to use to ensure consistent case priority entry is Path. Path allows users to see key fields and guidance for each stage of a process, such as a case lifecycle. Path can also enforce data quality by making certain fields required at each stage.

最適合用來確保一致性輸入的功能是「路徑 (Path)」。Path 可以在流程的每個階段（例如個案的不同狀態）顯示關鍵欄位和指引。建構者可以在每個階段的「指引 (Guidance for Success)」中明確提示使用者應如何選擇優先順序，或者將「優先順序」欄位設定為該階段的關鍵欄位，以引導使用者填寫。

【第七十九題 / NO. 79】


When an opportunity is closed date is pushed more than 30 days, manager approval is required. An approval process is in place but reps frequently forget to submit for approval to run the process.
How can an app builder ensure that these opportunities are submitted into the approval process?


當一個機會的結束日期被推遲超過 30 天時，需要經理批准。系統中已經有一個批准流程，但銷售代表常常忘記提交以供批准來執行該流程。
應用程式建構者應如何確保這些機會被提交到批准流程中？


A. Change the entry criteria on the approval process to criteria are met and lock the record on initial submission.
     

更改批准流程的進入條件為「符合條件」，並在初始提交時鎖定記錄。

B. Use a validation rule and an email alert to the manager requesting approval.
     

使用驗證規則和一封電子郵件警示向經理請求批准。

C. Submit the record for approval from an automated process.
     

從一個自動化流程中提交記錄以供批准。

D. Give the manager the "API Enabled" permission to permit approval responses by email.
     

給予經理「API 已啟用」的權限，以允許透過電子郵件回應批准。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
To ensure that opportunities are submitted into the approval process... an app builder should use an automated process to submit the record for approval. An automated process can be created using tools such as Process Builder or Flow Builder, and it can define the criteria and actions for submitting a record for approval.

為了避免使用者忘記手動提交，應該使用自動化流程來觸發「提交以供批准」的動作。可以使用 Flow（或舊版的 Process Builder）來建立一個在「機會」物件上記錄更新時觸發的流程。流程的進入條件設定為「結束日期被更改，且新舊日期間隔大於 30 天」。當條件滿足時，流程會自動執行「提交以供批准 (Submit for Approval)」的動作，從而啟動批准流程。

【第八十題 / NO. 80】


Universal Containers has a Lightning record page that supports both the mobile app and desktop. An app builder has downloaded a custom Lightning component from AppExchange, but users are unable to view the component on mobile devices.
What can be the issue?


Universal Containers 有一個同時支援行動應用程式和桌面的 Lightning 記錄頁面。一位應用程式建構者從 AppExchange 下載了一個自訂 Lightning 元件，但使用者無法在行動裝置上看到該元件。
可能的問題是什麼？


A. The record page needs to be activated.
     

記錄頁面需要被啟用。

B. The component has been developed for Desktop Pages.
     

該元件是為桌面頁面開發的。

C. The component needs to be activated.
   ˆ

該元件需要被啟用。

D. The record page template is unable to support mobile devices.
     

記錄頁面範本無法支援行動裝置。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The most likely reason why users are unable to view the custom Lightning component on mobile devices is that the component has been developed for Desktop Pages only. Some components are not supported on mobile devices or have different behavior on mobile devices. An app builder should check the component documentation or metadata to see if it is compatible with mobile devices.

最可能的原因是該自訂 Lightning 元件在開發時，其設定檔中沒有被設定為支援行動裝置 (Phone) 的規格 (form factor)。開發人員可以指定一個元件支援桌面 (Desktop)、行動裝置 (Phone) 或兩者皆可。如果該元件只被標記為支援桌面，那麼即使它被放置在一個同時支援桌面和行動裝置的頁面上，它也只會在桌面瀏覽器中顯示。

【第八十一題 / NO. 81】


An App Builder at UVC would like to prevent users from creating new records on an Account related list by overriding standard buttons.
Which two should the App Builder consider before overriding standard buttons? (Choose 2 answers)


UVC 的一位應用程式建構者希望透過覆寫標準按鈕，來防止使用者在「帳戶」的相關清單上建立新記錄。
在覆寫標準按鈕之前，建構者應該考慮哪兩點？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Standard buttons can be changed on lookup dialogs, list views, and search result layouts
     

標準按鈕可以在查詢對話方塊、清單檢視和搜尋結果版面配置上更改。

B. Standard buttons can be overridden with a Visualforce page
     

標準按鈕可以用 Visualforce 頁面來覆寫。

C. Standard buttons that are not available for overrides can still be hidden on page layouts
     

無法覆寫的標準按鈕仍然可以在頁面版面配置上被隱藏。

D. Standard buttons can be overridden, relocated on the detail page, and relabeled
     

標準按鈕可以被覆寫、在詳細資料頁面上重新定位和重新標記。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should consider two things before overriding standard buttons: 1. Standard buttons can be overridden with a Visualforce page. A Visualforce page can be used to override a standard button and provide custom functionality or logic. 2. Standard buttons that are not available for overrides can still be hidden on page layouts. A page layout can be used to hide a standard button that cannot be overridden by removing it from the layout.

在覆寫標準按鈕前，有兩點重要考量：
可以用 Visualforce 頁面覆寫：您可以建立一個自訂的 Visualforce 頁面來取代標準按鈕的預設行為，例如，點擊「新增」按鈕時導向一個自訂的頁面而不是標準的建立頁面。
無法覆寫的按鈕可以隱藏：即使某些標準按鈕不支援覆寫功能，您仍然可以透過編輯頁面版面配置，將這些按鈕從版面中移除，從而達到隱藏它們、讓使用者無法點擊的效果。

【第八十二題 / NO. 82】


Cloud Kicks wants to start tracking how many shoe subscriptions have been sold for each shoe catalog. A master-detail relationship exists between the Subscription_c and the Shoe_c objects.
Which type of field should an app builder create?


Cloud Kicks 希望開始追蹤每個鞋子型錄已售出多少鞋子訂閱。Subscription_c (訂閱) 和 Shoe_c (鞋子) 物件之間存在主從式關係。
應用程式建構者應該建立哪種類型的欄位？


A. Roll-up summary field
     

總計欄位

B. Lookup field
     

查詢欄位

C. Master-detail relationship field
     

主從式關係欄位

D. Number field
     

數字欄位

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
To start tracking how many shoe subscriptions have been sold for each shoe catalog, a roll-up summary field should be created. A roll-up summary field calculates values from related records on a master-detail relationship. It can count, sum, min, or max numeric values from child records on a parent record.

應建立「總計欄位 (Roll-up summary field)」。由於 Shoe_c (主) 和 Subscription_c (從) 之間已存在主從式關係，因此可以在 Shoe_c 物件上建立一個總計欄位。這個欄位可以設定為 COUNT (計數) Subscription_c 的記錄數量，從而得到每個鞋子型錄售出的訂閱總數。

【第八十三題 / NO. 83】


Universal Containers created a custom object called Component to capture details about products sold.
What approach should an app builder take to show Component as a related list on Product?


Universal Containers 建立了一個名為 Component (元件) 的自訂物件，以擷取所售產品的詳細資訊。
應用程式建構者應採取何種方法，將 Component 顯示為 Product (產品) 上的相關清單？


A. Create a master-detail relationship on Product to Component. Add the Component related list to the Product page layout.
     

在 Product 上建立一個到 Component 的主從式關係。將 Component 相關清單新增到 Product 頁面版面配置中。

B. Create a junction object to relate Component and Product. Add the Component related list to the Product page layout.
     

建立一個連接物件來關聯 Component 和 Product。將 Component 相關清單新增到 Product 頁面版面配置中。

C. Create a roll-up on Product. Add the Component related list to the Product page layout.
     

在 Product 上建立一個總計。將 Component 相關清單新增到 Product 頁面版面配置中。

D. Create a lookup relationship on Component to Product. Add the Component related list to the Product page layout.
     

在 Component 上建立一個到 Product 的查詢關係。將 Component 相關清單新增到 Product 頁面版面配置中。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
To show Component as a related list on Product, a lookup relationship on Component to Product should be created. A lookup relationship creates a loose association between two objects and allows users to relate records from one object to another. A lookup relationship also allows users to add the related list of the child object to the parent object's page layout.

應在 Component (子物件) 上建立一個指向 Product (父物件) 的「查詢關係 (lookup relationship)」。這樣就在兩個物件之間建立了一對多的關係。建立關係後，就可以在 Product 物件的頁面版面配置中，新增 Component 的相關清單。

【第八十四題 / NO. 84】


DreamHouse Realty (DHR) recently acquired Cloud Kicks (CK), a company that is still on Salesforce Classic. DHR is keeping the CK Salesforce org; however, it will migrate this org to Lightning Experience.
Where should the app builder find prebuilt resources to help with this project and overall adoption?


DreamHouse Realty (DHR) 最近收購了 Cloud Kicks (CK)，CK 仍在使用 Salesforce Classic。DHR 將保留 CK 的 Salesforce 組織；然而，它將把這個組織遷移到 Lightning Experience。
應用程式建構者應該在哪裡找到預先建置的資源來幫助這個專案和整體的採用？


A. Import Wizard
     

匯入精靈

B. Lightning Object Creator
     

Lightning 物件建立器

C. AppExchange

D. Flow Builder


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
AppExchange is a marketplace where app builders can find prebuilt resources to help with migration and adoption projects. AppExchange offers apps, components, solutions, and consulting services that can assist with moving from Classic to Lightning Experience.

AppExchange 是 Salesforce 的官方市集，提供了大量由 Salesforce 或第三方合作夥伴開發的應用程式、元件、解決方案和顧問服務。在進行 Classic 到 Lightning 的遷移專案時，可以在 AppExchange 上找到許多有用的工具和資源，例如遷移評估工具、使用者採用儀表板、導覽元件等，這些都可以加速專案進程並提高使用者採用率。

【第八十五題 / NO. 85】


Universal Containers has a new custom object for Invoices that includes an Invoice Number field. Before the Invoice object can be used, invoices will be migrated from an external system maintaining their current Invoice Number. After the migration, Salesforce will be the system of record and each new Invoice created in Salesforce must have a unique Invoice Number.
How should the app builder configure the Invoice Number field?


Universal Containers 有一個新的自訂物件「發票」，其中包含一個「發票號碼」欄位。在使用「發票」物件之前，將從外部系統遷移發票，並保留其現有的發票號碼。遷移完成後，Salesforce 將成為記錄系統，在 Salesforce 中建立的每一張新發票都必須有一個唯一的發票號碼。
應用程式建構者應如何設定「發票號碼」欄位？


A. Create a Text filed for the original Invoice Number and an AutoNumber field for the Salesforce Invoice Number..
     

為原始發票號碼建立一個文字欄位，並為 Salesforce 發票號碼建立一個自動編號欄位。

B. Create a Text field and mark it as a unique external ID field.
     

建立一個文字欄位，並將其標記為唯一的外部 ID 欄位。

C. Create a Text field, then change it to AutoNumber after the migration.
     

建立一個文字欄位，然後在遷移後將其更改為自動編號。

D. Create an AutoNumber field and migrate the Invoices
     

建立一個自動編號欄位並遷移發票。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The Invoice Number field should be a Text field and marked as a unique external ID field. This will allow the migration of invoices from an external system while maintaining their original Invoice Number. It will also ensure that each new Invoice created in Salesforce has a unique Invoice Number.

最佳方案是建立一個「文字 (Text)」欄位，並同時勾選「唯一 (Unique)」和「外部 ID (External ID)」屬性。
文字欄位：可以容納從舊系統遷移過來的、格式不一的發票號碼。
外部 ID：允許在資料遷移時使用這個欄位作為匹配鍵，方便 upsert 操作。
唯一：確保在遷移後，Salesforce 內部建立的新發票號碼不會與現有的重複，保證了資料的唯一性。
選項 C (先文字後改自動編號) 是不可行的，因為自動編號欄位無法從文字欄位轉換而來。

【第八十六題 / NO. 86】


Service agents at Ursa Major Solar want a more condensed case view. Service agents also want to be able to modify the associated contact and account records from the case page layout on the Lightning record page.
Which two components should an app builder use to meet these requirements? (Choose 2 answers)


Ursa Major Solar 的服務專員希望有一個更精簡的個案檢視畫面。專員們也希望能直接在個案的 Lightning 記錄頁面上修改相關的連絡人和帳戶記錄。
應用程式建構者應使用哪兩個元件來滿足這些需求？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. Path
     

路徑

B. Rich text
     

RTF

C. Related record
     

相關記錄

D. Tabs
     

索引標籤

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C, D

詳解 (Explanation):
Related record and Tabs. These are correct because the related record component allows service agents to view and edit fields from a related record on the same page, and the tabs component allows service agents to switch between different views of related lists or other components on the same page, creating a more condensed view.

索引標籤 (Tabs)：使用索引標籤元件可以將頁面上的不同區塊（如詳細資料、相關清單、活動等）組織到不同的標籤頁中，從而使整體畫面更為精簡，避免了過長的滾動。
相關記錄 (Related Record)：這個元件允許您直接在當前頁面（個案頁面）上顯示並編輯另一個相關記錄（如連絡人或帳戶）的欄位，而無需跳轉到連絡人或帳戶的頁面。

【第八十七題 / NO. 87】


An app builder needs to deploy a new account detail page layout from sandbox to production.
Which three components should an app builder include in the Change Set to ensure it deploys successfully and visually as expected? (Choose 3 answers)


一位應用程式建構者需要將一個新的帳戶詳細資料頁面版面配置從沙箱部署到生產環境。
為了確保它能成功部署並且視覺上符合預期，建構者應在變更集中包含哪三個元件？(選擇 3 個答案)


A. Detail page layout
     

詳細資料頁面版面配置

B. Custom fields
     

自訂欄位

C. Custom actions
     

自訂動作

D. Lightning App Builder
     

Lightning 應用程式建構器

E. System administrator profile
     

系統管理員設定檔

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, B, C

詳解 (Explanation):
To deploy a new account detail page layout from sandbox to production, an app builder should include three components in the change set: 1. Detail page layout. 2. Custom fields: Any new custom fields that were added to the layout must be included in the change set. 3. Custom actions: Any custom buttons or actions added to the layout must also be included.

為了確保頁面版面配置能完整且正確地部署，必須包含所有與其相關的相依元件：
詳細資料頁面版面配置 (Detail page layout)：這是部署的核心目標。
自訂欄位 (Custom fields)：如果這個版面配置上放置了任何新的自訂欄位，這些欄位本身也必須被加入變更集中，否則部署會因找不到欄位而失敗。
自訂動作 (Custom actions)：同樣地，如果版面配置上包含了任何自訂按鈕或快速動作，這些動作也需要被加入變更集中。

【第八十八題 / NO. 88】


Ursa Major Solar has a lookup relationship between a custom Galaxy_c object and a custom Star_c object.
An app builder wants to create a roll-up summary field that counts the total number of Star_c records related to each Galaxy_c record.
How would the current configuration impact the ability to achieve the desired result?


Ursa Major Solar 在自訂物件 Galaxy_c 和自訂物件 Star_c 之間有一個查詢關係。
一位應用程式建構者想要建立一個總計欄位，用來計算每個 Galaxy_c 記錄相關的 Star_c 記錄總數。
目前的設定會如何影響達成此目標的能力？


A. The roll-up summary can be achieved by creating a formula field on the Galaxy_c object.
     

可以透過在 Galaxy_c 物件上建立一個公式欄位來實現總計。

B. The lookup relationship will need to be converted to a master-detail relationship before a roll-up summary field can be created.
     

在建立總計欄位之前，需要將查詢關係轉換為主從式關係。

C. The roll-up summary can be achieved by creating a formula field on the Star_c object.
     

可以透過在 Star_c 物件上建立一個公式欄位來實現總計。

D. A roll-up summary field will need to be created on the Galaxy_c object with a field filter that select all related Star_c records
     

需要在 Galaxy_c 物件上建立一個總計欄位，並使用欄位篩選器來選擇所有相關的 Star_c 記錄。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The lookup relationship will need to be converted to a master-detail relationship before a roll-up summary field can be created. This is correct because roll-up summary fields are only available on the master object in a master-detail relationship, and a lookup relationship does not establish a parent-child hierarchy between the objects.

總計欄位 (Roll-up summary fields) 是主從式關係 (master-detail relationship) 的專屬功能。由於 Galaxy_c 和 Star_c 之間目前是查詢關係，所以無法在 Galaxy_c (父物件) 上建立總計欄位來計算 Star_c (子物件) 的記錄。必須先將這個查詢關係轉換為主從式關係，然後才能建立總計欄位。

【第八十九題 / NO. 89】


Cloud Kicks recently implemented the application lifecycle management process to its release management strategy.
Which category handles bug fixes and simple changes?


Cloud Kicks 最近在其發布管理策略中實施了應用程式生命週期管理流程。
哪個類別處理錯誤修復和簡單的變更？


A. Patch
    ˆ

修補

B. Minor
     

次要

C. Major
     

主要

D. Rollback
     

回滾

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The category that handles bug fixes and simple changes is minor. A minor release is a type of release that introduces small enhancements or fixes to existing functionality. A patch release is a type of release that addresses critical issues or defects that affect the functionality or security of an application.

處理錯誤修復和簡單變更的類別是「次要 (Minor)」發布。次要發布通常指的是對現有功能進行的小幅增強或修復。 而「修補 (Patch)」發布通常用於解決影響功能或安全性的重大緊急問題。

【第九十題 / NO. 90】


The finance manager at Universal Containers wants to receive a new business notification email each time a new client is won. The sales manager wants to receive a task letting them know to onboard the new client unless it is a top-tier client.
Which automation tool should an app builder use to best address all these requests?


Universal Containers 的財務經理希望每次贏得新客戶時，都能收到一封新業務通知電子郵件。銷售經理則希望收到一個任務，通知他們去引導新客戶上線，除非該客戶是頂級客戶。
應用程式建構者應使用哪種自動化工具來最好地處理所有這些請求？


A. Record-triggered flow
     

記錄觸發的流程

B. Screen flow
     

畫面流程

C. Apex

D. Approval process
     

批准流程

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
Record-triggered flow is the automation tool that the app builder should use to best address all these requests. According to the Salesforce documentation, "Record-triggered flows automate processes for you. They start when a record is created or updated...". A record-triggered flow can perform actions such as sending an email alert or creating a record based on criteria or conditions.

最適合的工具是「記錄觸發的流程 (Record-triggered flow)」。因為 Flow 可以在單一流程中處理多個條件分支和多種動作類型。
觸發條件：當機會或帳戶被標記為「新客戶贏得」時。
動作 1：無條件發送電子郵件通知給財務經理。
條件分支：判斷客戶是否為「非頂級客戶」。
動作 2：如果條件成立，則建立一個任務指派給銷售經理。
Flow 可以完美地處理這種包含條件邏輯和多種不同動作的複雜場景。

【第九十一題 / NO. 91】


The appraisal team at DreamHouse Realty wants to leverage Salesforce mobile app.
What are three things an app builder should do to optimize mobile experience? (Choose 3 answers)


DreamHouse Realty 的估價團隊希望利用 Salesforce 行動應用程式。
為了優化行動體驗，應用程式建構者應該做哪三件事？(選擇 3 個答案)


A. Use Global Actions to make it easy to perform vital functionality on mobile.
     

使用全域動作，以便在行動裝置上輕鬆執行重要功能。

B. Avoid using default field values so that the user is required to fill in all fields on the screen.
     

避免使用預設欄位值，以便要求使用者填寫畫面上所有欄位。

C. Minimize the amount of formula fields and lookup fields to reduce page load time.
     

最小化公式欄位和查詢欄位的數量，以減少頁面載入時間。

D. Create individual customized layouts for different phone operating systems.
     

為不同的手機作業系統建立個別的自訂版面配置。

E. Put the most important fields in the compact layout so they are easy to find.
     

將最重要的欄位放在緊湊版面配置中，以便於尋找。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C, E

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should do three things to optimize mobile experience: 1. Use Global Actions to make it easy to perform vital functionality on mobile. 2. Minimize the amount of formula fields and lookup fields to reduce page load time. 3. Put the most important fields in the compact layout so they are easy to find.

為了優化行動體驗，應考慮以下三點：
使用全域動作 (Global Actions)：全域動作可以讓使用者從應用程式的任何地方快速執行常用操作（如新建任務、記錄通話），非常適合行動裝置的快速操作情境。
最小化複雜欄位：大量的公式欄位和跨物件查詢會增加伺服器的計算負擔，從而減慢頁面載入速度，這在行動網路上尤其明顯。
善用緊湊版面配置 (Compact Layout)：緊湊版面配置決定了記錄頂部重點區域、清單檢視和相關清單中顯示的關鍵欄位。將最重要的欄位放在這裡，可以讓使用者一目了然，無需過多滾動。

【第九十二題 / NO. 92】


Which two places can an app builder go to see a list of available Custom Lightning components in their org? (Choose 2 answers)


應用程式建構者可以去哪兩個地方查看其組織中可用的自訂 Lightning 元件清單？(選擇 2 個答案)

Lightning Components in Setup: This is a setup menu that allows an app builder to view, create, edit, and delete custom Lightning components in their org.

Lightning 應用程式建構器 (Lightning App Builder)：在編輯任何 Lightning 頁面時，左側的元件面板中會有一個「自訂 (Custom)」區段，其中列出了所有可以在該頁面上使用的自訂元件。

【第九十四題 / NO. 94】


Cloud Kicks wants to display 10 key fields at once in a separate section at the top of opportunity records on the desktop.

重點面板

折疊區段
