詳解 (Explanation):
Highlights Panel. This is correct because the highlights panel component displays key fields from a record at the top of the page, and it can be configured to show up to 10 fields. The fields displayed are determined by the object's compact layout.

應使用「重點面板 (Highlights Panel)」元件。這個元件專門用於在 Lightning 記錄頁面的最頂部顯示關鍵欄位和動作按鈕。它顯示的欄位內容是由該物件的「緊湊版面配置 (Compact Layout)」所控制的，而緊湊版面配置最多可以設定顯示 10 個欄位。

【第九十五題 / NO. 95】


The app builder at Ursa Major Solar has just created a master-detail relationship between a parent object Galaxy_c and child object Star_c.
What would be the effect of creating this type of relationship if users want to report on Galaxy_c with Star_c?


Ursa Major Solar 的應用程式建構者剛在父物件 Galaxy_c 和子物件 Star_c 之間建立了一個主從式關係。
如果使用者想要報告 Galaxy_c 與 Star_c 的資料，建立這種關係會有什麼效果？


A. A Star_c report type with Galaxy_c as a field will be automatically created.
     

一個以 Star_c 為主、Galaxy_c 作為欄位的報告類型將被自動建立。

B. A new custom report type will need to be created for Star_c with lookup fields from Galaxy_c.
     

需要為 Star_c 建立一個新的自訂報告類型，並包含來自 Galaxy_c 的查詢欄位。

C. A Galaxy_c with Star_c report type will be automatically created.
     

一個「Galaxy_c 包含 Star_c」的報告類型將被自動建立。

D. A new custom report type will need to be created for Galaxy_c with Star_c.
     

需要為 Galaxy_c 和 Star_c 建立一個新的自訂報告類型。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
A master-detail relationship between two objects automatically creates a report type that includes both objects. The app builder does not need to create a custom report type for this scenario. The report type will have the format of "Parent object with Child object".

當您在兩個物件之間建立主從式關係時，Salesforce 會自動建立一個標準報告類型，格式為「主物件名稱 包含 子物件名稱」(Parent object with Child object)。因此，系統會自動產生一個名為「Galaxy_c with Star_c」的報告類型，使用者可以直接使用它來建立報告，無需手動建立自訂報告類型。

【第九十六題 / NO. 96】


A user is unable to use inline editing on a list view. A quick check verifies the user should be able to perform inline editing as they have been assigned the appropriate permissions.
Which two conditions should the app builder review? (Choose 2 answers)


一位使用者無法在清單檢視中使用「內嵌編輯 (inline editing)」。快速檢查後確認，該使用者已被指派適當的權限，應該能夠執行內嵌編輯。
應用程式建構者應檢查哪兩個條件？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. If the list view restricts sharing for the user
     

如果清單檢視限制了該使用者的共用。

B. If the list view selected is the recently viewed list view
     

如果所選的清單檢視是「最近檢視」的清單檢視。

C. If the list view contains a chart created by the user
     

如果清單檢視包含使用者建立的圖表。

D. If the list view contains more than one record type
     

如果清單檢視包含多於一種的記錄類型。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, D

詳解 (Explanation):
Two conditions that can prevent inline editing on a list view are if the list view selected is the recently viewed list view, or if the list view contains more than one record type. The recently viewed list view does not support inline editing. The list view must have a single record type to enable inline editing, as different record types may have different fields and values.

有幾個條件會導致即使有權限也無法使用內嵌編輯，其中兩個常見的是：
清單檢視是「最近檢視 (Recently Viewed)」：這個特殊的、由系統自動產生的清單檢視不支援內嵌編輯。
清單檢視包含多個記錄類型：如果清單檢視的篩選條件導致結果中包含多種記錄類型，內嵌編輯功能將被停用，因為不同的記錄類型可能有不同的頁面版面配置和必填欄位規則。

【第九十七題 / NO. 97】


An app builder has modified a Lightning record page for a case and has added an email button item to the page layout; however, users are unable to see the new item on the layout.
What are two potential reasons why users are unable to view the item on the Case Lightning record page? (Choose 2 answers)


一位應用程式建構者修改了一個個案的 Lightning 記錄頁面，並在頁面版面配置中新增了一個電子郵件按鈕項目；然而，使用者無法在版面配置上看到這個新項目。
使用者無法在個案 Lightning 記錄頁面上看到該項目的兩個潛在原因是什麼？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. The page layout includes the case feed component.
     

頁面版面配置包含了個案動態元件。

B. The email button contains JavaScript.
     

電子郵件按鈕包含 JavaScript。

C. The case page layout also contains custom buttons.
     

個案頁面版面配置也包含自訂按鈕。

D. The page layout excludes the case feed component.
     

頁面版面配置排除了個案動態元件。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, B

詳解 (Explanation):
The email button item will not be visible on the Lightning record page if the page layout includes the case feed component or if the email button contains JavaScript. The case feed component replaces the standard buttons on the page layout with actions in the feed. The email button item will not work if it contains JavaScript because JavaScript buttons are not supported in Lightning Experience.

有兩個可能的原因：
版面配置包含個案動態 (Case Feed) 元件：在啟用個案動態的頁面版面配置上，傳統的按鈕區塊會被動態發布者 (Feed Publisher) 中的動作所取代。因此，新增到傳統按鈕區的按鈕將不會顯示。
按鈕包含 JavaScript：在 Lightning Experience 中，不支援包含 JavaScript 的自訂按鈕。如果這個電子郵件按鈕是基於 JavaScript 的，它將不會在 Lightning 頁面上呈現。

【第九十八題 / NO. 98】


Which three Salesforce functionalities are ignored when processing field updates in workflow rules and approval processes? (Choose 3 answers)


在處理工作流程規則和批准流程中的欄位更新時，會忽略哪三種 Salesforce 功能？(選擇 3 個答案)


A. Multiple currencies
     

多重貨幣

B. Field-Level Security
     

欄位級別安全性

C. Validation Rules
     

驗證規則

D. Record type picklist value assignments
     

記錄類型的選項清單值指派

E. Decimal places and character limits
     

小數位數和字元限制

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C, E

詳解 (Explanation):
The three Salesforce functionalities that are ignored when processing field updates in workflow rules and approval processes are: 1. Field-Level Security: This means that the field update will occur regardless of the user's profile or permission set settings. 2. Validation Rules: This means that the field update will bypass any validation rules. 3. Decimal places and character limits: This means that the field update will round or truncate the value to fit the field's format.

由工作流程或批准流程觸發的欄位更新是在後端以系統權限執行的，它會繞過一些前端的 UI 限制：
欄位級別安全性 (Field-Level Security)：即使執行操作的使用者沒有該欄位的編輯權限，欄位更新仍然會成功。
驗證規則 (Validation Rules)：欄位更新會繞過驗證規則。(註：這是一個重要的考量，因為可能導致不符合業務規則的資料被寫入)。
小數位數和字元限制 (Decimal places and character limits)：如果更新的值超過欄位定義的長度或精度，系統會自動截斷或四捨五入，而不會像在 UI 上那樣報錯。

【第九十九題 / NO. 99】


How should an app builder configure access to a contact's Twitter profile for Salesforce mobile app users?


應用程式建構者應如何為 Salesforce 行動應用程式使用者設定對連絡人 Twitter 個人資料的存取權限？


A. Add a formula field to the Contact page layout.
     

將一個公式欄位新增到連絡人頁面版面配置中。

B. Add an AppExchange Lightning Component to the mobile app.
     

將一個 AppExchange Lightning 元件新增到行動應用程式中。

C. Add the Twitter component to mobile view Lightning pages.
     

將 Twitter 元件新增到行動檢視的 Lightning 頁面。

D. Add a Twitter Quick Action to the mobile navigation.
     

將一個 Twitter 快速動作新增到行動導覽中。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
The Twitter component is a standard Lightning component that can be added to mobile view Lightning pages using the Lightning App Builder. It displays a contact's Twitter profile and recent tweets.

Salesforce 提供了一個標準的「Twitter」Lightning 元件。建構者可以使用 Lightning 應用程式建構器編輯連絡人的記錄頁面，並將這個 Twitter 元件拖曳到頁面上。這個元件會自動根據連絡人記錄上的 Twitter 帳號欄位，顯示其個人資料和最近的推文。這個元件同時支援桌面和行動裝置。

【第一百題 / NO. 100】


An app builder has created a change set and deployed a report from their development sandbox for User Acceptance Testing. When the app builder runs the report, no data is returned.
What can be a reason for this?


一位應用程式建構者建立了一個變更集，並將一份報告從他們的開發沙箱部署到使用者驗收測試 (UAT) 環境。當建構者執行該報告時，沒有返回任何資料。
這可能的原因是什麼？


A. Reports have to be deployed with Salesforce DX.
     

報告必須使用 Salesforce DX 進行部署。

B. Reports have to be manually re-created in each environment.
     

報告必須在每個環境中手動重新建立。

C. Data is deployed when added to a change sets.
     

資料在新增到變更集時被部署。

D. Data is unable to be deployed with change sets.
     

資料無法透過變更集進行部署。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
Data is unable to be deployed with change sets. Change sets are used to deploy metadata components such as custom objects, fields, workflows, reports, etc. from one Salesforce org to another. However, change sets do not include any data or records from the source org.

原因是資料無法透過變更集進行部署。變更集 (Change Sets) 只能用來遷移「設定資料 (Metadata)」，例如物件、欄位、報告的結構、流程等，但不包含任何「業務資料 (Data)」，也就是記錄本身。因此，即使報告本身被成功部署到 UAT 環境，如果 UAT 環境中沒有符合報告篩選條件的資料，報告執行後自然會是空的。

【第一百零一題 / NO. 101】


The CFO of Cloud Kicks needs to sign off on any major shoe retail deal that has a discount of more than 30% before the deal can be closed.
What feature would be used to handle this requirement?


Cloud Kicks 的財務長 (CFO) 需要在任何折扣超過 30% 的重大鞋類零售交易結案之前進行簽核。
應該使用哪個功能來處理此需求？


A. Approval Process
     

批准流程

B. Email Alert
     

電子郵件警示

C. Field Update
     

欄位更新

D. Workflow Rule
     

工作流程規則

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
Approval Process is the feature that would be used to handle the requirement of signing off on major show retail deals with more than 30% discount. An approval process automates how Salesforce records are approved in your org.

處理需要簽核、審批的業務需求，標準功能就是「批准流程 (Approval Process)」。您可以建立一個批准流程，設定進入條件為「折扣 > 30%」，並將批准人指定為 CFO。當符合條件的記錄被提交時，系統會自動將其鎖定並發送批准請求給 CFO。

【第一百零二題 / NO. 102】


Properly installing managed packages helps prevent conflicts with customizations made by customers and partners.
What functionality should be used to set up packages?


正確安裝受管理封裝有助於防止與客戶和合作夥伴所做的自訂發生衝突。
應該使用什麼功能來設定封裝以達到此目的？


A. Description
     

描述

B. Allow sharing
     

允許共用

C. Help setting
     

說明設定

D. Namespace
     

命名空間

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
The functionality that should be used to set up packages is namespace. A namespace is a unique identifier that distinguishes one package from another and prevents naming conflicts with other packages or customizations.

應該使用的功能是「命名空間 (Namespace)」。命名空間是一個唯一的識別碼，它會作為封裝中所有元件（如自訂物件、欄位、Apex 類別等）API 名稱的前置詞。這可以確保您的封裝元件名稱不會與安裝組織中已有的自訂元件，或其他安裝的封裝發生命名衝突。

【第一百零三題 / NO. 103】


The case handling process at Universal Containers includes multiple steps Including approvals, notifications, and fields updates. To manage and evaluate all of these changes in a single save operation, an app builder wants to use Process Builder and the Advanced option to let the process evaluate a record multiple times has been selected.
Which two options should the app builder avoid to prevent recursion? (Choose 2 answers)


Universal Containers 的個案處理流程包含多個步驟，包括批准、通知和欄位更新。為在單一儲存操作中管理和評估所有這些變更，一位應用程式建構者希望使用 Process Builder，並已選擇「進階」選項讓流程可以多次評估一筆記錄。
為了防止遞迴，建構者應避免哪兩個選項？(選擇 2 個答案)


A. IF statements
     

IF 陳述式

B. Setting a criteria node to No criteria-just execute the procedure
     

將條件節點設定為「沒有條件—僅執行程序」。

C. Invocable processes
     

可叫用的流程

D. The ISCHANGED function
     

ISCHANGED 函數

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C, D (註：題庫答案為 C 和 D，但其解釋 B 和 C 才是導致遞迴的直接原因。此處依題庫答案，但解釋會澄清。)

詳解 (Explanation):
The two options that the app builder should avoid to prevent recursion are setting a criteria node to No criteria-just execute the procedure and invocable processes. Setting a criteria node to No criteria- just execute the procedure means that the process will always execute the actions regardless of the record values, which can cause recursion if the process updates the same record that triggered it. Invocable processes are processes that can be invoked from another process or a flow, which can cause recursion if the invocable process updates the same record. The ISCHANGED function (D) is actually a tool to prevent recursion by ensuring the process only runs when a specific field changes.

當 Process Builder 設定為可以多次評估記錄時，如果一個動作更新了記錄，就會導致整個流程重新執行，這很容易造成無限循環（遞迴）。
將條件設為「沒有條件」 (B)：如果一個節點沒有任何進入條件，那麼每次流程重新評估時，它都會執行，如果它的動作又更新了記錄，就會立即觸發下一次執行，造成無限循環。
可叫用的流程 (C)：如果主流程呼叫一個子流程，而子流程又更新了觸發主流程的記錄，同樣會導致主流程重新執行，可能造成遞迴。
題庫答案 D (ISCHANGED) 實際上是防止遞迴的常用方法，透過檢查特定欄位是否真的發生變化來決定是否執行動作。然而，根據題庫答案，我們選擇 C 和 D。

【第一百零四題 / NO. 104】


Northern Trail Outfitters wants the field sales team to only see the accounts that they own. Separate North American and European marketing teams should only see accounts in their respective regions. The inside sales team needs to see all accounts in Salesforce.
How can this be accomplished?


Northern Trail Outfitters 希望外部銷售團隊只能看到他們自己擁有的帳戶。北美和歐洲的獨立行銷團隊應只能看到各自區域的帳戶。內部銷售團隊則需要看到 Salesforce 中的所有帳戶。
應如何實現此目標？


A. Set the Organization-Wide Default to Public for accounts. Create criteria- based sharing rules for each marketing team, and create an Inside Sales Team permission set with the "View All" setting for accounts.
     

將帳戶的 OWD 設為「公開」。為每個行銷團隊建立基於條件的共用規則，並為內部銷售團隊建立一個具有「檢視全部」帳戶設定的權限集。

B. Set the Organization-Wide Default to Public for accounts. Create profiles for each marketing team, and create an Inside Sales Team role that is at the top of the Role Hierarchy.
     

將帳戶的 OWD 設為「公開」。為每個行銷團隊建立設定檔，並建立一個處於角色層級結構頂端的內部銷售團隊角色。

C. Set the Organization-Wide Default to Private for accounts. Create criteria- based sharing rules for each marketing team, and create an Inside Sales Team profile with the "View All" setting for accounts.
     

將帳戶的 OWD 設為「私人」。為每個行銷團隊建立基於條件的共用規則，並為內部銷售團隊建立一個具有「檢視全部」帳戶設定的設定檔。

D. Set the Organization-Wide Default to Private for accounts. Create permission sets for each marketing team, and create an Inside Sales Team profile with the "View All" setting for accounts.
     

將帳戶的 OWD 設為「私人」。為每個行銷團隊建立權限集，並為內部銷售團隊建立一個具有「檢視全部」帳戶設定的設定檔。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
Set the Organization-Wide Default to Private for accounts. Create criteria- based sharing rules for each marketing team, and create an Inside Sales Team profile with the "View All" setting for accounts. This combination correctly implements the security model.

這是典型的共用模型設定，應遵循「從最嚴格開始，逐步放寬」的原則：
將 OWD 設為「私人 (Private)」：這是基礎。這樣預設情況下，所有使用者（包括外部銷售）只能看到自己擁有的帳戶。
建立基於條件的共用規則 (Criteria-based sharing rules)：建立兩條規則。一條是「當 Region = North America 時，分享給北美行銷團隊」；另一條是「當 Region = Europe 時，分享給歐洲行銷團隊」。
為內部銷售團隊設定「檢視全部」：可以透過編輯內部銷售團隊的設定檔 (Profile)，授予他們對帳戶物件的「檢視全部 (View All)」權限，這樣他們就可以看到所有帳戶，無視 OWD 和共用規則。

【第一百零五題 / NO. 105】


Universal containers wants to ensure that they are accepting clean data from their users and verify that important fields are entered.
What should an app builder recommend to meet this requirement?


Universal Containers 希望確保他們從使用者那裡接收到乾淨的資料，並驗證重要的欄位都已填寫。
應用程式建構者應推薦什麼來滿足此需求？


A. Update the important fields to be required on the page layout
     

在頁面版面配置上將重要欄位更新為必填。

B. Make a formula field to check the format of the important fields
     

製作一個公式欄位來檢查重要欄位的格式。

C. Create a workflow rule to check the fields are formatted correctly
     

建立一個工作流程規則來檢查欄位格式是否正確。

D. Configure a validation to require a field for a specific record type
     

設定一個驗證規則，要求特定記錄類型的欄位為必填。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
Configuring a validation rule to require a field for a specific record type is the best way to ensure that important fields are entered and formatted correctly. Making fields required on the page layout will not prevent users from entering invalid data using other methods, such as data loader or quick actions.

設定「驗證規則 (Validation Rule)」是確保資料品質和完整性的最佳方式。與僅在頁面版面配置上設定必填不同，驗證規則在資料庫層級生效，無論資料是透過 UI、API、Data Loader 還是其他方式輸入，都會被強制執行。驗證規則不僅可以檢查欄位是否為空（例如 ISBLANK(My_Field__c)），還可以檢查資料的格式是否符合特定模式（例如使用 REGEX 函數）。

【第一百零六題 / NO. 106】


Universal Containers has a single Contact Lightning record page. A component takes up a lot of room on the page and is NOT needed by users with a Marketing profile.
What should the app builder use to solve this Issue?


Universal Containers 只有一個單一的連絡人 Lightning 記錄頁面。頁面上有一個元件佔用了大量空間，但具有「行銷」設定檔的使用者並不需要它。
應用程式建構者應該使用什麼來解決這個問題？


A. Detail page layouts
     

詳細資料頁面版面配置

B. Component visibility filter
     

元件可見度篩選器

C. Field-level security
     

欄位級別安全性

D. AppExchange


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The feature that the app builder should use to solve this issue is component visibility filter. A component visibility filter is a setting that can be applied to a Lightning component on a record page to control when the component is hidden or displayed based on certain conditions. The app builder can use a component visibility filter to hide the component from users with a Marketing profile.

應使用「元件可見度篩選器 (Component visibility filter)」。在 Lightning 應用程式建構器中，可以為頁面上的任何元件設定可見度規則。建構者可以為該元件新增一個篩選條件，例如「User > Profile > Name = Marketing」時隱藏，或者「User > Profile > Name != Marketing」時顯示。這樣，就可以在不建立多個頁面或版面配置的情況下，動態地控制元件的顯示與否。

【第一百零七題 / NO. 107】


Cloud Kicks (CK) keeps track of its shoe inventory in Salesforce. When an order's status is changed to Activated, the inventory for the ordered shoe is reduced. At that point, a SOAP web service on the CK website must be called so that the website is updated to display the correct inventory amount for the shoe.
What should an app builder use to communicate to the CK web service when a shoe's inventory has changed?


Cloud Kicks (CK) 在 Salesforce 中追蹤其鞋子庫存。當訂單狀態變為「已啟用 (Activated)」時，訂購鞋子的庫存會減少。在那時，必須呼叫 CK 網站上的一個 SOAP Web 服務，以便網站更新並顯示鞋子的正確庫存量。
當鞋子庫存發生變化時，應用程式建構者應使用什麼來與 CK 的 Web 服務進行通訊？


A. After-Save Record-Triggered flow
     

儲存後記錄觸發的流程

B. Before-Save Record-Triggered flow
     

儲存前記錄觸發的流程

C. Process Builder

D. Workflow rule
     

工作流程規則

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
To communicate to the CK web service when a shoe's inventory has changed, an app builder should use an after-save record-triggered flow. An after-save record-triggered flow is a type of flow that runs after a record is saved and can perform actions such as updating related records, sending emails, calling external services, etc. A before-save flow is for fast field updates on the same record and cannot make callouts.

應使用「儲存後記錄觸發的流程 (After-Save Record-Triggered flow)」。呼叫外部系統 (Callout) 是一個需要時間的操作，並且必須在記錄成功儲存到資料庫之後才能執行。儲存後流程正是在記錄被認可並儲存後運行的，它支援執行諸如呼叫 Apex 動作（用於執行 callout）、發送電子郵件等非同步或耗時的操作。儲存前流程 (Before-Save) 僅用於快速更新觸發記錄本身的欄位，不支援 callout。

【第一百零八題 / NO. 108】


The DreamHouse Realty (DR) service manager has asked for some improvements in case management to enforce process compliance so that cases are unable to be reverted to an earlier case status, and to ensure that certain fields are required when specific case criteria are met.
What solution should an app builder implement to meet these requirements?


DreamHouse Realty (DR) 的服務經理要求對個案管理進行一些改進以強制執行流程合規性，以便個案無法還原到較早的個案狀態，並確保在滿足特定個案條件時某些欄位是必填的。
應用程式建構者應實施哪種解決方案來滿足這些需求？


A. Workflow Rules
     

工作流程規則

B. Process Builder

C. A Validation Rule
     

一個驗證規則

D. Activities Component
     

活動元件

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
A validation rule can enforce process compliance by preventing users from saving records that do not meet certain criteria. In this case, a validation rule can prevent users from reverting to an earlier case status or leaving certain fields blank when specific case criteria are met.

應使用「驗證規則 (Validation Rule)」。驗證規則是在使用者嘗試儲存記錄時觸發的，如果公式條件為真，則會阻止儲存並顯示錯誤訊息。它可以完美地處理這兩個需求：
防止狀態還原：可以使用 PRIORVALUE() 函數來比較狀態欄位的前一個值和當前值，從而阻止狀態向後移動。
條件式必填：可以設定一個規則，例如 AND(ISPICKVAL(Status, "Closed"), ISBLANK(Resolution__c))，來確保在狀態為「已結案」時，「解決方案」欄位必須填寫。

【第一百零九題 / NO. 109】


Universal Containers wants to improve the process to create Opportunity records related to an Account. Many fields can be populated based on the Account record. Some fields require input from the user.
What should an app builder configure to meet the requirement?


Universal Containers 希望改善從「帳戶」建立相關「機會」記錄的流程。許多欄位可以根據帳戶記錄自動填入，但有些欄位需要使用者輸入。
應用程式建構者應如何設定以滿足此需求？


A. Process Builder triggered from Opportunity update
     

由機會更新觸發的 Process Builder。

B. Quick Action on the Account object
     

在「帳戶」物件上的快速動作。

C. Quick Action on the Opportunity object
     

在「機會」物件上的快速動作。

D. Process Builder triggered from Account update
     

由帳戶更新觸發的 Process Builder。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
A quick action on the Account object can be used to create Opportunity records related to an Account. The quick action can pre-populate some fields based on the Account record, and also allow the user to input some fields. This would improve the process of creating Opportunity records.

應在「帳戶」物件上設定一個「快速動作 (Quick Action)」。這個快速動作的類型是「建立記錄 (Create a Record)」，目標物件是「機會」。在設定中，您可以：
預先填入欄位：使用公式從帳戶記錄中帶入值（例如，Account.Name）。
讓使用者輸入：將需要使用者填寫的欄位加入到快速動作的版面配置中。
這樣，使用者在帳戶頁面上點擊此動作時，就會彈出一個已預填部分資訊的表單，只需填寫剩餘欄位即可快速建立機會。

【第一百一十題 / NO. 110】


Cloud Kicks has three types of customer support processes: Platinum, Diamond, and Bronze. The app builder created separate record types for each process on the Case object. The customer support team should be unable to create new cases with the Bronze record type.
How should this requirement be met?


Cloud Kicks 有三種客戶支援流程：白金、鑽石和青銅。應用程式建構者在「個案」物件上為每個流程建立了獨立的記錄類型。客戶支援團隊應該無法建立「青銅」記錄類型的新個案。
應如何滿足此需求？


A. Update the organization-wide defaults to private for Case.
   ˆ

將個案的全組織預設值更新為「私人」。

B. Update the support team profile to remove the Bronze record type.
     

更新支援團隊的設定檔，移除「青銅」記錄類型。

C. Create permission set group for Case that includes Platinum and Diamond record types.
     

為個案建立一個權限集群組，其中包含白金和鑽石記錄類型。

D. Make the record type hidden to support users; update sharing roles to private.
     

將記錄類型對支援使用者隱藏；將共用角色更新為「私人」。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The solution that should meet this requirement is updating the support team profile to remove the Bronze record type. This way, the support team users will not be able to create new cases with the Bronze record type, as it will not appear in their record type selection list.

使用者在建立新記錄時能看到哪些記錄類型，是由他們的「設定檔 (Profile)」或「權限集 (Permission Set)」決定的。要阻止支援團隊建立「青銅」類型的個案，最直接的方法就是編輯他們所屬的設定檔，在該設定檔的「記錄類型設定 (Record Type Settings)」中，將「青銅」記錄類型從「可用的記錄類型 (Available Record Types)」列表中移除。

【第一百一十一題 / NO. 111】


An app builder has created a new report type but users are unable to select it from the Report Type list when making a new report for records they own.
What could be causing this issue?


一位應用程式建構者建立了一個新的報告類型，但使用者在為他們擁有的記錄建立新報告時，無法從「報告類型」清單中選取它。
可能的原因是什麼？


A. Access to the necessary object is unavailable.
     

對必要物件的存取權限不可用。

B. The report type is in a status of Deployed.
     

報告類型的狀態是「已部署」。

C. Access to Create and Customize Reports is disabled.
     

「建立和自訂報告」的存取權限被停用。

D. The report type is in a status of In Development.
     

報告類型的狀態是「開發中」。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
A report type that is in a status of In Development is not available for users to select when creating a new report. The app builder needs to change the status to Deployed to make it visible to users.

自訂報告類型有兩種狀態：「開發中 (In Development)」和「已部署 (Deployed)」。處於「開發中」狀態的報告類型只有管理員和建立者可以看到，普通使用者是無法在建立報告時看到的。必須將報告類型的狀態更改為「已部署」，它才會對所有有權限的使用者可見。

【第一百一十二題 / NO. 112】


Sales reps at Cloud Kicks (CK) forget to submit for approval when CK needs orders reviewed before close won. CK wants to automatically submit opportunities into the Secure Commitment Stage to eliminate manual submission.
Which three features would meet the business requirements? (Choose 3 answers)


Cloud Kicks (CK) 的銷售代表在訂單需要於「結案成交」前被審核時，常常忘記提交以供批准。CK 希望在機會進入「安全承諾階段」時自動提交，以消除手動提交。
哪三個功能可以滿足此業務需求？(選擇 3 個答案)


A. Workflow
     

工作流程

B. Process Builder

C. Apex

D. Chatter action
     

Chatter 動作

E. Flow


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C, E

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should use three features to meet the business requirements: Process Builder, Apex, and Flow. Process Builder can have a criteria that evaluates if an opportunity is in the Secure Commitment Stage, and then execute an action that submits it for approval. Apex can be used to create a trigger that runs before or after certain events...and submits it for approval. Flow can be used to create a record-triggered flow that runs after an opportunity is updated and submits it for approval.

有三種自動化工具可以實現「自動提交以供批准」的功能：
Flow：這是目前推薦的宣告式工具。可以建立一個記錄觸發的流程，在機會進入指定階段時，自動執行「提交以供批准」的動作。
Process Builder：這是舊版的宣告式工具，同樣可以設定條件並執行「提交以供批准」的動作。
Apex：可以使用 Apex 觸發器 (Trigger) 編寫程式碼，在記錄更新時檢查條件，並以程式碼方式提交記錄以供批准。
Workflow Rule (A) 不支援「提交以供批准」這個動作。

【第一百一十三題 / NO. 113】


An app builder needs a custom solution and is considering using community. Ease of updates is the primary consideration.
What should the app builder consider?


一位應用程式建構者需要一個自訂解決方案，並正在考慮使用社群。更新的便利性是主要考量。
建構者應該考慮什麼？
(註：題目的 "using community" 可能有誤，應為 "considering a third-party solution"，因為答案與社群無關。)


A. A managed package from AppExchange
     

來自 AppExchange 的受管理封裝

B. An unmanaged package from AppExchange
     

來自 AppExchange 的未管理封裝

C. An open-source unmanaged package
     

一個開源的未管理封裝

D. An open-source custom development
     

一個開源的自訂開發

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
A managed package from AppExchange is a custom solution that is developed by a third-party provider and can be installed in Salesforce. A managed package can be easily updated by the provider without affecting the existing functionality or customizations. This makes it suitable for the app builder's requirement of ease of updates.

如果「更新的便利性」是首要考量，那麼應該選擇「來自 AppExchange 的受管理封裝 (Managed Package)」。受管理封裝的開發者可以推送更新版本，而安裝者（使用者）可以像更新手機 App 一樣輕鬆地升級封裝，通常不會影響到自己在組織內所做的其他自訂設定。未管理封裝一旦安裝，就與開發者脫鉤，無法接收後續更新。

【第一百一十四題 / NO. 114】


Universal Containers wants to understand return on investment for the latest advertising buy. They currently use a private security model for all objects.
What should an app builder recommend?


Universal Containers 希望了解最近一次廣告採購的投資回報率 (ROI)。他們目前對所有物件都使用私人安全模型。
應用程式建構者應該推薦什麼？


A. Utilize Account Hierarchies and Roll-Up Summary fields
     

利用帳戶層級和總計欄位。

B. Run an opportunities pipeline report
     

執行一個機會流程報告。

C. Change to a public security model
     

改為公開安全模型。

D. Configure Campaign Hierarchies and Campaign statistics
     

設定行銷活動層級和行銷活動統計資料。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should recommend configuring Campaign Hierarchies and Campaign statistics to understand return on investment. Campaign Hierarchies allow users to organize campaigns into parent-child relationships. Campaign statistics allow users to track and measure key metrics for campaigns, such as budgeted cost, actual cost, expected revenue, number of leads, etc. By using these features, users can calculate return on investment.

為了追蹤廣告採購的 ROI，應該使用 Salesforce 的「行銷活動 (Campaign)」物件。透過「設定行銷活動層級和行銷活動統計資料」可以實現：
行銷活動層級 (Campaign Hierarchies)：可以將相關的行銷活動組織在一起，例如一個主廣告活動下有多個子活動，以便匯總整體成效。
行銷活動統計資料：行銷活動物件內建了「預算成本」、「實際成本」、「產生的機會金額」、「成交機會金額」等欄位，系統會自動計算這些值。透過比較成本和收入，就可以直接分析 ROI。

【第一百一十五題 / NO. 115】


The Director of Marketing at Northern Trail Outfitters wants the app builder to create a formula field that tracks how many days have elapsed since a contact was sent a marketing communication. The director is only interested in whole units.
Which function should be used to return a date for calculating the difference?


Northern Trail Outfitters 的行銷總監希望應用程式建構者建立一個公式欄位，用來追蹤自從向某個連絡人發送行銷通訊以來已經過了多少天。總監只對整數天數感興趣。
應該使用哪個函數來返回一個用於計算差異的日期？


A. DATETIMEVALUE()

B. TODAY()

C. DATEVALUE()

D. NOW()


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
TODAY() is the function that should be used to return a date for calculating the difference between today and the date a marketing communication was sent. TODAY() returns the current date as a Date value. NOW() returns the current Date/Time value. Since the director is only interested in whole units (days), using TODAY() is appropriate.

應該使用 TODAY() 函數。這個函數會返回目前的日期（不含時間）。NOW() 函數則會返回目前的日期和時間。由於題目要求計算經過的「天數」（整數單位），使用 TODAY() 進行日期相減 (TODAY() - Communication_Sent_Date__c) 會直接得到天數的差值，是最直接且正確的方法。

【第一百十六題 / NO. 116】


A custom field on an account is used to track finance information about a customer. Only members of the Finance Team have access to this field. However, the business wants to allow one customer service agent, who is assigned the customer service profile, read-only access to this field for special circumstances.
What is the recommended solution to grant the customer service agent access to the field?


帳戶上的一個自訂欄位被用來追蹤客戶的財務資訊。只有財務團隊的成員可以存取這個欄位。然而，業務部門希望允許一位被指派了「客戶服務」設定檔的客服專員，在特殊情況下對此欄位有唯讀存取權。
授予該客服專員欄位存取權的推薦解決方案是什麼？

A. Create a permission set that allows read-only access to the field via Field Level Security and assign it to the agent.
     

建立一個權限集，透過欄位級別安全性允許對該欄位的唯讀存取，並將其指派給該專員。

B. Create a new profile to allow for read-only access to the field via Field Level Security and assign it to the agent
     

建立一個新的設定檔，透過欄位級別安全性允許對該欄位的唯讀存取，並將其指派給該專員。

C. Update the Customer Service Profile already assigned to the agent to allow for read-only access to the field via Field Level Security
     

更新已指派給該專員的「客戶服務」設定檔，以允許對該欄位的唯讀存取。

D. Update the custom field's Field Level Security In setup to allow the agent read-only access to the field.
     

在設定中更新該自訂欄位的欄位級別安全性，以允許該專員唯讀存取。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The recommended solution is creating a permission set that allows read-only access to the field via Field Level Security and assigning it to the agent. A permission set is a collection of settings and permissions that give users access to various tools and functions. This allows granting specific permissions to individual users without changing their profile, which would affect all users with that profile.

推薦的解決方案是建立一個「權限集 (Permission Set)」。權限集是用來在不更改使用者基本設定檔 (Profile) 的情況下，授予特定使用者額外權限的最佳實踐。您可以建立一個權限集，在其中設定該財務欄位的欄位級別安全性 (FLS) 為「唯讀」，然後只將這個權限集指派給那一位特定的客服專員。這樣既滿足了需求，又不會影響其他擁有「客戶服務」設定檔的使用者。

【第一百十七題 / NO. 117】


Northern Trail Outfitters has two custom objects that are part of a master-detail relationship.
What determines the ownership and sharing access of the detail record?


Northern Trail Outfitters 有兩個自訂物件，它們是主從式關係的一部分。
什麼決定了明細記錄 (detail record) 的所有權和共用存取權？

A. The default owner is set in the parent object's settings.
     

預設負責人在父物件的設定中設定。

B. The Owner field on the Detail record.
     

明細記錄上的「負責人」欄位。

C. The Owner field on the Master record.
     

主記錄上的「負責人」欄位。

D. The owner is set independently on the detail object's settings.
     

負責人在明細物件的設定中獨立設定。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
The Owner field on the Master record determines the ownership and sharing access of the detail record in a master-detail relationship. According to the Salesforce documentation, "The detail record inherits the sharing and security settings of its master record." The detail record does not have its own Owner field.

在主從式關係中，明細記錄 (Detail) 本身沒有獨立的「負責人 (Owner)」欄位。它的所有權和共用存取權完全由其主記錄 (Master) 的「負責人」欄位決定。簡而言之，誰擁有主記錄，誰就擁有其下所有的明細記錄，並且明細記錄會繼承主記錄的共用設定。

【第一百十八題 / NO. 118】


Nickname__c is a custom text field on a contact record that is utilized to override the contact's name appearing on an email template. This field is not required and is not always filled in.
Which formula should an app builder use to select the contact's preferred name for email communications?


Nickname__c 是連絡人記錄上的一個自訂文字欄位，用於覆寫顯示在電子郵件範本上的連絡人姓名。這個欄位不是必填的，也不一定總是會被填寫。
應用程式建構者應該使用哪個公式來選擇用於電子郵件通訊的連絡人首選姓名？

A. IF (NOT(ISBLANK(Nickname__c)), Nickname__c,FirstName)

B. IF(TEXT(Nickname__c), Nickname__c,FirstName)

C. IF (ISNULL(Nickname__c), Nickname__c, FirstName)

D. IF(NOT(BLANKVALUE (Nickname__c)), Nickname__c, FirstName)


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D (註：選項 A 也是完全正確且常用的寫法。BLANKVALUE 是一個更簡潔的替代方案。此處依題庫答案。)

詳解 (Explanation):
The formula that should be used is IF (NOT (BLANKVALUE (Nickname__c)), Nickname_c, FirstName). This formula checks if the Nickname__c field is blank or null. The logic is flawed in the question's explanation, a better formula would be BLANKVALUE(Nickname__c, FirstName). This function checks if Nickname__c is blank; if it is, it returns FirstName; if not, it returns Nickname__c. Option A is also a perfectly valid and common way to write this logic.

這個問題的核心是檢查「暱稱」欄位是否為空。如果不是空的，就使用暱稱；如果是空的，就使用名字 (FirstName)。
選項 A IF(NOT(ISBLANK(Nickname__c)), Nickname__c, FirstName)：這個寫法完全正確。ISBLANK 檢查欄位是否為空，NOT 將其反轉，所以如果「不是空的」，則返回 Nickname__c，否則返回 FirstName。
選項 D：雖然題庫選擇了 D，但其寫法 IF(NOT(BLANKVALUE(...))) 是多餘的。BLANKVALUE(expression, substitute_expression) 函數本身的用途就是檢查 expression 是否為空，如果是，則返回 substitute_expression。因此，最簡潔的寫法是 BLANKVALUE(Nickname__c, FirstName)。
鑒於選項，選項 A 和 D 的邏輯目標相同，但 A 的寫法更標準。

【第一百十九題 / NO. 119】


A sales rep at AW Computing is unable to find what they are looking for while scrolling through their Chatter feed.
How can a filter be utilized to show only posts from their key account and opportunity records?


AW Computing 的一位銷售代表在滾動瀏覽他們的 Chatter 動態時，找不到他們想要的東西。
如何利用篩選器來只顯示來自他們關鍵帳戶和機會記錄的貼文？

A. Create a Chatter group.
     

建立一個 Chatter 群組。

B. Create Chatter bookmarks
     

建立 Chatter 書籤。

C. Create a Chatter stream.
     

建立一個 Chatter 摘要。

D. Create a Chatter notification.
     

建立一個 Chatter 通知。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
Create a Chatter stream. This is correct because a Chatter stream allows users to follow multiple records and people in one feed, and filter the feed by selecting a stream.

應建立一個「Chatter 摘要 (Chatter stream)」。Chatter 摘要允許使用者將多個他們感興趣的記錄（例如關鍵帳戶和機會）以及人物組合到一個自訂的動態中。這樣，使用者就可以只查看這個摘要，從而過濾掉所有不相關的 Chatter 更新，只專注於他們想看的內容。

【第一百二十題 / NO. 120】


Universal Containers (UC) maintains information for over 2 million assets in an external system. UC needs to access these assets in real-time data in Salesforce and is nearing the data storage limits.
What feature could an app builder recommend UC use?


Universal Containers (UC) 在一個外部系統中維護著超過 200 萬筆資產的資訊。UC 需要在 Salesforce 中即時存取這些資產資料，並且其資料儲存空間已接近上限。
應用程式建構者可以推薦 UC 使用什麼功能？

A. Data Loader

B. Salesforce Connect

C. Salesforce to Salesforce

D. Data Export Wizard
     

資料匯出精靈

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should recommend UC use Salesforce Connect to access the assets in real-time data in Salesforce. Salesforce Connect is a feature that allows users to view, search, and modify data that is stored outside Salesforce. Salesforce Connect uses external objects and external data sources to integrate data from various sources without copying or synchronizing it. This can help UC access their assets in real-time without consuming data storage limits in Salesforce.

應推薦使用「Salesforce Connect」。這個功能允許 Salesforce 透過「外部物件 (External Objects)」直接連接並顯示儲存在外部系統中的資料，而無需將這些資料實際匯入並儲存在 Salesforce 中。這完美地解決了兩個問題：1. 即時存取：資料是即時從外部系統讀取的。2. 不佔用儲存空間：因為資料沒有被複製進來，所以不會消耗 Salesforce 的資料儲存上限。

【第一百二十一題 / NO. 121】


A production org includes custom objects containing confidential Information. A sandbox is needed that includes data records, excludes all of the confidential objects, and can be refreshed weekly.
What steps should an App Builder take to meet these requirements?


一個生產環境包含帶有敏感資訊的自訂物件。現在需要一個沙箱，該沙箱需要包含部分資料記錄，但要排除所有敏感物件，並且可以每週重新整理一次。
應用程式建構者應採取什麼步驟來滿足這些需求？

A. Create a Full Sandbox and use a sandbox template
     

建立一個完整沙箱並使用沙箱範本。

B. Create a Developer Pro Sandbox and schedule Data loader to download selected object data weekly.
     

建立一個開發人員專業版沙箱，並排程 Data loader 每週下載選定的物件資料。

C. Create a Partial Copy Sandbox and use a sandbox template.
     

建立一個部分複製沙箱並使用沙箱範本。

D. Create a Developer Sandbox and schedule Data loader to download selected object data weekly.
     

建立一個開發人員沙箱，並排程 Data loader 每週下載選定的物件資料。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
The steps that the app builder should take are creating a Partial Copy Sandbox and using a sandbox template. A Partial Copy Sandbox can include data records, exclude confidential objects, and be refreshed weekly (refresh interval is 5 days). A sandbox template can specify which objects and data are copied from the production org to the sandbox org.

應建立一個「部分複製沙箱 (Partial Copy Sandbox)」並使用「沙箱範本 (sandbox template)」。
部分複製沙箱：這種沙箱類型可以包含生產環境的部分資料，且其重新整理間隔為 5 天，滿足「每週重新整理」的需求。
* 沙箱範本：在建立部分複製沙箱時，可以使用沙箱範本來精確地指定要複製哪些物件的資料到沙箱中。這樣就可以包含所需的物件，同時排除掉包含敏感資訊的物件。

【第一百二十二題 / NO. 122】


Sales manager at universal containers would like to standardize what information sales rep are gathering. Sales rep want recommendations, sales strategies and to know what key fields need to be completed at each step of the sales process on the opportunity record.
What feature should an app builder use to provide this functionally?


Universal Containers 的銷售經理希望標準化銷售代表收集的資訊。銷售代表希望在機會記錄的銷售流程每一步中，都能獲得建議、銷售策略，並知道需要完成哪些關鍵欄位。
應用程式建構者應使用哪個功能來提供此功能？

A. Workflow
     

工作流程

B. Path
     

路徑

C. Chatter feed
     

Chatter 動態

D. Global Action
     

全域動作

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should use the Path feature to provide the functionality that the sales manager wants. The Path feature allows an app builder to create a visual representation of the stages in a business process. The app builder can also add key fields, guidance, and resources for each stage to help sales reps gather information and complete tasks.

應使用「路徑 (Path)」功能。Path 提供了一個業務流程（如機會的銷售階段）的視覺化表示。在設定 Path 時，您可以為每個階段定義：
關鍵欄位 (Key Fields)：提醒使用者在此階段應填寫的重要欄位。
成功指引 (Guidance for Success)：提供文字說明、建議和銷售策略。
這完全符合題目的需求。

【第一百二十三題 / NO. 123】


An app builder installs an unmanaged package in a full copy sandbox that is an exact match for production, and now they are ready to install it in production. When the app builder attempts to install the package in production, it fails.
Why did the package fail to install?


一位應用程式建構者在一個與生產環境完全匹配的 Full Copy 沙箱中安裝了一個未管理封裝，現在他們準備將其安裝到生產環境中。當建構者嘗試在生產環境中安裝該封裝時，卻失敗了。
為什麼封裝安裝會失敗？

A. Incorrect license types
     

不正確的授權類型

B. Package features not compatible
     

封裝功能不相容

C. Object limits exceeded
     

超出物件限制

D. Apex unit test failures
     

Apex 單元測試失敗

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
Apex unit test failures can cause a package installation to fail. According to the Salesforce documentation, "If your package contains Apex code, all tests must complete successfully for your package to install." A Full Copy sandbox has a copy of production data, which may differ from the actual production data at the time of deployment, causing tests to fail in production that passed in the sandbox.

一個常見的部署失敗原因是「Apex 單元測試失敗」。當您將包含 Apex 程式碼的變更（包括未管理封裝）部署到生產環境時，Salesforce 會執行您組織中所有的 Apex 測試。所有測試都必須成功通過，且程式碼覆蓋率必須達到至少 75%，部署才能成功。即使在沙箱中測試通過，生產環境中不同的資料或設定也可能導致測試失敗。

【第一百二十四題 / NO. 124】


The VP of Sales at Universal Containers has asked the app builder to let sales reps create opportunity records directly from the account, with a number of fields pre-populated.
Which feature should the app builder use to allow users to create the opportunity?


Universal Containers 的銷售副總要求應用程式建構者讓銷售代表能夠直接從帳戶建立機會記錄，並預先填入一些欄位。
應用程式建構者應使用哪個功能來讓使用者建立機會？

A. A quick action
     

快速動作

B. A default action
     

預設動作

C. A custom button
     

自訂按鈕

D. A custom link
     

自訂連結

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The feature that the app builder should use is a quick action. A quick action...can create or update records...from a record page. The app builder can create a quick action on the account object that creates an opportunity record with pre-populated fields.

應使用「快速動作 (Quick Action)」。可以在「帳戶」物件上建立一個「建立記錄」類型的物件特定快速動作，目標物件設為「機會」。在設定這個快速動作時，可以定義「預設值」，例如將機會的 AccountId 設定為目前帳戶的 ID，或將帳戶的其他欄位值帶入到機會的新欄位中。

【第一百二十五題 / NO. 125】


DreamHouse Realty wants to track how many lifts are being installed into customer garages. The To Be Installed custom checkbox field on the custom Lift object should be checked and an external system should be notified via an outbound message the next day when a lift is sold.
What automation tool should be used to complete this task?


DreamHouse Realty 想要追蹤有多少電梯被安裝到客戶的車庫中。當一個電梯售出時，自訂的 Lift 物件上的「待安裝」自訂核取方塊欄位應該被勾選，並且應在第二天透過一個傳出訊息通知一個外部系統。
應該使用哪種自動化工具來完成此任務？
(註：此題答案在舊版中適用，現在應使用 Flow)

A. Approval process
     

批准流程

B. Workflow
     

工作流程

C. Flow

D. Process Builder


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D (根據題庫)

詳解 (Explanation):
Process Builder is the best automation tool to complete this task. Process Builder can perform actions when a record is created or updated, and it can also schedule actions to execute at a later time. Process Builder can update a field and call an outbound message as actions.

Process Builder 是完成此任務的最佳工具，因為它能同時滿足兩個需求：
立即動作：當電梯售出時（滿足觸發條件），立即更新「待安裝」核取方塊欄位。
排程動作 (Scheduled Action)：在同一個流程中，設定一個排程動作，在觸發時間的「1 天後」執行「傳出訊息 (Outbound Message)」動作。
工作流程 (Workflow) 也可以做到，但 Process Builder 更為強大且是當時的趨勢。現在，Flow 是完成此類任務的標準工具。

【第一百二十六題 / NO. 126】


When an opportunity close date is delayed by more than 60 days, the manager and the VP of sales must approve the change.
How can this requirement be met? (Choose 2 answers)


當一個機會的結束日期被延遲超過 60 天時，經理和銷售副總必須批准此變更。
如何滿足此需求？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Build an approval process that requires unanimous approval from the manager and VP of sales.
     

建立一個需要經理和銷售副總一致批准的批准流程。

B. Create a workflow rule that checks for close date less than 60 days and add an email alert.
     

建立一個檢查結束日期小於 60 天的工作流程規則，並新增一個電子郵件警示。

C. Create a lightning process builder flow that submits the record for an approval process.
     

建立一個提交記錄以供批准流程的 Lightning Process Builder 流程。

D. Build a validation rule that does not allow a user to save the opportunity record.
     

建立一個不允許使用者儲存機會記錄的驗證規則。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C (註：現在建議使用 Flow 取代 Process Builder)

詳解 (Explanation):
The requirement can be met by using a combination of process builder and approval process. The process builder can be used to trigger the approval process when the close date is delayed by more than 60 days. The approval process can be configured to require unanimous approval from the manager and VP of sales.

這個需求需要兩部分結合：
自動觸發：使用一個自動化工具（如 Process Builder 或 Flow）來監控「結束日期」的變更。當變更超過 60 天時，自動觸發「提交以供批准」的動作。這符合選項 C 的描述。
多級批准：建立一個「批准流程 (Approval Process)」，設定多個批准步驟。第一步給經理，第二步給銷售副總，並設定為需要所有批准人同意（一致批准）。這符合選項 A 的描述。

【第一百二十七題 / NO. 127】


UVC's CFO has asked that all deals with more than a 40% discount get automatically sent to the VP of Finance. He will review these deals without the sales rep needing to take action.
Which two ways can this be accomplished without building code? (Choose 2 answers)


UVC 的財務長要求所有折扣超過 40% 的交易都自動發送給財務副總。他將審核這些交易，而無需銷售代表採取任何行動。
哪兩種無需編寫程式碼的方式可以實現這一點？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Launch a new approval process that has automatic submission enabled as an initial submission action
     

啟動一個新的批准流程，該流程已將自動提交設定為初始提交動作。

B. Create a new process with a submit for approval action to automatically submit deals for approval
     

建立一個帶有「提交以供批准」動作的新流程，以自動提交交易以供批准。

C. Create a new approval process that has automatic submission enabled in the entry criteria
     

建立一個新的批准流程，該流程在進入條件中已啟用自動提交。

D. Launch a flow that uses the submit for approval action to submit deals for approval
     

啟動一個使用「提交以供批准」動作來提交交易以供批准的 Flow。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C (註：此題答案在概念上重複且描述不精確。更常見的實現方式是B和D。但此處依題庫答案。)

詳解 (Explanation):
Launch a new approval process that has automatic submission enabled as an initial submission action, and Create a new approval process that has automatic submission enabled in the entry criteria. These are correct because both options allow the deals to be automatically submitted for approval without requiring any action from the sales rep.

根據題庫的答案，這兩種方式都旨在讓批准流程自動啟動，無需使用者手動點擊「提交以供批准」。
選項 C：在批准流程的「進入條件 (Entry Criteria)」中設定條件（例如 Discount > 0.40），當記錄被建立或編輯並滿足此條件時，批准流程會自動啟動。
選項 A：這描述了批准流程內部的一個動作，但自動提交的觸發點通常是在進入條件或由外部自動化工具（如 Flow）觸發。
在實務中，最常見的無程式碼作法是 B (使用 Process Builder) 或 D (使用 Flow)，在滿足條件時呼叫「提交以供批准」動作。

【第一百二十八題 / NO. 128】


An app builder wants to add the option to 'Send New Email' from Leads, Contacts and Accounts for users on mobile.
What is the benefit of using global actions to accomplish this?


一位應用程式建構者希望為行動裝置上的使用者在潛在客戶、連絡人和帳戶上新增「傳送新電子郵件」的選項。
使用全域動作來完成此任務有什麼好處？

A. Global actions can be accessed anywhere actions are pages, feed and Chatter groups.
     

全域動作可以在任何支援動作的地方存取，例如頁面、動態和 Chatter 群組。

B. Salesforce Lightning Component Library houses existing global actions prebuilt for use.
     

Salesforce Lightning 元件庫中存放了預先建置好的現有全域動作以供使用。

C. The global action's layout automatically clones the default page layout.
     

全域動作的版面配置會自動複製預設的頁面版面配置。

D. Global actions are record-specific and are available when searching that particular record.
     

全域動作是特定於記錄的，並且在搜尋該特定記錄時可用。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
Global actions can be accessed anywhere actions are pages, feed and Chatter groups. This is correct because global actions are not tied to a specific object, and they can be added to any page that supports actions, such as record pages, home pages, feed pages, and Chatter groups.

全域動作 (Global Actions) 的最大好處是它們不與任何特定物件綁定。這意味著您可以將它們新增到全域發佈器版面配置中，然後在行動應用程式的導覽列、Chatter 動態以及其他多個地方存取它們，讓使用者無論在哪個頁面都能快速執行該動作。

Which tool should be used?


Cloud Kicks (CK) 想要快速插入一個超過 60,000 筆全新帳戶的清單。該清單是根據 CK 資料模型的範本填寫的。

A. Data Loader

B. A Lightning Object Creator
     

Lightning 物件建立器

C. Import Wizard
     

匯入精靈

D. Schema Builder
     

結構描述產生器

The app builder should use Data Loader to quickly insert a list of over 60,000 net new Accounts. Data Loader can handle up to 5 million records at a time. Import Wizard is not a valid tool, as it cannot handle more than 50,000 records at a time.

應使用 Data Loader。因為「匯入精靈 (Import Wizard)」一次最多只能處理 50,000 筆記錄，而題目中的資料量超過了 60,000 筆。Data Loader 是一個功能更強大的用戶端工具，可以處理高達 500 萬筆記錄的插入、更新、刪除和匯出操作，是處理大量資料的首選。

【第一百三十題 / NO. 130】


An app builder at Northern Trad Outfitters created a sandbox template for Accounts, Projects, and Project Milestones to reconfigure some flows for the project management app.
Which type of testing environment should the app builder create?


Northern Trail Outfitters 的一位應用程式建構者為「帳戶」、「專案」和「專案里程碑」物件建立了一個沙箱範本，以便為專案管理應用程式重新設定一些流程。
建構者應該建立哪種類型的測試環境？

A. Developer
     

開發人員

B. Partial Copy
     

部分複製

C. Developer Pro
     

開發人員專業版

D. Scratch Org
     

臨時組織

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
Partial Copy is the type of testing environment that the app builder should create to use a sandbox template. According to the Salesforce documentation, "Partial Copy sandboxes copy your production org's configuration (metadata) and some of your production org's data as defined by a sandbox template." Other sandbox types like Developer or Developer Pro do not use sandbox templates for data selection.

應建立「部分複製 (Partial Copy)」沙箱。因為只有「部分複製」和「完整 (Full)」沙箱才能使用「沙箱範本 (Sandbox Template)」來選擇性地複製生產環境中的資料。Developer 和 Developer Pro 沙箱只會複製設定資料 (metadata)，不會複製任何業務資料，因此也用不到沙箱範本。

【第一百三十一題 / NO. 131】


A Service Coordinator (SC) for Ursa Major Solar (UMS) does a final review of work orders owned by a technician for a specific region before the records are submitted for an invoice. Before closing out the work order, the SC needs to modify data or remove attachments that were added by mistake. The SC also needs access to any other related records owned by the technician.
What solution would provide the required access, given a private data model?


Ursa Major Solar (UMS) 的一位服務協調員 (SC) 會在記錄提交開立發票前，對特定區域技術人員擁有的工單進行最終審核。在結案工單之前，SC 需要修改資料或移除錯誤新增的附件。SC 也需要存取該技術人員擁有的任何其他相關記錄。
在私人資料模型下，什麼解決方案可以提供所需的存取權限？

A. Give the SC a permission set with the Modify All Data system permission.
     

給予 SC 一個帶有「修改所有資料」系統權限的權限集。

B. Put the SC in the role hierarchy above the technicians whose work orders they review.
     

將 SC 放在他們所審核的技術人員之上的角色層級結構中。

C. Create a workflow rule that updates records owned by technicians in that regionwith the S

C.
     

建立一個工作流程規則，將該區域技術人員擁有的記錄更新給 SC。

D. Change work order access on the SC's profile to 'Modify All'.
     

在 SC 的設定檔上將工單存取權限更改為「修改全部」。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
Putting the SC in the role hierarchy above the technicians whose work orders they review will provide the required access, given a private data model. The role hierarchy determines how users can access records they do not own. Users at any given role level can view, edit, and report on all data owned by or shared with users below them in the role hierarchy.

最好的解決方案是將服務協調員 (SC) 的角色設定在技術人員的角色之上。在 Salesforce 的角色層級結構中，處於較高層級角色的使用者預設可以存取其下屬角色使用者擁有的所有記錄（檢視、編輯、報告等）。這是在私人共用模型下，提供垂直存取權限的標準方法。給予「修改所有資料」權限過於寬泛且危險。

【第一百三十二題 / NO. 132】


Universal Containers (UC) tracks Account locations in Zip_Code__c, a custom text field with a validation rule to enforce proper formatting of the US ZIP+4 code for UC's orders.
What formula should the app builder create on Order to display only the first five digits of Zip_Code__c from the parent Account?


Universal Containers (UC) 在一個名為 Zip_Code__c 的自訂文字欄位中追蹤帳戶地點，該欄位有一條驗證規則來強制執行 UC 訂單的美國 ZIP+4 郵遞區號格式。
應用程式建構者應在「訂單 (Order)」上建立什麼公式，以僅顯示來自父帳戶的 Zip_Code__c 的前五位數字？

A. BEGINS (Account.Zip_Code__r, 5)

B. TEXT(Account.Zip_Code__c, 5)

C. LEFT(Account.Zip_Code__c, 5)

D. LPAD(Account.Zip_Code__r, 5)


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
LEFT(Account.Zip_Code__c, 5) is the correct formula to display only the first five digits of Zip_Code__c from the parent Account. LEFT function returns the specified number of characters from the left side of a text string. Account.Zip_Code__c is the custom text field that stores the Zip Code on Account object. 5 is the number of characters to return from the left side of the Zip Code.

正確的公式是 LEFT(Account.Zip_Code__c, 5)。 LEFT() 函數的作用是從一個文字字串的左側開始，傳回指定數量的字元。在這個公式中，Account.Zip_Code__c 是從相關的帳戶物件中取得郵遞區號的文字值，5 則是指定要傳回的字元數量。

【第一百三十三題 / NO. 133】

How should an app builder automate travel requests based on these criteria?

應用程式建構者應如何根據這些標準自動化差旅申請？

A. Process Builder

B. Workflow rule
     

工作流程規則

C. Approval process
     

批准流程

D. Apex


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
Approval process is the best way to automate travel requests based on internal policy. Approval process can define the steps, criteria, and actions for approving records. The app builder can create an approval process for travel requests that requires approval from managers or executives before they are submitted.

根據內部政策自動化提交和審核申請，最好的方法是使用「批准流程 (Approval Process)」。批准流程可以定義批准記錄所需的步驟、進入條件、批准人和批准/拒絕後的動作。建構者可以為差旅申請建立一個批准流程，要求在提交後必須由經理或高階主管批准。

【第一百三十四題 / NO. 134】


A recently refreshed partial sandbox at Cloud Kicks has no data In the custom object Shipping__c. Checking in production, there are two million rows of data in the object.
What could be the reason the data is missing?


Cloud Kicks 最近重新整理的一個 Partial Sandbox 中，自訂物件 Shipping__c 裡沒有任何資料。經檢查，生產環境中該物件有兩百萬行資料。
資料遺失的原因可能 copious 是什麼？

A. The sandbox was refreshed too early.
     

沙箱重新整理得太早了。

B. The selected objects in the sandbox template.
     

沙箱範本中選擇的物件。

C. The Partial sandbox is at capacity.
     

Partial Sandbox 的容量已滿。

D. The sandbox is still populating data.
     

沙箱仍在填入資料中。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The selected objects in the sandbox template. This is correct because a partial sandbox only copies a subset of data from production, and the data to be copied is determined by the sandbox template. If the Shipping__c object was not selected in the template, then its data would not be copied to the sandbox.

正確的原因是「沙箱範本中選擇的物件」。Partial Sandbox 只會複製生產環境中由「沙箱範本 (Sandbox Template)」所定義的物件子集資料。如果 Shipping__c 物件沒有被包含在用於這次重新整理的沙箱範本中，那麼該物件的任何資料都不會被複製到沙箱裡。

【第一百三十五題 / NO. 135】


At Universal containers, all US Sales reps should be able to view the US Team dashboard, however, only the US sales directors should be able to see the data in the component and view its source report.
How can an app builder ensure the proper access is granted?


在 Universal Containers，所有美國銷售代表都應該能看到「美國團隊」儀表板，然而，只有美國銷售總監才能看到元件中的資料並檢視其來源報告。
應用程式建構者應如何確保授予適當的存取權限？

A. Make the US Sales Director the running user and share the dashboard folder with the role US Sales Rep
     

將美國銷售總監設為執行使用者，並將儀表板資料夾與「美國銷售代表」角色共用。

B. Make the dashboard dynamic and give US Sales Reps the view my team's dashboard permission
     

將儀表板設為動態，並給予美國銷售代表「檢視我團隊的儀表板」權限。

C. Share the dashboard folder with roles and subordinates of the US Sales Director and share the report folder with the role of US Sales Director
    ˆ

將儀表板資料夾與「美國銷售總監」的角色和部屬共用，並將報告資料夾與「美國銷售總監」的角色共用。

D. Share the dashboard with the public group US Sales Reps and share the dashboard's source reports folder with the US Sales Director profile
     

將儀表板與「美國銷售代表」公開群組共用，並將儀表板的來源報告資料夾與「美國銷售總監」設定檔共用。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
Sharing the dashboard folder with roles and subordinates of the US Sales Director and sharing the report folder with the role of US Sales Director will ensure that only the US sales directors can see the data in the component and view its source report, while all US sales reps can view the US Team dashboard. The access to a dashboard is controlled by the dashboard folder sharing, while the access to the underlying data and source reports is controlled by the report folder sharing and the user's data access rights.

這個需求需要分開控制儀表板和報告的存取權限。正確的作法是：
儀表板權限：將儲存儀表板的資料夾分享給「美國銷售總監」的角色和其部屬 (Roles and Subordinates)。這樣所有銷售代表（作為總監的部屬）都能看到儀表板本身。
報告權限：將儲存儀表板來源報告的資料夾只分享給「美國銷售總監」的角色。這樣一來，只有總監才能存取報告，從而看到儀表板元件中的詳細資料和點擊進入來源報告。
銷售代表雖然能看到儀表板，但因為沒有報告的權限，他們看到的元件會顯示權限不足的錯誤訊息。

【第一百三十六題 / NO. 136】


Ursa Major Solar (UMS) uses a public sharing model for accounts. UMS would like to move to a more restrictive sharing model but wants the Sales team to continue to have access to all account records with the sales record type.
Which two actions should an app builder complete to implement this change? (Choose 2 answers)


Ursa Major Solar (UMS) 目前對帳戶使用公開共用模型。UMS 希望轉向更嚴格的共用模型，但希望銷售團隊能繼續存取所有具有「銷售」記錄類型的帳戶記錄。
應用程式建構者應完成哪兩個動作來實施此變更？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Update the Sales profile.
     

更新銷售設定檔。

B. Update the organization-wide defaults
     

更新全組織預設值。

C. Create a criteria-based sharing rule.
     

建立一個基於條件的共用規則。

D. Create an owner-based sharing rule.
     

建立一個基於負責人的共用規則。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C

詳解 (Explanation):
Update the organization-wide defaults and create a criteria based sharing rule are two actions that an app builder should complete. First, update the OWD for Accounts to a more restrictive setting like 'Private' or 'Public Read Only'. Then, create a criteria-based sharing rule where the criteria is 'Account Record Type equals Sales', and share it with the roles, territories, or public group representing the Sales team.

為了實施此變更，需要兩個步驟：
1. 更新全組織預設值 (Update OWD)：首先，將帳戶物件的 OWD 從公開模型（如 Public Read/Write）更改為更嚴格的模型（如 Private）。這是收緊權限的基礎。
2. 建立基於條件的共用規則 (Create a criteria-based sharing rule)：OWD 收緊後，為了重新開放權限，需要建立一條共用規則。該規則的條件設定為「帳戶記錄類型等於銷售」，然後將這些記錄分享給代表銷售團隊的公開群組或角色。

【第一百三十七題 / NO. 137】


Universal Containers uses a private sharing model for opportunities. This model CANNOT be changed due to a regional structure A new sales operations team has been created. This team needs to perform analysis on Opportunity data, and should have read and write access to all Opportunities.
What are two recommended solutions for the app builder to give the users appropriate access? (Choose 2 answers)


Universal Containers 對機會使用私人共用模型。由於區域結構的原因，此模型無法更改。現在成立了一個新的銷售運營團隊。該團隊需要對機會資料進行分析，並且應該對所有機會擁有讀寫存取權限。
應用程式建構者有哪些推薦的解決方案來給予使用者適當的存取權限？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Create a criteria-based sharing rule to share all opportunities with the sales operations public group.
     

建立一個基於條件的共用規則，將所有機會與銷售運營公開群組共用。

B. Add a manual share for all opportunities with each user on the sales operations team.
     

為銷售運營團隊的每個使用者手動共用所有機會。

C. Add a permission set with 'View All' and 'Modify All' opportunity permissions enabled.
     

新增一個啟用了「檢視全部」和「修改全部」機會權限的權限集。

D. Create a criteria-based sharing rule to share all opportunities with the sales operations private group
     

建立一個基於條件的共用規則，將所有機會與銷售運營私人群組共用。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C

詳解 (Explanation):
The two recommended solutions are creating a criteria-based sharing rule...with the sales operations public group and adding a permission set with 'View All' and 'Modify All' opportunity permissions enabled. A criteria-based sharing rule can grant access to all opportunities that meet certain criteria (e.g., 'Created Date not equal to null' to capture all records). A permission set with 'View All' and 'Modify All' overrides all sharing settings for that object and grants complete access.

有兩種推薦的方法可以授予團隊對所有機會的存取權：
1. 使用共用規則：建立一個銷售運營團隊的「公開群組 (Public Group)」。然後，建立一條「基於條件的共用規則」，條件可以設定為一個永遠為真的條件（例如「建立日期不等於空值」），將所有機會的讀寫權限分享給這個公開群組。
2. 使用權限集：建立一個新的「權限集 (Permission Set)」，在該權限集中，為「機會」物件啟用「檢視全部 (View All)」和「修改全部 (Modify All)」的權限。然後將這個權限集指派給銷售運營團隊的每一位成員。這會無視 OWD 和共用規則，直接授予他們對所有機會的完全存取權。

【第一百三十八題 / NO. 138】


Cloud Kicks (CK) wants to begin socializing and collaborating within Salesforce around customer accounts to discuss various topics. CK would like all company employees to see these conversations.
Which two features of Chatter would meet CK's business needs? (Choose 2 answers)


Cloud Kicks (CK) 希望開始在 Salesforce 內部圍繞客戶帳戶進行社交和協作，以討論各種主題。CK 希望所有公司員工都能看到這些對話。
Chatter 的哪兩個功能可以滿足 CK 的業務需求？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Set up new private Chatter groups.
     

設定新的私人 Chatter 群組。

B. Set up new public Chatter groups.
     

設定新的公開 Chatter 群組。

C. Use post action on the Account object.
     

在帳戶物件上使用貼文動作。

D. Use Chatter actions to create tasks to complete.
     

使用 Chatter 動作來建立要完成的工作。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C

詳解 (Explanation):
The two features of Chatter that would meet CK's business needs are: Set up new public Chatter groups. A public Chatter group is a way to create a collaborative space for users to share information... and can be joined by any user. Use post action on the Account object. A post action is a type of quick action that allows users to create a post on a record's feed.

為了讓所有員工都能看到圍繞帳戶的對話，可以使用以下兩種 Chatter 功能：
1. 設定公開 Chatter 群組 (Public Chatter Groups)：可以為特定主題（例如「關鍵客戶策略」）建立公開群組。公開群組的內容對組織內所有使用者可見，任何人都可以加入。
2. 在帳戶物件上使用貼文 (Use post action on the Account object)：直接在特定帳戶記錄的 Chatter 動態上發布貼文。只要使用者有權限查看該帳戶記錄，他們就能看到與該帳戶相關的對話。

【第一百三十九題 / NO. 139】


Cloud Kicks works on an annual subscription model. When a sales rep marks an opportunity as closed won, a new opportunity should automatically be created for the renewal. The contracts team works outside of salesforce but also needs to be notified about closed deals in order to initiate the contract process with the customer.
Which automation solution would meet these requirements?


Cloud Kicks 採用年度訂閱模式。當銷售代表將一個機會標記為「結案成交 (closed won)」時，應自動為續約建立一個新的機會。合約團隊在 Salesforce 外部工作，但也需要收到關於已成交交易的通知，以便與客戶啟動合約流程。
哪種自動化解決方案可以滿足這些需求？

A. Approval Process
     

批准流程

B. Outbound Message
     

傳出訊息

C. Validation Rule
     

驗證規則

D. Record-triggered flow
     

記錄觸發的流程

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
A record-triggered flow can be used to automate actions when a record is created or updated. In this case, a record-triggered flow can be configured to create a new opportunity and send an email to the contracts team when an opportunity is marked as closed won.

應使用「記錄觸發的流程 (Record-triggered flow)」。Flow 是目前 Salesforce 中最強大的宣告式自動化工具，可以同時滿足這兩個需求：
建立記錄 (Create Records)：當機會的階段更新為「結案成交」時，Flow 可以自動建立一個新的續約機會記錄。
傳送電子郵件 (Send Email)：在同一個流程中，可以加入一個「傳送電子郵件警示」的動作，通知合約團隊。
其他工具無法同時完成這兩項任務（例如，Workflow 無法建立記錄）。

【第一百四十題 / NO. 140】


Cloud Kicks (CK) captures all shipping information in a custom object called Shipments__c. CK's app builder is tasked with creating an approval process to ensure department members can approve all overnight shipments.
Where should the app builder route the approval request?


Cloud Kicks (CK) 在一個名為 Shipments__c 的自訂物件中擷取所有貨運資訊。CK 的應用程式建構者被指派建立一個批准流程，以確保部門成員可以批准所有隔夜運送的貨件。
建構者應將批准請求路由到哪裡？

A. Hierarchy field
     

層級欄位

B. Role
     

角色

C. Public group
     

公開群組

D. Queue
     

佇列

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C (註：Queue 也可以接收批准請求，但 Public Group 更靈活。此處依題庫答案。)

詳解 (Explanation):
Public group is the best option to route the approval request for overnight shipments. Public groups can include users, roles, or other groups. Queues are used to assign ownership of records to a group of users, not for approval processes.

最好的選項是將批准請求路由到「公開群組 (Public Group)」。公開群組非常靈活，它可以包含特定的使用者、特定角色的使用者，甚至是其他群組的成員。您可以建立一個包含所有需要批准隔夜運送的部門成員的公開群組，然後在批准流程步驟中將此群組設定為批准人。這樣，群組中的任何一個成員都可以處理批准請求。 雖然佇列 (Queue) 也可以被指派為批准人，但公開群組在成員組合上更具彈性。

【第一百四十一題 / NO. 141】


Universal Containers wants to streamline its data capture process by linking fields together. They wish to do this so that the available value on dependent fields are driven by the value selected on controlling fields.
Which consideration supports the stated requirements? (Choose 3 answers)


Universal Containers 公司希望透過將欄位連結在一起來簡化其資料擷取流程。他們希望這樣做，以便相依欄位的可用值由控制欄位中選擇的值來決定。
哪個考量因素支援所述的需求？(選擇 3 個答案)
(註：此題的答案選項與 Salesforce 的實際功能有些出入，我們依據題庫答案解釋。)

A. The import wizard only allows a value to be imported into a dependent picklist if it matches the appropriate controlling field.
     

匯入精靈只允許在相依選項清單的值與其對應的控制欄位相符時，才將其匯入。

B. Custom picklist fields can be either controlling or dependent fields.
     

自訂選項清單欄位可以是控制欄位，也可以是相依欄位。

C. Multi-select picklist can be dependent picklists but not controlling fields.
     

多選選項清單可以是相依選項清單，但不能是控制欄位。

D. Standard and custom picklist fields can be dependent fields.
     

標準和自訂選項清單欄位都可以是相依欄位。

E. Checkbox fields can be controlling fields but not dependent fields.
     

核取方塊欄位可以是控制欄位，但不能是相依欄位。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, B, E

詳解 (Explanation):

B. Custom picklist fields can be either controlling or dependent fields.

E. Checkbox fields can be controlling fields but not dependent fields. A . The import wizard only allows value to be imported into a dependent picklist if they match the appropriate controlling field. This ensures data integrity. (Note: Option C is also correct according to Salesforce documentation, but the provided answer key selects A, B, E).

關於相依選項清單的考量因素：

A. 匯入精靈的限制：為了確保資料的完整性，當您使用匯入精靈匯入資料時，相依選項清單的值必須與其控制欄位的值是有效的組合，否則會匯入失敗。

B. 自訂選項清單的彈性：自訂的選項清單欄位既可以作為控制欄位，也可以作為相依欄位。

E. 核取方塊的角色：標準或自訂的核取方塊欄位可以作為控制欄位（其值為 true 或 false），但它們不能作為相依欄位。
(註：根據 Salesforce 官方文件，選項 C「多選選項清單可以是相依的，但不能是控制的」也是正確的。)


【第一百四十二題 / NO. 142】


An app builder is creating a custom object called Testimonial__c and wants to connect Testimonial__c records with both the submitter's Contact record and Account record. If the Account is deleted, the Testimonial__c should also be deleted. If the Contact is deleted, but the Account remains, the Testimonial__c should remain.
How should this be accomplished?


一位應用程式建構者正在建立一個名為 Testimonial__c 的自訂物件，並希望將 Testimonial__c 記錄與提交者的「連絡人」記錄和「帳戶」記錄兩者都連接起來。如果「帳戶」被刪除，Testimonial__c 也應該被刪除。如果「連絡人」被刪除，但「帳戶」仍然存在，則 Testimonial__c 應該保留下來。
應如何實現此目標？

A. Make both the Contact and Account fields required on the Testimonial__c object and create lookup relationships from Testimonial__c to Contact and to Account.
     

在 Testimonial__c 物件上將「連絡人」和「帳戶」欄位都設為必填，並從 Testimonial__c 建立到「連絡人」和「帳戶」的查詢關係。

B. Create a master-detail relationship from Testimonial__c to Account and a lookup relationship from Testimonial__c to Contact.
     

從 Testimonial__c 到「帳戶」建立一個主從式關係，並從 Testimonial__c 到「連絡人」建立一個查詢關係。

C. Make Testimonial__c a junction object between Account and Contact using master-detail relationships.
     

使用主從式關係將 Testimonial__c 設為「帳戶」和「連絡人」之間的連接物件。

D. Create a lookup relationship from Testimonial__c to Account and a master-detail relationship from Testimonial__c to Contact.
     

從 Testimonial__c 到「帳戶」建立一個查詢關係，並從 Testimonial__c 到「連絡人」建立一個主從式關係。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
To connect Testimonial__c records with both the submitter's Contact record and Account record, an app builder should create a master-detail relationship from Testimonial__c to Account and a lookup relationship from Testimonial__c to Contact. A master-detail relationship creates a parent-child relationship... and cascading actions [like delete]. A lookup relationship creates a loose association...

根據需求，Testimonial__c 的生命週期與「帳戶」緊密綁定（帳戶刪除，它也要刪除），但與「連絡人」是鬆散綁定（連絡人刪除，它不刪除）。
* 主從式關係 (Master-Detail)：這種關係具有「級聯刪除 (cascade delete)」的特性，即刪除主記錄時，會自動刪除所有相關的明細記錄。因此，應在 Testimonial__c (Detail) 和 Account (Master) 之間建立主從式關係。
* 查詢關係 (Lookup)：這種關係是鬆散的，刪除被查詢的記錄不會影響查詢方。因此，應在 Testimonial__c 和 Contact 之間建立查詢關係。

【第一百四十三題 / NO. 143】


SERVICE AGENTS ARE REQUIRED TO CONFIRM A USER'S IDENTITY BEFORE PROVIDING SUPPORT INFORMATION OVER THE PHON

E.
WHAT FEATURE CAN AN APP BUILDER USE TO HELP AGENTS MEET THIS REQUIREMENT?


服務專員在透過電話提供支援資訊之前，必須先確認使用者身份。
應用程式建構者可以使用什麼功能來幫助專員滿足此要求？

A. Include Surveys as a Case related list
     

將「調查」作為個案相關清單包含進來。

B. Case Validation Rules
     

個案驗證規則。

C. Add Path to the top of the Case layout
     

將「路徑」新增到個案版面配置的頂部。

D. Guided Action Flows on the record page
     

記錄頁面上的引導式動作流程。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
Guided Action Flows on the record page can help service agents meet the requirement of confirming a user identity. Guided Action Flows are a series of screens that guide agents through a predefined process, such as verifying user information, collecting case details, or resolving issues.

應使用「引導式動作流程 (Guided Action Flows)」，也就是「畫面流程 (Screen Flow)」。您可以建立一個畫面流程，包含一系列畫面來引導服務專員完成身份驗證的步驟（例如，詢問安全問題、核對資料等）。將這個流程作為一個動作放在記錄頁面上，專員只需點擊即可啟動標準化的驗證程序。

【第一百四十四題 / NO. 144】


Ursa Major Solar wants to create a relationship between the standard Contact object and a custom Solar Project object. Contacts can potentially be related to multiple Solar Project objects, and a Solar Project can have multiple Contacts associated with it.
How should an app builder configure the data model?


Ursa Major Solar 希望在標準的「連絡人 (Contact)」物件和自訂的「太陽能專案 (Solar Project)」物件之間建立關係。「連絡人」可能與多個「太陽能專案」物件相關，而一個「太陽能專案」也可以與多個「連絡人」相關聯。
應用程式建構者應如何設定資料模型？

A. One Master-detail relationship on Contact and one Master-detail relationship on Solar Project
     

在「連絡人」上建立一個主從式關係，在「太陽能專案」上建立一個主從式關係。

B. Two Lookup relationships on a new custom object
     

在一個新的自訂物件上建立兩個查詢關係。

C. One Lookup relationship on Contact and one Lookup relationship on Solar Project
     

在「連絡人」上建立一個查詢關係，在「太陽能專案」上建立一個查詢關係。

D. Two Master-detail relationships on a new custom object
     

在一個新的自訂物件上建立兩個主從式關係。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D (註：此答案有誤。標準物件不能作為主從式關係中的 Detail 端。正確答案應為 B。此處依題庫答案。)

詳解 (Explanation):
Two Master-detail relationships on a new custom object is how an app builder should configure the data model to create a relationship between Contact and Solar Project objects where each Contact can be related to multiple Solar Project objects, and each Solar Project can have multiple Contacts associated with it. This is an example of a many-to-many relationship that requires a junction object with two master-detail relationships.

題目的描述是典型的「多對多 (many-to-many)」關係。在 Salesforce 中，實現多對多關係的標準方法是建立一個「連接物件 (Junction Object)」。這個新的自訂物件會與另外兩個物件（此例中為 Contact 和 Solar Project）建立關係。
* 題庫答案解釋 (D)：認為應在連接物件上建立兩個主從式關係。
正確的 Salesforce 實踐 (B)：由於標準物件 (Contact) 不能位於主從式關係的「明細 (Detail)」端，因此不能直接建立主從式關係。正確的做法應該是在新的連接物件上建立兩個查詢關係 (Lookup relationships)，一個指向 Contact，另一個指向 Solar Project。

【第一百四十五題 / NO. 145】


Universal Containers allows all employees to submit reviews for leadership using a custom object called Review. These Reviews should only be visible to the HR department and the employee who submitted the record.
Which three steps should an app builder take to properly control access to Reviews? (Choose 3 answers)


Universal Containers 允許所有員工使用一個名為 Review 的自訂物件來提交對領導層的評論。這些評論應該只有人力資源部門和提交該記錄的員工本人才能看到。
應用程式建構者應採取哪三個步驟來適當地控制對 Review 的存取？(選擇 3 個答案)

A. Disable Grant Access Using Hierarchies.
     

停用「使用階層授與存取權」。

B. Add a Master-Detail (User) field on the Review object.
     

在 Review 物件上新增一個主從式 (使用者) 欄位。

C. Create a criteria-based Sharing Rule for the HR Department.
     

為人力資源部門建立一個基於條件的共用規則。

D. Remove Review Read permission from non-HR Department user Profiles.
     

從非人力資源部門使用者的設定檔中移除 Review 的讀取權限。

E. Set organization-wide default to Private.
     

將全組織預設值設為「私人」。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C, E (註：題庫答案為 A, C, D，但 A, E, C 才是邏輯上最完整的組合。此處依題庫答案解釋，並補充正確邏輯。)

詳解 (Explanation):
Disable Grant Access Using Hierarchies, Create a criteria-based Sharing Rule for the HR Department, and Remove Review Read permission from non-HR profiles. These are correct because disabling Grant Access Using Hierarchies prevents users above the record owner in the role hierarchy from viewing the Review records, creating a criteria-based Sharing Rule for the HR Department allows users in that group to view all Review records, and removing Review Read permission from non-HR profiles prevents users in other profiles from viewing any Review records. (A more standard approach would be A, C, E).
(中文詳解 - 基於正確邏輯)
為了實現這個嚴格的存取控制，應遵循「從最嚴格開始，逐步放寬」的原則：

E. 將 OWD 設為「私人 (Private)」：這是基礎。這樣預設只有記錄的負責人（提交者）能看到記錄。

A. 停用「使用階層授與存取權」：由於評論的敏感性，即使是提交者的主管也不應該能自動看到。停用這個選項可以阻止角色階層帶來的預設存取權。

C. 為 HR 部門建立共用規則：建立一個公開群組給 HR 部門，然後設定一條共用規則，將所有 Review 記錄的讀取權限分享給這個群組。
(註：題庫答案 D 雖然也能達到限制非 HR 員工的目的，但與 E 在邏輯上有些重疊，A、E、C 的組合更為標準和完整。)


【第一百四十六題 / NO. 146】


Universal Containers wants to display the real-time stock price for each Account on the Account record page.
How should an app builder implement this request?


Universal Containers 希望在每個帳戶的記錄頁面上顯示該公司的即時股價。
應用程式建構者應如何實現此請求？

A. Create a Lightning Web Component.
     

建立一個 Lightning Web 元件。

B. Install a solution from the AppExchange.
     

從 AppExchange 安裝一個解決方案。

C. Build a Flow that uses API calls.
     

建立一個使用 API 呼叫的 Flow。

D. Use a scheduled Apex job.
     

使用一個已排程的 Apex 工作。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The best way to implement this request is to create a Lightning Web Component that can fetch the real-time stock price from an external API and display it on the Account record page. Installing a solution from the AppExchange may not be feasible as it may not match the exact requirements or may have additional costs. Building a Flow that uses API calls may not be efficient as it may consume API limits and may not be able to update the stock price in real-time.

實現這個「即時」顯示外部資料需求的最佳方法是建立一個 Lightning Web 元件 (LWC)。LWC 可以在前端（使用者瀏覽器）直接呼叫外部的股價 API，並將獲取的即時資料顯示在頁面上，而無需將資料儲存在 Salesforce 中。 雖然 AppExchange (B) 可能有現成方案，但 LWC 提供了最高的客製化彈性。Flow (C) 進行 API 呼叫的即時性和使用者體驗較差，而排程 Apex (D) 則無法滿足即時性要求。

【第一百四十七題 / NO. 147】


Universal Containers uses a custom object called Projects. When managers assign projects they set a custom field on the project called Estimated_Hours__c. Once set, users should be able to decrease but not increase the value.
How can an app builder meet this requirement?


Universal Containers 使用一個名為 Projects 的自訂物件。當經理指派專案時，他們會設定專案上一個名為 Estimated_Hours__c 的自訂欄位。一旦設定後，使用者應該能夠減少但不能增加該值。
應用程式建構者應如何滿足此需求？

A. Create a formula default value for the custom field.
     

為該自訂欄位建立一個公式預設值。

B. Create a formula field that uses the PREVGROUPVAL function
     

建立一個使用 PREVGROUPVAL 函數的公式欄位。

C. Create a validation rule that uses the ISCHANGED function
     

建立一個使用 ISCHANGED 函數的驗證規則。

D. Create a validation rule that uses the PRIORVALUE function.
     

建立一個使用 PRIORVALUE 函數的驗證規則。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
Create a validation rule that uses the PRIORVALUE function is how an app builder can meet the requirement. According to the Salesforce documentation, "PRIORVALUE returns the previous value of a field." The validation rule can compare the current value and the prior value of Estimated_Hours__c and display an error message if the current value is greater than the prior value.

應建立一個使用 PRIORVALUE() 函數的「驗證規則 (Validation Rule)」。PRIORVALUE(field) 函數可以取得欄位在儲存前的原始值。因此，可以設定一條驗證規則，其錯誤條件公式為：
Estimated_Hours__c > PRIORVALUE(Estimated_Hours__c)
這條規則的含義是：如果「預估工時」的新值大於它的舊值，則驗證失敗，阻止記錄儲存。這就完美地實現了「只能減少，不能增加」的需求。

【第一百四十八題 / NO. 148】


What option is available to an App Builder when defining an object-specific Create Record custom action? (Choose 2 answers)


在定義一個物件特定的「建立記錄」自訂動作時，應用程式建構者有哪些選項可用？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Pre-Defining field values on the target object.
     

預先定義目標物件上的欄位值。

B. Redirecting the end user to the detail page of the target object
     

將使用者重新導向到目標物件的詳細資料頁面。

C. Specifying the fields and layout of the action.
     

指定該動作的欄位和版面配置。

D. Allowing the end user to choose the record type
     

允許使用者選擇記錄類型。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder has two options available when defining an object-specific Create Record custom action: 1. Pre-Defining field values on the target object. This means that the app builder can specify default values for certain fields...when creating a new record using the custom action. 2. Specifying the fields and layout of the action. This means that the app builder can choose which fields to include in the action and how they are arranged on the screen.

在定義「建立記錄」的快速動作時，建構者可以：

A. 預先定義欄位值：可以設定預設值，例如從來源記錄中帶入某些欄位的值，或者設定固定的值。

C. 指定欄位和版面配置：可以自訂這個快速動作彈出視窗的版面配置，決定要顯示哪些欄位、欄位的順序，以及哪些是必填的。


【第一百四十九題 / NO. 149】


Which opportunity standard field is available to be configured directly? (Choose 3 answers)


哪個機會的標準欄位可以直接設定？(選擇 3 個答案)
(註：此題原文為 "directly in the page layout"，意指可直接在版面配置編輯器中設定，如修改選項值等)

A. Forecast category
     

預測種類

B. Stage
     

階段

C. Lead source
     

潛在客戶來源

D. Type
     

類型

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C, D

詳解 (Explanation):
The opportunity standard fields that are available to be configured directly are Stage, Lead Source, and Type. These fields can be modified by editing their picklist values, adding or removing values, or changing their default values. Forecast Category is not a standard field on the opportunity object, but rather a system field that is automatically derived from the Stage field.

「階段 (Stage)」、「潛在客戶來源 (Lead Source)」和「類型 (Type)」都是「機會」物件上的標準選項清單 (picklist) 欄位。這意味著管理員可以直接進入「物件管理員」來編輯、新增或移除這些欄位的選項值。
相反地，「預測種類 (Forecast Category)」是一個系統欄位，它的值是根據「階段」欄位的值自動決定的，無法直接編輯其選項值。

【第一百五十題 / NO. 150】


An app builder has been asked to display an overdue date that is two months after a task's due date.
Which approach should the app builder take?


一位應用程式建構者被要求顯示一個逾期日期，該日期是一個工作到期日的兩個月後。
建構者應採取何種方法？

A. Use process builder and set overdue date equal to Due Date + ((365/12)*2)
     

使用 Process builder 並將逾期日期設為 Due Date + ((365/12)*2)。

B. Create a formula field using Due Date + 60
     

建立一個使用 Due Date + 60 的公式欄位。

C. Use process builder and set overdue Date equal to Due Date + 60
     

使用 Process builder 並將逾期日期設為 Due Date + 60。

D. Create a formula field using the ADDMONTHS() function
     

建立一個使用 ADDMONTHS() 函數的公式欄位。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
The best way to calculate an overdue date that is two months after a task due date is to use a formula field with the ADDMONTHS() function. This function adds a specified number of months to a date value, and returns a new date value. Using + 60 is inaccurate because months have different numbers of days.

計算「N 個月後」的日期，最準確且最佳的方法是使用 ADDMONTHS(date, num) 函數。這個函數會精確地處理月份的增減，包括跨年和大小月的情況。因此，應建立一個公式欄位，其公式為 ADDMONTHS(DueDate, 2)。 使用 + 60 的方法是不準確的，因為每個月的天數不同。

【第一百五十一題 / NO. 151】


On the Account Lightning record page, users need to see ten fields and the ability to sort and wrap text on their Related Lists.

在帳戶 Lightning 記錄頁面上，使用者需要在他們的相關清單上看到十個欄位，並能夠進行排序和文字換行。
應用程式建構者應為相關清單 Lightning 元件選擇哪種相關清單類型？

A. Enhanced List
     

增強清單

B. Basic List
     

基本清單

C. ListView
     

清單檢視

D. List Class
     

清單類別

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should select Enhanced List for the Related List type for the Related List Lightning component. Enhanced List allows users to see up to ten fields, sort, wrap text, and perform mass actions on their Related Lists. Basic List only allows users to see four fields and has limited functionality.

在 Lightning 記錄頁面上設定「相關清單」元件時，有兩種主要類型可選。為了滿足顯示最多十個欄位、可排序、可文字換行等高級功能，應選擇「增強清單 (Enhanced List)」。 「基本清單 (Basic List)」只顯示前四個欄位，且功能非常有限。

【第一百五十二題 / NO. 152】


Universal Containers requires different fields to be filled out at each stage of the Opportunity sales process.
What configuration steps can an app builder use to meet this requirement?


Universal Containers 要求在機會銷售流程的每個階段都需要填寫不同的欄位。
應用程式建構者可以使用哪些設定步驟來滿足此需求？

A. Set page layout required fields based on the current stage.
     

根據目前階段在頁面版面配置上設定必填欄位。

B. Create a Process Builder to prompt the User for field information.
     

建立一個 Process Builder 來提示使用者輸入欄位資訊。

C. Define record types and page layouts for each stage.
     

為每個階段定義記錄類型和頁面版面配置。

D. Add the Path component to the Lightning record page.
     

將「路徑」元件新增到 Lightning 記錄頁面。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should use the Path component to meet the requirement. The Path component is a Lightning component that displays the key fields and guidance for each stage of a standard or custom picklist field, such as the Opportunity Stage field. The app builder can configure the Path component to show the fields that need to be filled out...for each stage. While validation rules could enforce this, Path is designed to guide users through the process.

應使用「路徑 (Path)」元件。Path 專為引導使用者完成業務流程而設計。在設定 Path 時，您可以為機會的每個「階段 (Stage)」指定「關鍵欄位 (Key Fields)」。這些欄位會直接顯示在路徑元件中，方便使用者在推進階段時快速填寫，從而滿足在不同階段填寫不同欄位的需求。 雖然也可以用驗證規則來強制填寫，但 Path 提供了更好的使用者引導體驗。

【第一百五十三題 / NO. 153】

加總

最小值

The app builder should use Sum as the type of summary in the roll-up summary field.
