【第一百五十五題 / NO. 155】


An app builder wants to update a field on the parent record when a child record connected via lookup is deleted.
What automation should the app builder use?


一位應用程式建構者希望在一個透過查詢關係連接的子記錄被刪除時，更新父記錄上的一個欄位。
建構者應該使用哪種自動化工具？

A. Screen flow
     

畫面流程

B. Process Builder

C. Apex code
     

Apex 程式碼

D. Workflow rule
     

工作流程規則

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should use Apex code to update a field on the parent record when a child record connected via lookup is deleted. Apex code is a programming language that allows developers to execute complex logic... Apex code can be triggered by certain events, such as insert, update, delete, or undelete of records. Standard declarative automation tools like Flow, Process Builder, and Workflow Rules cannot trigger on the delete event.

應使用 Apex 程式碼。標準的宣告式自動化工具，如 Flow、Process Builder 和 Workflow Rules，都無法在記錄被刪除 (on delete) 時觸發。唯一能夠捕捉刪除事件並執行複雜邏輯（如更新相關的父記錄）的方法是編寫一個「Apex 觸發器 (Apex Trigger)」。

【第一百五十六題 / NO. 156】


Universal Containers has two types of applicants, hourly and salary. There are separate record types for each. While all members of the human resource department need to be able to view all applicant records, only the hiring Manager and VP of HR should be able to create salary applicant records.
What should the app builder recommend to meet this requirement?


Universal Containers 有兩種類型的申請人：時薪制和月薪制。每種類型都有獨立的記錄類型。雖然所有人力資源部門的成員都需要能夠查看所有申請人記錄，但只有招聘經理和人資副總應該能夠建立月薪制申請人記錄。
應用程式建構者應推薦什麼方案來滿足此需求？

A. Update the org-wide default to private and create a sharing rule for the role of recruiting manager.
     

將全組織預設值更新為私人，並為招聘經理角色建立一個共用規則。

B. Create a permission set containing the salary record type and assign it to the appropriate users.
     

建立一個包含月薪記錄類型的權限集，並將其指派給適當的使用者。

C. Remove "create" permission for the salary applicant object for everyone except the manager and VP.
     

移除除了經理和副總之外所有人對月薪申請人物件的「建立」權限。

D. Configure the hourly record type as the default and instruct non-management users to accept the default record type.
     

將時薪記錄類型設定為預設，並指示非管理層使用者接受預設記錄類型。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
A permission set containing the salary record type and assigning it to the appropriate users would allow only those users to create salary applicant records, while still allowing all users to view all applicant records. This is the most granular and flexible way to meet the requirement.

最佳方法是使用「權限集 (Permission Set)」。可以這樣設定：
在所有相關使用者的「設定檔 (Profile)」中，只分配「時薪」記錄類型的存取權限。
建立一個新的權限集，在其中授予「月薪」記錄類型的存取權限。
將這個權限集只指派給招聘經理和人資副總。
這樣，只有被指派了權限集的使用者在建立新記錄時才能選擇「月薪」記錄類型。

Which two solutions should an app builder suggest to help meet these requirements? (Choose 2 answers)


Universal Containers 希望對其機會頁面版面配置進行一些增強，以提高效率和協作。

C. 新增「路徑 (Path)」元件：Path 可以視覺化地展示銷售流程的各個階段，並在每個階段提供「成功指引」和顯示「關鍵欄位」，能極大地引導使用者，提高效率和協作。

A. 標記階段相依欄位為必填：這可以透過「驗證規則」或在 Path 中設定來實現，確保在進入下一階段前，所有必要的資訊都已填寫完整，從而提高資料品質和效率。 (註：頁面版面配置本身無法根據階段動態設定必填，但 Path 或驗證規則可以)。


【第一百五十八題 / NO. 158】


Universal Containers conducts evaluations of their sales reps using a custom object consisting of numerical scores and executive comments. The company wants to ensure that only the sales reps, and their manager's executive can view the rep's evaluation record but the reps should not be able to view the executive comment field on their review.
How can these requirements be met?


Universal Containers 使用一個包含數值分數和主管評論的自訂物件來對其銷售代表進行評估。公司希望確保只有銷售代表本人和他們經理的主管可以檢視該代表的評估記錄，但代表本人不應該能看到他們評估中的主管評論欄位。
如何滿足這些需求？

A. Use a private sharing model granting record access using hierarchy; manage field access with record types and field-level security
     

使用私人共用模型，透過階層授與記錄存取權；透過記錄類型和欄位級別安全性管理欄位存取權。

B. Use a private sharing model granting record access using custom setting; manage field access with page layouts and field level security
     

使用私人共用模型，透過自訂設定授與記錄存取權；透過頁面版面配置和欄位級別安全性管理欄位存取權。

C. Use a private sharing model granting record access using hierarchy; manage field access with field-level security
     

使用私人共用模型，透過階層授與記錄存取權；透過欄位級別安全性管理欄位存取權。

D. Use a private sharing model granting record access using custom setting manage field access with record types and page layouts
     

使用私人共用模型，透過自訂設定管理記錄存取權；透過記錄類型和頁面版面配置管理欄位存取權。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
To ensure that only the sales reps and their manager's executive can view the rep's evaluation record but the reps should not be able to view the executive comment field...a private sharing model granting record access using hierarchy and field-level security should be used. A private sharing model means that only the owner of a record and users above them in the role hierarchy can view the record by default. Field-level security controls which fields are visible or editable for different profiles or permission sets.

這個需求需要結合兩種安全控制：
記錄層級存取：將該自訂物件的 OWD 設為「私人 (Private)」。這樣，預設只有記錄負責人（銷售代表）和其角色階層中的上級（經理、主管等）可以存取記錄。
欄位層級存取：使用「欄位級別安全性 (Field-Level Security, FLS)」來控制「主管評論」欄位的可見性。將此欄位對銷售代表的設定檔 (Profile) 或權限集設為「不可見 (Not Visible)」，同時對經理和主管的設定檔設為「可見 (Visible)」。

【第一百五十九題 / NO. 159】


An app builder has created a custom Lightning App and wants to make it available to the internal users at Universal Containers.
Which two steps are necessary to accomplish this task? (Choose 2 answers)


一位應用程式建構者已經建立了一個自訂的 Lightning 應用程式，並希望讓 Universal Containers 的內部使用者可以使用它。
完成此任務需要哪兩個必要的步驟？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Add the app to a Visualforce page.
     

將應用程式新增到 Visualforce 頁面。

B. Upload the app to Static Resources.
     

將應用程式上傳到靜態資源。

C. Create a subdomain using My Domain.
     

使用「我的網域」建立一個子網域。

D. Build a Custom Tab for the app.
     

為該應用程式建立一個自訂索引標籤。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C, D

詳解 (Explanation):
Create a subdomain using My Domain: My Domain is a feature that allows an organization to set up a custom domain name for their Salesforce instance. This is required to use custom Lightning components and apps. Build a Custom Tab for the app: A custom tab is a tab that displays any custom object or web page in Salesforce. This is required to make the custom Lightning App accessible from the navigation menu or app launcher.

為了讓使用者能使用自訂的 Lightning 應用程式，需要：

C. 建立「我的網域 (My Domain)」：使用 Lightning 元件和自訂 Lightning 應用程式的前提是必須在組織中啟用並部署「我的網域」。

D. 建立自訂索引標籤 (Custom Tab)：您需要為您的 Lightning 應用程式頁面建立一個「Lightning 頁面索引標籤」，這樣才能將它加入到導覽列中，讓使用者可以點擊並存取。


【第一百六十題 / NO. 160】


Universal Containers assigns system access via permission sets and permission set groups to ensure each user has proper access. One department with varying levels of support staff has five consistent permission sets they require in order to complete their duties. Some higher-level staff have additional permission sets that are only required for them.
How should an app builder recommend assigning permission sets to users?


Universal Containers 透過權限集和權限集群組來指派系統存取權，以確保每個使用者都有適當的存取權。一個支援人員級別不同的部門，有五個他們完成職責所需的一致權限集。一些較高層級的員工還有一些只對他們才需要的額外權限集。
應用程式建構者應如何推薦指派權限集給使用者？

A. Utilize the manage assignments button to assign a permission set group and additional individual permission sets to each user.
     

利用「管理指派」按鈕，為每個使用者指派一個權限集群組和額外的個別權限集。

B. Utilize the manage assignments button to assign each user with the same set of permission set groups and permission sets.
     

利用「管理指派」按鈕，為每個使用者指派相同的權限集群組和權限集組合。

C. Utilize the Data Import Wizard to mass update the desired users with their full list of permission sets and permission set groups.
     

利用「資料匯入精靈」來大量更新所需使用者，給予他們完整的權限集和權限集群組清單。

D. Utilize the Data Loader to mass update the desired users with their full list of permission sets and permission set groups.
     

利用 Data Loader 來大量更新所需使用者，給予他們完整的權限集和權限集群組清單。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should recommend utilizing the manage assignments button to assign a permission set group and additional individual permission sets to each user. This way, the app builder can assign the five consistent permission sets to all users in one permission set group, and then assign additional permission sets to higher-level staff as needed.

最佳實踐是將所有部門成員都需要的五個一致權限集打包成一個「權限集群組 (Permission Set Group)」。然後，將這個權限集群組指派給部門中的所有使用者。對於那些需要額外權限的較高層級員工，再單獨為他們指派那些額外的個別權限集。這種方法既簡化了對基礎權限的管理，又保持了對特殊權限指派的靈活性。

【第一百六十一題 / NO. 161】


Ursa Major Solar wants to see the Type field from the parent object Galaxy listed on the child record Star. The app builder is receiving an error stating "Picklist values are only supported in certain functions".
What formula should an app builder use to achieve the desired result?


Ursa Major Solar 公司希望在子記錄 Star 上，看到來自父物件 Galaxy 的 Type 欄位。應用程式建構者收到一個錯誤，指出「選項清單值僅在特定函數中受支援」。
應用程式建構者應使用哪個公式來達到預期結果？

A. ISPICKVAL (Galaxy__r.Type__c)

B. VALUE(Galaxy__r.Type__c)

C. TEXT(Galaxy__r.Type__c)

D. FIND(Galaxy__r.Type__c)


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
TEXT() is a formula function that converts a picklist value to text. This can be used to display the Type field from the parent object Galaxy on the child record Star. The error message occurs because you cannot directly reference a picklist field from another object in a formula; it must be converted to text first.

在公式欄位中直接引用另一個物件的選項清單 (picklist) 欄位時，會出現錯誤。您必須使用 TEXT() 函數將該選項清單的值轉換為純文字格式，然後才能在公式中顯示或使用它。因此，正確的公式是 TEXT(Galaxy__r.Type__c)。

【第一百六十二題 / NO. 162】


Universal Containers is adding drone delivery to service offerings, and the developer has written and tested code prior to deployment to production, and the change set is ready to go. The deployment window will occur when the developer is on vacation.
What can the app builder do to ensure a smooth deployment to production?


Universal Containers 正在將無人機配送加入到服務項目中，開發人員在部署到生產環境之前已經編寫並測試了程式碼，變更集也已準備就緒。但部署窗口期間，開發人員正在休假。
應用程式建構者可以做什麼來確保順利部署到生產環境？

A. Remove Apex classes from outbound change set
     

從傳出的變更集中移除 Apex 類別。

B. Validate the inbound change set.
     

驗證傳入的變更集。

C. Use a metadata package set.
     

使用一個 metadata 封裝集。

D. Validate the outbound change set.
     

驗證傳出的變更集。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should validate the inbound change set to ensure a smooth deployment to production. Validating an inbound change set allows the app builder to test whether the change set can be deployed without errors in the target org. Validating an inbound change set does not affect any data or metadata in the target org. This can be done ahead of the actual deployment window to identify any potential issues.

最佳實踐是在實際部署之前，先在目標環境（生產環境）中「驗證傳入的變更集 (Validate the inbound change set)」。驗證過程會模擬一次完整的部署，包括執行所有的 Apex 測試，但不會實際儲存任何變更。這可以讓建構者提前發現任何潛在的錯誤（如測試失敗、遺漏相依元件等），並在部署窗口到來之前進行修正，確保正式部署時的成功率。

【第一百六十三題 / NO. 163】


Managers at Universal Containers want a quick way to create additional accounts to form a hierarchy from a Parent Account record. They want to auto-populate five fields based on the parent to make it easier for users to create the child accounts quickly.
What should the app builder recommend?


Universal Containers 的經理希望有一種快速的方法，可以從一個父帳戶記錄中建立額外的帳戶來形成一個層級結構。他們希望根據父帳戶自動填入五個欄位，以便使用者能更輕鬆地快速建立子帳戶。
應用程式建構者應推薦什麼？

A. Add Path on Account hierarchy
     

在帳戶層級上新增「路徑」。

B. Add a custom link on Account
     

在帳戶上新增一個自訂連結。

C. Customize a Global Quick Action
     

自訂一個全域快速動作。

D. Create a custom action
     

建立一個自訂動作。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
Create a custom action is the recommended solution. According to the Salesforce documentation, "Actions let users quickly create or update records... in the context of a particular object." A custom action can auto-populate fields based on the parent account and make it easier for users to create child accounts. Global Quick Actions (C) are not tied to a specific record context.

應推薦「建立一個自訂動作 (Create a custom action)」，更具體地說，是一個「物件特定的快速動作」。這種動作建立在「帳戶」物件上，因此可以感知到它是在哪個父帳戶記錄上被觸發的。在設定這個動作時，您可以定義預設值，將父帳戶的欄位值（例如 Account.Name）帶入到新子帳戶的對應欄位中，從而實現自動填入。 全域快速動作則無法獲取父帳戶的上下文資訊。

【第一百六十四題 / NO. 164】


Universal Containers would like to automatically assign a specific permission set to new users.
How can this requirement be met? (Choose 2 Answers)


Universal Containers 希望能自動將一個特定的權限集指派給新建立的使用者。
如何滿足此需求？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Create an approval process on the User object to assign a permission set
     

在使用者物件上建立一個批准流程來指派權限集。

B. Create a flow on the user object to assign a permission set.
     

在使用者物件上建立一個 Flow 來指派權限集。

C. Create a lightning process on the user object to launch a flow.
     

在使用者物件上建立一個 Lightning Process 來啟動一個 Flow。

D. Create a workflow rule on the User object to assign a permission set.
     

在使用者物件上建立一個工作流程規則來指派權限集。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C (註：現在建議直接使用 Flow (B))

詳解 (Explanation):
A flow or a process can be used to assign a permission set to new users. A flow can be triggered by a record change... while a process can launch a flow as an immediate or scheduled action. Workflow rules cannot assign permission sets.

滿足此需求的無程式碼方法是使用 Flow 或 Process Builder。

B. 建立一個 Flow：可以建立一個在「使用者」記錄建立時觸發的 Record-Triggered Flow。在 Flow 中，使用「指派權限集 (Assign Permission Set)」動作來完成指派。

C. 建立一個 Process Builder 來啟動 Flow：這是舊的作法。建立一個在使用者物件上觸發的 Process Builder，然後在動作中呼叫一個可啟動的 Flow (invocable flow) 來執行權限集的指派。
工作流程規則 (Workflow Rule) 沒有指派權限集的動作。


【第一百六十五題 / NO. 165】


An app builder wants to use Process Builder to automate some of the work being done by the sales team.
What are three capabilities of Process Builder that can improve productivity? (Choose 3 answers)


一位應用程式建構者希望使用 Process Builder 來自動化銷售團隊正在做的一些工作。
Process Builder 的哪三項功能可以提高生產力？(選擇 3 個答案)

A. Send an email alert.
     

傳送電子郵件警示。

B. Update a related record.
     

更新一筆相關記錄。

C. Send an outbound message.
     

傳送傳出訊息。

D. Delete a related record.
     

刪除一筆相關記錄。

E. Create a child record.
     

建立一筆子記錄。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, B, E

詳解 (Explanation):
Send an email alert, update a related record, and create a child record are three capabilities of Process Builder that can improve productivity for the sales team. Process Builder can automate these actions based on criteria or events. Send an outbound message and delete a related record are not capabilities of Process Builder.

Process Builder 支援多種自動化動作，其中包括：

A. 傳送電子郵件警示：在滿足條件時自動發送預設的郵件通知。

B. 更新相關記錄：不僅能更新觸發流程的記錄本身，還能更新與其相關的父記錄或子記錄。

E. 建立子記錄：在滿足條件時自動建立一筆新的記錄（例如，當機會成交時自動建立一個訂單記錄）。
Process Builder 本身不能刪除記錄或直接傳送傳出訊息（傳出訊息是 Workflow 的功能）。


【第一百六十六題 / NO. 166】


DreamHouse Realty (DR) has a policy that requires the phone number on Contact to be deleted when the DoNotCall checkbox is checked.
What automation tool should the app builder recommend?


DreamHouse Realty (DR) 有一項政策，要求當「請勿致電 (DoNotCall)」核取方塊被勾選時，必須刪除連絡人上的電話號碼。
應用程式建構者應推薦哪種自動化工具？

A. Quick action
     

快速動作

B. Approval process
     

批准流程

C. Validation rule
     

驗證規則

D. Workflow rule
     

工作流程規則

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D (註：現在應使用 Flow，但 Workflow Rule 仍是此題庫的正確答案)

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should recommend a workflow rule to automate this process. A workflow rule is a type of automation tool that can execute actions based on certain criteria. In this case, the workflow rule can have a criterion that evaluates if the DoNotCall checkbox is checked on a Contact record, and then execute a field update action that sets the Phone field to null.

應推薦使用「工作流程規則 (Workflow Rule)」。這是一個簡單的自動化需求：當一個欄位滿足特定條件時，更新同一個記錄上的另一個欄位。可以設定一條工作流程規則，觸發條件為「當 DoNotCall 核取方塊等於 True 時」，執行的動作為「欄位更新 (Field Update)」，將 Phone 欄位的值設定為空 (null)。 Flow 也能完成此任務，但對於如此簡單的場景，Workflow Rule（在它被淘汰前）是個非常直接的選擇。

【第一百六十七題 / NO. 167】


An app builder wants to limit the number of fields users are required to fill out when creating a new Opportunity. Once they fill out the required fields and save, the full record page with additional fields relevant to the Opportunity type becomes available.
How could this be accomplished?


一位應用程式建構者希望限制使用者在建立新機會時需要填寫的欄位數量。一旦他們填寫完必填欄位並儲存後，與該機會類型相關的、包含額外欄位的完整記錄頁面就會變得可用。
如何實現這一點？

A. Make the Opportunity type a required field on the initial Opportunity page layout and use automation to fill in the type field to a record type.
     

在初始的機會頁面版面配置上將「機會類型」設為必填欄位，並使用自動化將類型欄位填入到一個記錄類型中。

B. Use different page layouts for Opportunity types based on the user profile.
    ˆ

根據使用者設定檔為不同的機會類型使用不同的頁面版面配置。

C. Once the required fields are populated, use a sharing rule to share the new fields with the user.
     

一旦必填欄位被填入，使用共用規則將新欄位與使用者共用。

D. Hide additional sections on the page layout and show the users how to manually expand them when they want to fill in the fields in the hidden sections.
     

在頁面版面配置上隱藏額外的區段，並教導使用者在想要填寫隱藏區段中的欄位時如何手動展開它們。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A (註：此答案描述了一個較為複雜的實現方式，更常見的作法是讓使用者在第一步選擇記錄類型。)

詳解 (Explanation):
Making the Opportunity type a required field on the initial Opportunity page layout and using automation to fill in the type field to a record type is a way to limit the number of fields users are required to fill out when creating a new Opportunity. This way, the app builder can assign different page layouts for different record types based on the Opportunity type.

這個方法的邏輯是：
建立一個非常簡潔的初始頁面版面配置，上面只有最少的必填欄位，包括一個「機會類型」的選項清單。
為每種機會類型建立不同的記錄類型，並為每個記錄類型指派一個包含完整欄位的頁面版面配置。
設定一個自動化流程（例如 Flow），當新機會被建立且「機會類型」被填寫時，自動將該記錄的「記錄類型 (Record Type)」更新為對應的類型。
當記錄被儲存並觸發自動化後，使用者再次查看該記錄時，就會因為記錄類型已變更而看到完整的頁面版面配置。

【第一百六十八題 / NO. 168】


An App Builder is loading the data into salesforce. To link the new records back to the legacy system, a field will be used to track the legacy ID on the account object. For future data loads this ID will be used when upserting records.
Which two field attributes should be selected? (Choose 2 answers)


一位應用程式建構者正在將資料載入到 Salesforce 中。為了將新記錄與舊系統連結起來，將在帳戶物件上使用一個欄位來追蹤舊系統的 ID。對於未來的資料載入，這個 ID 將在更新插入 (upserting) 記錄時使用。
應該選擇哪兩個欄位屬性？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Unique
     

唯一

B. Required
     

必填

C. External ID
     

外部 ID

D. Text (encrypted)
     

文字 (已加密)

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C

詳解 (Explanation):
The field attributes that should be selected are Unique and External I

D. Unique means that the field will not allow duplicate values. External ID means that the field can be used as a foreign key for data imports and upserts.

為了在資料載入時用作匹配鍵，應選擇以下兩個屬性：

C. 外部 ID (External ID)：將一個欄位標記為「外部 ID」是告訴 Salesforce，這個欄位包含來自外部系統的唯一識別碼，可以用於 upsert 操作（一種結合了插入和更新的操作）來匹配記錄。

A. 唯一 (Unique)：將欄位設為「唯一」可以確保 Salesforce 中不會有兩筆記錄擁有相同的舊系統 ID，這有助於保持資料的完整性和匹配的準確性。


【第一百六十九題 / NO. 169】


The app builder needs to change the data types of a new custom field. The app builder is not able to delete and recreate any of the fields, nor modify any apex code.
Which data type change will require the app builder to perform the additional steps in order to retain existing functionalities?


應用程式建構者需要更改一個新自訂欄位的資料類型。建構者不能刪除並重新建立任何欄位，也不能修改任何 Apex 程式碼。
哪種資料類型變更將需要建構者執行額外的步驟以保留現有功能？
(註：此題原文可能有誤，因為題目假設不能修改 Apex，但答案 A 的影響正是 Apex。我們依題庫邏輯回答。)

A. Changing the data type of a field used in an apex class from number to text.
     

將一個在 Apex 類別中使用過的欄位，其資料類型從數字更改為文字。

B. Changing the data type of a field used in a report from a text to an encrypted field
     

將一個在報告中使用過的欄位，其資料類型從文字更改為加密欄位。

C. Changing the data type of a field used as an external id from number to text.
     

將一個作為外部 ID 使用的欄位，其資料類型從數字更改為文字。

D. Changing the data type of a field used in lead conversion from number to text
     

將一個在潛在客戶轉換中使用過的欄位，其資料類型從數字更改為文字。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
Changing the data type of a field used in an apex class from number to text will require the app builder to perform additional steps. This is because changing the data type of a field may affect the apex code that references or manipulates the field value, and may cause compilation errors or unexpected results. If the app builder cannot modify the Apex code, this change might be blocked entirely or cause runtime errors.

將一個被 Apex 程式碼引用的欄位資料類型從「數字」改為「文字」會產生最大的影響。Apex 是強型別語言，如果程式碼期望處理一個數字（例如進行數學運算），而欄位變成了文字，將會導致程式碼編譯失敗或在執行時出錯。因此，這種變更會直接破壞現有的 Apex 功能，需要開發人員介入修改程式碼才能保留功能。

【第一百七十題 / NO. 170】


An app builder would like to streamline the user experience by reflecting summarized calculations of specific fields on various objects.
Which field types could be used in roll-up summary fields to accomplish this? (Choose 3 answers)


一位應用程式建構者希望透過在各種物件上反映特定欄位的匯總計算來簡化使用者體驗。
可以在總計欄位中使用哪些欄位類型來完成此任務？(選擇 3 個答案)

A. Currency
     

貨幣

B. Percent
     

百分比

C. Date
     

日期

D. Checkbox
     

核取方塊

E. Time
     

時間

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, B, D (註：題庫答案為 A, B, D，但這是一個有爭議的點。)

詳解 (Explanation):
Roll-up summary fields can only be created on master-detail relationships, and they can calculate numeric fields, such as currency, percent, and number. Checkbox fields can be used in roll-up summary with the COUNT function (it counts the records where the checkbox is true). Date and time fields can be used with MIN and MAX, but not SUM or AVG. Given the options, Currency and Percent are valid for SUM/AVG/MIN/MAX, and Checkbox is valid for COUNT.

總計欄位 (Roll-up summary fields) 可以對子記錄的特定欄位進行計算。可用的欄位類型和計算方式如下：

A. 貨幣 (Currency)：可以進行 SUM, AVG, MIN, MAX 計算。

B. 百分比 (Percent)：可以進行 SUM, AVG, MIN, MAX 計算。

D. 核取方塊 (Checkbox)：只能用於 COUNT 計算，它會計算所有該核取方塊被勾選的記錄數量。
日期 (Date) 和時間 (Time) 欄位也可以用於 MIN 和 MAX 計算，但不能用於 SUM 或 AVG。由於題目答案選了 A, B, D，這是一個有效的組合。


【第一百七十一題 / NO. 171】


Cloud Kicks wants to summarize the number of open Cases related to an Account, as well as the number of closed Cases to indicate whether customer support utilization is high, medium, or low.
Two number fields have been created: NUM_Open_Cases__c and NUM_Closed_Cases__c. Which two automation solutions would meet these business requirements? (Choose 2 answers)


Cloud Kicks 希望匯總與一個帳戶相關的未結案個案數量，以及已結案個案的數量，以指示客戶支援利用率是高、中還是低。
已經建立了兩個數字欄位：NUM_Open_Cases__c 和 NUM_Closed_Cases__c。哪兩種自動化解決方案可以滿足這些業務需求？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. AppExchange

B. Process Builder

C. Workflow
     

工作流程

D. Apex


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, D (註：現在應使用 Flow 取代 Process Builder)

詳解 (Explanation):
Process Builder and Apex are two automation solutions that can meet the business requirements of summarizing the number of open and closed Cases related to an Account. Since the relationship between Account and Case is a standard lookup, a standard Roll-Up Summary Field cannot be used. Therefore, an automated solution is needed to count the child records and update a field on the parent. Process Builder (or more modernly, Flow) and Apex triggers are capable of this.

由於「帳戶」和「個案」之間是標準的查詢關係，而不是主從式關係，因此不能使用標準的「總計欄位」。要實現跨查詢關係的匯總計算，需要使用更進階的自動化工具。

D. Apex：可以編寫一個 Apex 觸發器，在個案建立、更新（狀態變更）或刪除時，重新計算相關帳戶的未結案和已結案個案數量，並更新帳戶上的欄位。

B. Process Builder（或現今的 Flow）：可以建立一個在個案物件上觸發的流程。當個案的狀態發生變化時，流程可以找到相關的帳戶記錄，並更新計數欄位。這比 Apex 觸發器更複雜，但也是一種無程式碼的解決方案。


【第一百七十二題 / NO. 172】


Ursa Major Solar (UMS) has a custom object where they track Galactic Vendors. The object has four custom fields for the Galactic Vendor's location:
Street__c
City__c
Planet__c
Galaxy__c
The UMS's leadership wants these fields to be concatenated into a single formula field on two lines.
Which formula fulfills this requirement?


Ursa Major Solar (UMS) 有一個自訂物件用來追蹤銀河供應商。該物件有四個自訂欄位表示供應商的位置：
Street__c (街道)
City__c (城市)
Planet__c (行星)
Galaxy__c (星系)
UMS 的領導層希望將這些欄位合併成一個顯示為兩行的單一公式欄位。
哪個公式能滿足此需求？

(選項為圖片，此處以文字描述)

A. Street & BR() & City & ", " & Planet & " " & Galaxy

B. (圖片顯示兩行文字，但非公式)
> Street
> City, Planet Galaxy

C. Street__c & BR() & City__c & ", " & Planet__c & " " & Galaxy__c

D. (圖片顯示兩行文字，但非公式)
> Street_c
> City_c, Planet_c Galaxy_c


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
This formula concatenates the four custom fields for the Galactic Vendor's location into a single text value, separated by commas and spaces. The formula also uses the BR() function to insert a line break. It correctly references the custom fields using the __c suffix.

正確的公式需要做到兩件事：
正確引用自訂欄位：自訂欄位的 API 名稱必須以 __c 結尾。
實現換行：在公式中，BR() 函數用於插入一個換行符。
選項 C 的公式 Street__c & BR() & City__c & ", " & Planet__c & " " & Galaxy__c 完整地滿足了這兩個條件，它將街道地址放在第一行，然後換行，接著是城市、行星和星系。

【第一百七十三題 / NO. 173】


Universal Containers uses a custom picklist called Account_Region__c on the Account object. The vice president of sales has asked that the value of this field is visible on Opportunities.
How should an app builder create this solution?


Universal Containers 公司在「帳戶 (Account)」物件上使用一個名為 Account_Region__c 的自訂選項清單。銷售副總要求在「機會 (Opportunities)」上也能看到此欄位的值。
應用程式建構者應如何建立此解決方案？

A. Field history tracking
     

欄位歷史追蹤

B. Cross-object formula field
     

跨物件公式欄位

C. Lookup field
     

查詢欄位

D. Field-level security
     

欄位級別安全性

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
A cross-object formula field is a formula field that references fields from another object. This can be used to display the value of the Account_Region__c field on Opportunities, as long as there is a relationship between the two objects. The formula would be TEXT(Account.Account_Region__c).

應使用「跨物件公式欄位 (Cross-object formula field)」。由於「機會」物件上已經有一個指向「帳戶」的標準關係，因此可以在「機會」物件上建立一個公式欄位，直接引用其相關帳戶的 Account_Region__c 欄位值。因為 Account_Region__c 是一個選項清單，所以公式應該寫成 TEXT(Account.Account_Region__c) 來顯示其文字值。

【第一百七十五題 / NO. 175】


An app builder wants to create a new field using Schema Builder.
Who will get access to the new field by default?


一位應用程式建構者希望使用結構描述產生器 (Schema Builder) 建立一個新欄位。
預設情況下，誰將獲得對該新欄位的存取權限？

A. Standard profiles
     

標準設定檔

B. No profiles
     

沒有設定檔

C. Internal profiles
     

內部設定檔

D. All profiles
     

所有設定檔

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D (註：此行為與在物件管理員中建立欄位不同。)

詳解 (Explanation):
All profiles will get access to the new field by default when it is created using Schema Builder. The app builder can modify the field-level security settings later to restrict access for certain profiles.

當使用「結構描述產生器 (Schema Builder)」建立一個新欄位時，Salesforce 的預設行為是將該欄位的「欄位級別安全性 (FLS)」對所有設定檔設定為可見和可編輯。這與在「物件管理員」中逐步建立欄位時可以選擇性地授予權限不同。使用 Schema Builder 建立後，管理員需要手動去調整每個設定檔對該欄位的存取權限。

【第一百七十六題 / NO. 176】


Universal Containers uses a custom picklist field Account Region on the account record. They want this region to be reflected on all related contact records and stay in sync if the value of this field changes on the Account.
How should an app builder meet this requirement?


Universal Containers 在帳戶記錄上使用一個自訂的選項清單欄位「帳戶區域」。他們希望這個區域能反映在所有相關的連絡人記錄上，並且如果帳戶上的此欄位值發生變化，連絡人上的值也能保持同步。
應用程式建構者應如何滿足此需求？

A. Create a picklist field called 'Account Region' on Contact object > Create a workflow rule to update this picklist field if the Account Region field on the Account is changed.
     

在連絡人物件上建立一個名為「帳戶區域」的選項清單欄位 > 建立一個工作流程規則，在帳戶上的「帳戶區域」欄位變更時更新此選項清單欄位。

B. Create a formula field on the Contact object > Set the value of the formula to ISPICKVAL(Account.Account_Region__c).
     

在連絡人物件上建立一個公式欄位 > 將公式的值設為 ISPICKVAL(Account.Account_Region__c)。

C. Create a formula field on the Contact object > Set the value of the formula to TEXT(Account.Account_Region__c).
     

在連絡人物件上建立一個公式欄位 > 將公式的值設為 TEXT(Account.Account_Region__c)。

D. Create a text field called 'Account Region' on Contact object > Create a workflow rule to update this picklist field if the Account Region field on the Account is changed.
     

在連絡人物件上建立一個名為「帳戶區域」的文字欄位 > 建立一個工作流程規則，在帳戶上的「帳戶區域」欄位變更時更新此選項清單欄位。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
Creating a formula field on the Contact object and setting the value of the formula to TEXT(Account.Account_Region__c) would reflect the region of the related account on the contact record and stay in sync if the value changes on the account. This is the most efficient and maintainable way to meet the requirement.

為了讓子物件 (Contact) 上的欄位能「即時同步」父物件 (Account) 上的欄位值，最佳方法是使用「跨物件公式欄位」。因為父物件的欄位是選項清單，所以在子物件的公式欄位中需要使用 TEXT() 函數將其轉換為文字來顯示。公式 TEXT(Account.Account_Region__c) 能確保只要帳戶的區域一變動，所有相關連絡人上顯示的區域值也會立即更新，無需任何自動化流程。

【第一百七十七題 / NO. 177】


Universal Containers implemented an application process that uses custom objects Internships and Applications. The organization-wide default for Internships has been set to private and is the master in the master-detail relationship with Applications. The VP of HR wants to allow edit access to Applications to recruiters.
How should an app builder configure the proper access?


Universal Containers 實施了一個使用自訂物件「實習 (Internships)」和「申請 (Applications)」的申請流程。「實習」的全組織預設值被設為私人，並且是在與「申請」的主從式關係中的主物件。人資副總希望允許招聘人員對「申請」有編輯權限。
應用程式建構者應如何設定適當的存取權限？
(註：此題的答案 D 在 Salesforce 的標準行為中是錯誤的，因為無法對主從關係的明細端建立共用規則。正確答案應為 B。此處依題庫答案。)

A. Set the organization-wide default on the Applications object to Read/Write.
     

將「申請」物件的全組織預設值設為「讀取/寫入」。

B. Add a sharing rule that grants the users Read/Write access to the Internship records.
     

新增一條共用規則，授予使用者對「實習」記錄的讀寫存取權。

C. Create a queue for the web applications and assign access to the users who will be editing the records.
     

為網站申請建立一個佇列，並將存取權限指派給將要編輯記錄的使用者。

D. Create a sharing rule that grants the users Read/Write access to the Application records.
     

建立一條共用規則，授予使用者對「申請」記錄的讀寫存取權。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D (根據題庫)

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should create a sharing rule that grants the users Read/Write access to the Application records. (Note: This is incorrect based on standard Salesforce functionality. In a Master-Detail relationship, the Detail object's sharing is 'Controlled by Parent', and you cannot create sharing rules on it. Access must be granted via the Master record. The correct answer should be

B.)

根據題庫答案的解釋：題庫認為應直接在「申請 (Applications)」物件上建立一條共用規則來授予存取權。
根據 Salesforce 實際行為的正確解釋：在主從式關係中，「申請」物件作為明細端，其共用設定是「由父項控制 (Controlled by Parent)」，這意味著您不能為它單獨建立共用規則。要授予使用者對「申請」記錄的存取權，您必須授予他們對其父記錄——「實習 (Internships)」記錄的存取權。因此，正確的作法應該是選項 B：建立一條共用規則，將相關的「實習」記錄分享給招聘人員。


【第一百七十八題 / NO. 178】


What are two reasons to create an unmanaged package? (Choose 2 answers)


建立一個未管理封裝 (unmanaged package) 的兩個原因是什麼？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Distributing open-source projects on the AppExchange.
     

在 AppExchange 上發布開源專案。

B. Publishing an application for sale on the AppExchange
     

在 AppExchange 上發布一個待售的應用程式。

C. Deploying from a Developer Edition environment
     

從一個開發人員版本環境進行部署。

D. Distributing upgradeable components to another Salesforce org
     

將可升級的元件發布到另一個 Salesforce 組織。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C

詳解 (Explanation):
The two reasons to create an unmanaged package are to distribute open-source projects on the AppExchange and to deploy from a Developer Edition environment. An unmanaged package is a collection of components that can be installed in any Salesforce org but cannot be upgraded or controlled by the developer. For selling and upgrading, a managed package (B, D) is used.

未管理封裝 (Unmanaged Package) 是一種一次性的元件分發方式，一旦安裝，其元件就會變成安裝組織的一部分，開發者無法後續控制或升級。
其主要用途包括：

A. 發布開源專案：非常適合分享範本或開源專案，因為安裝者可以自由修改其程式碼和元件。

C. 從開發人員版本環境部署：對於無法建立沙箱和生產環境之間變更集連結的 Developer Edition 組織，使用未管理封裝是將元件從開發環境遷移到另一個組織（如客戶的組織）的一種方式。
若要銷售應用程式或提供可升級的版本，則應使用「管理封裝 (Managed Package)」。


【第一百七十九題 / NO. 179】


Universal Containers' app builder has been tasked with replacing workflow rules and Apex triggers with Process Builders where possible.
What are two important considerations an app builder should know before the project is started? (Choose 2 answers)


Universal Containers 的應用程式建構者被指派在可能的情況下，用 Process Builder 取代工作流程規則和 Apex 觸發器。
在專案開始前，建構者應該知道哪兩項重要的考量因素？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Avoid generating infinite loops.
     

避免產生無限循環。

B. Apex has a different SOQL query limit than Flow.
     

Apex 與 Flow 有不同的 SOQL 查詢限制。

C. Create a process for each workflow rule.
     

為每個工作流程規則建立一個流程。

D. Combine actions when possible.
     

在可能的情況下合併動作。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, D

詳解 (Explanation):
Before replacing workflow rules and Apex triggers with Process Builders, the app builder should consider avoiding generating infinite loops and combining actions when possible. Infinite loops can occur when a process updates a record that causes another process to run on the same record. Combining actions can reduce the number of processes and improve performance and maintainability. A best practice is to have one process per object.

在建構 Process Builder（或現今的 Flow）時，有兩個重要的最佳實踐：

A. 避免無限循環：由於 Process Builder 可以觸發對記錄的更新，而這個更新又可能再次觸發同一個或其他 Process Builder，因此需要謹慎設計進入條件和遞迴設定，以避免造成無限循環，從而達到 governor limits。

D. 盡可能合併動作：Salesforce 的最佳實踐是「每個物件只建立一個記錄變更流程 (one record-change process per object)」。應該將針對同一個物件的所有自動化邏輯盡可能地合併到一個 Process Builder（或一個 Flow）中，並使用不同的條件節點來區分不同的業務場景。這有助於控制執行的順序並提高效能。


【第一百八十題 / NO. 180】


UC has a requirement that an opportunity should have a field showing the value of its associated account's billing state. This value should not change after the opportunity has been created.
What is the recommended solution to configure this automated behavior?


UC 有一個需求，要求機會上應有一個欄位顯示其關聯帳戶的帳單州別。這個值在機會建立後不應再改變。
設定此自動化行為的推薦解決方案是什麼？

A. Formula field
    ˆ

公式欄位

B. Apex

C. Workflow
     

工作流程

D. Roll-up summary field
     

總計欄位

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B (註：此題庫答案為 Apex，但更簡單的無程式碼作法是 Flow + 驗證規則。此處依題庫答案。)

詳解 (Explanation):
Apex. This is correct because Apex is a programming language that can perform complex logic and manipulate data in Salesforce. Apex can be used to create a trigger on the opportunity object that copies the value of the billing state from the related account record when the opportunity is created, and prevents it from being changed afterwards. The other options are not suitable for this requirement because they either cannot copy data from a related object (formula field, roll-up summary field) or cannot prevent data from being changed (workflow). (Note: A before-save Flow could populate the field, and a Validation Rule could prevent changes, achieving this declaratively).

根據題庫答案，推薦使用 Apex。可以編寫一個 before insert 的 Apex 觸發器，在機會記錄首次插入資料庫之前，從其關聯的帳戶中讀取 BillingState 的值，並填入到機會的對應欄位中。因為這個觸發器只在 insert 時執行，所以之後的更新將不會再改變這個值，從而滿足「建立後不再變更」的需求。
其他選項為何不適用：
公式欄位 (A)：會即時反映帳戶的值，如果帳戶的州別改變，機會上的值也會跟著變，不符合「不再改變」的需求。
工作流程/Flow (C)：雖然可以在建立時填入值，但無法阻止使用者之後手動修改它。需要額外搭配一個驗證規則才能鎖定該欄位。

【第一百八十一題 / NO. 181】


universal containers has several large customers that sell their products through dealers. Each customer and dealer have an individual rep who works directly with uc and each is billed separately.
How can an app builder implement these requirements?


Universal Containers 有幾個大客戶，他們透過經銷商 (dealers) 銷售其產品。每個客戶和經銷商都有一位直接與 UC 合作的獨立代表，並且每個都是分開計費的。
應用程式建構者應如何實現這些需求？

A. Create a single account record, add each rep as a contact and create a custom dealer object
     

建立一個單一的帳戶記錄，將每個代表新增為連絡人，並建立一個自訂的經銷商物件。

B. Create both customer and dealer as accounts, add each rep as a contact on the corresponding account and create an account hierarchy.
     

將客戶和經銷商都建立為帳戶，在相應的帳戶上將每個代表新增為連絡人，並建立一個帳戶層級。

C. Create a single parent record, add each rep as a contact to the parent account and add each dealer as a child record
     

建立一個單一的父記錄，將每個代表新增為父帳戶的連絡人，並將每個經銷商新增為子記錄。

D. Create both customer and dealer as accounts, create account teams on each account and associate the dealer records with the parent account.
     

將客戶和經銷商都建立為帳戶，在每個帳戶上建立帳戶團隊，並將經銷商記錄與父帳戶關聯。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
Creating both customer and dealer as accounts, creating account teams on each account and associating the dealer records with the parent account would allow UC to track each customer and dealer separately, as well as their relationships and reps. Account hierarchy is not suitable for this scenario, as it is used to show the relationships among parent and child accounts within a single company.

最佳作法是將客戶和經銷商都建立為獨立的「帳戶」記錄，因為他們需要分開計費。然後：
使用「帳戶團隊 (Account Teams)」來表示與該帳戶合作的代表 (rep)。
使用「父帳戶 (Parent Account)」欄位或「合作夥伴 (Partners)」相關清單來建立客戶與經銷商帳戶之間的關聯。
帳戶層級 (Account hierarchy) 通常用於表示同一公司內的母子公司關係，不適用於此客戶-經銷商場景。

【第一百八十二題 / NO. 182】


An App Builder creates an Account validation rule on the Industry field that will throw an error if the length of the field is longer than 6 characters. Another App Builder creates a workflow rule with a field update that sets the Industry field to Technology whenever the Billing City field is set to San Francisco.
What will happen the next time a sales person saves an Account with a Billing City of San Francisco?


一位應用程式建構者在「產業 (Industry)」欄位上建立了一條帳戶驗證規則，如果該欄位長度超過 6 個字元，將會拋出錯誤。另一位建構者建立了一條工作流程規則，其欄位更新會在「帳單城市 (Billing City)」欄位設為「San Francisco」時，將「產業」欄位設為「Technology」。
下一次銷售人員儲存一個帳單城市為「San Francisco」的帳戶時，會發生什麼事？

A. The record will save and the Industry field will change to Technology
     

記錄將會儲存，且「產業」欄位將變為 Technology。

B. The record will not save and the validation rule's error message will be displayed
     

記錄將不會儲存，且會顯示驗證規則的錯誤訊息。

C. The record will not save and no error message will be displayed
     

記錄將不會儲存，且不會顯示任何錯誤訊息。

D. The record will save but the Industry field will not change to Technology
     

記錄將會儲存，但「產業」欄位不會變為 Technology。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The record will not save and the validation rule's error message will be displayed because the field update will violate the validation rule. The validation rule will prevent the record from being saved if the Industry field is longer than 6 characters, and Technology is 10 characters long. In Salesforce's order of execution, workflow field updates run before validation rules are re-evaluated.

記錄將不會儲存，且會顯示驗證規則的錯誤訊息。在 Salesforce 的儲存執行順序中，工作流程的欄位更新會先執行，然後系統會再次執行驗證規則。
使用者儲存記錄，Billing City 為 "San Francisco"。
工作流程觸發，將 Industry 欄位更新為 "Technology" (長度 10)。
系統重新檢查驗證規則，發現 Industry 欄位的長度 (10) 大於 6，驗證失敗。
儲存操作被中止，並顯示驗證規則的錯誤訊息。

【第一百八十三題 / NO. 183】


Sales reps at Universal Containers use Salesforce on their mobile devices. They want a way to add new contacts quickly and then follow up later to complete the additional Information necessary.
What mobile solution should an App Builder recommend?


Universal Containers 的銷售代表在他們的行動裝置上使用 Salesforce。他們希望有一種方法可以快速新增連絡人，然後稍後再跟進以完成必要的額外資訊。
應用程式建構者應推薦哪種行動解決方案？

A. Customize the mobile menu to move Contacts to the top.
     

自訂行動功能表，將「連絡人」移到頂部。

B. Build a global action to create Contacts.
     

建立一個「建立連絡人」的全域動作。

C. Add a compact layout to Contacts.
     

為「連絡人」新增一個緊湊版面配置。

D. Use Path and set pre-defined values
     

使用「路徑」並設定預定義的值。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should recommend building a global action to create Contacts. A global action allows users to create records quickly from any page in Salesforce on their mobile devices. The app builder can configure the action layout to include only a few essential fields for quick creation.

應推薦建立一個「建立連絡人」的「全域動作 (Global Action)」。全域動作允許使用者從行動應用程式的任何地方（例如，點擊畫面底部的 + 按鈕）快速建立記錄。建構者可以為這個動作設計一個簡潔的版面配置，只包含最少的必填欄位（如姓名），讓銷售代表可以快速輸入核心資訊並儲存，之後再回來補充完整資料。

【第一百八十四題 / NO. 184】


Ursa Major Solar's sales team has been struggling to enter data on mobile since rollout; the team dislikes scrolling through all of the fields to input only the necessary data.
How could the app builder solve this with minimal impact to desktop users?


Ursa Major Solar 的銷售團隊自從推行行動版以來，一直在行動裝置上輸入資料時遇到困難；團隊不喜歡為了輸入必要的資料而滾動瀏覽所有欄位。
應用程式建構者應如何解決這個問題，同時對桌面使用者產生最小的影響？

A. Filter components by device using Form Factor.
     

使用「規格」按裝置篩選元件。

B. Reorder the fields to make sense for the reps when in the field.
     

重新排序欄位，使其對在外工作的代表來說更合理。

C. Update the training documentation with better screenshots.
     

用更好的螢幕截圖更新訓練文件。

D. Deselect the phone radio button on the Lightning record page assignment.
     

在 Lightning 記錄頁面指派中取消選取「手機」選項按鈕。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The best way to solve this problem is to filter components by device using Form Factor. Form Factor is an attribute that can be applied to components on a Lightning record page to control their visibility based on the device type, such as desktop, phone, or tablet. By using Form Factor, the app builder can create a simplified version of a component for mobile users while leaving the desktop version unchanged.

最好的解決方案是使用「規格 (Form Factor)」來按裝置篩選元件。在 Lightning 應用程式建構器中，您可以為頁面上的任何元件設定「元件可見度 (Component Visibility)」。其中一個篩選條件就是「裝置 (Device)」，您可以設定某個元件只在「桌面 (Desktop)」顯示，而另一個更簡潔的元件只在「手機 (Phone)」顯示。這樣就可以在同一個記錄頁面上為不同裝置提供不同的體驗，同時對桌面使用者影響最小。

【第一百八十五題 / NO. 185】


A Cloud Kicks employee submitted an opportunity for approval by their manager.
What would happen if the employee attempts to edit the description field after submission?


一位 Cloud Kicks 的員工提交了一個機會給他們的經理進行批准。
如果該員工在提交後嘗試編輯「描述」欄位，會發生什麼事？

A. User will be presented with a 'Record Lock' notification.
     

使用者將會看到「記錄已鎖定」的通知。

B. User will be able to edit the description field only.
     

使用者將只能編輯「描述」欄位。

C. User will see the record is now owned by their manager.
     

使用者將會看到記錄現在由他們的經理擁有。

D. User will be able to edit the name, but unable to edit the description.
     

使用者將能夠編輯名稱，但無法編輯描述。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
If an employee attempts to edit the description field after submitting an opportunity for approval, they will be presented with a 'Record Lock' notification. This means that the record is locked for editing while it is in the approval process and only users with the "Modify All" permission or the currently assigned approver (if allowed by settings) can edit it.

當一筆記錄被提交到批准流程後，它預設會被「鎖定 (Locked)」，以防止提交者在審核期間修改記錄內容，確保審核的資料是一致的。如果提交者嘗試編輯任何欄位，系統會阻止儲存並顯示一條通知，告知該記錄已被鎖定無法編輯。

【第一百八十六題 / NO. 186】


Cloud Kicks has a sales rep who is stating that their Contact is unavailable for other users to see within Salesforce.
In which three ways can an app builder troubleshoot this issue? (Choose 3 answers)


Cloud Kicks 的一位銷售代表說，他們的某個「連絡人」記錄在 Salesforce 中其他使用者看不到。
應用程式建構者可以透過哪三種方式來排解這個問題？(選擇 3 個答案)

A. Create an Account Sharing Rule to give the users access to all records.
     

建立一個帳戶共用規則，給予使用者對所有記錄的存取權。

B. Confirm whether Default Organization-Wide Sharing Settings provide access to the Account.
     

確認全組織預設共用設定是否提供了對該帳戶的存取權。

C. Review the Contact record and ensure it is linked to an Account.
     

檢查該連絡人記錄，並確保它已連結到一個帳戶。

D. Verify the users with the issue have access to the Contact object.
     

驗證有問題的使用者是否對「連絡人」物件有存取權。

E. Create a new Contact and have the users try again.
     

建立一個新的連絡人，讓使用者再試一次。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C, D

詳解 (Explanation):
To troubleshoot the issue of a contact being unavailable for other users to see, an app builder should check the following things:

D. Verify the users with the issue have access to the Contact object (Object-Level Security).

C. Review the Contact record and ensure it is linked to an Account (Private Contacts).

B. Confirm whether Default Organization-Wide Sharing Settings for Contact (often 'Controlled by Parent') and Account provide access (Record-Level Security).

排查可見性問題應從最基礎的權限開始：

D. 物件級別權限：首先確認那些看不到記錄的使用者，他們的設定檔 (Profile) 或權限集 (Permission Set) 是否至少有「連絡人」物件的「讀取 (Read)」權限。

C. 是否為私有連絡人：沒有連結到任何帳戶的連絡人是「私有的 (Private)」，預設只有其負責人和管理員能看到。檢查該連絡人是否已關聯到一個帳戶是關鍵一步。

B. 記錄級別權限 (OWD)：「連絡人」的 OWD 通常是「由父項控制 (Controlled by Parent)」。這意味著使用者能否看到連絡人，取決於他們能否看到該連絡人所屬的帳戶。因此，需要檢查帳戶的 OWD 以及是否有共用規則讓這些使用者可以看到相關的帳戶記錄。


【第一百八十七題 / NO. 187】


Universal Containers (UC) has a custom Invoice object and a custom Invoice Line Item object. The Invoice Line-Item object has a lookup relationship to the Invoice. UC would like to convert the lookup relationship to a master-detail relationship but is unable to do so.
Which two reasons could be preventing this relationship conversion? (Choose 2 answers)


Universal Containers (UC) 有一個自訂的「發票 (Invoice)」物件和一個自訂的「發票明細 (Invoice Line Item)」物件。「發票明細」物件上有一條到「發票」的查詢關係。UC 希望將這條查詢關係轉換為主從式關係，但無法成功。
哪兩個原因可能會阻止此關係的轉換？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Custom objects are unable to be on the detail side of a master-detail relationship.
     

自訂物件不能位於主從式關係的明細端。

B. There are already two master-detail relationships on the Invoice Line Item.
     

「發票明細」上已經有兩個主從式關係。

C. Invoice Line-Item records exist without having the Invoice lookup field populated.
     

存在沒有填入「發票」查詢欄位的「發票明細」記錄。

D. There is a roll-up summary field on the Invoice object.
     

「發票」物件上存在一個總計欄位。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C

詳解 (Explanation):
The two reasons that could be preventing this relationship conversion are that there are already two master-detail relationships on the Invoice Line Item and that Invoice Line Item records exist without having the Invoice lookup field populated. A custom object can have up to two master-detail relationships. Also, a master-detail relationship requires that the detail records have a value in the master lookup field.

將查詢關係轉換為主從式關係有幾個關鍵的先決條件：

C. 子記錄必須都有父記錄：在轉換前，所有現存的「發票明細」記錄都必須在其「發票」查詢欄位中填有值。主從式關係不允許子記錄沒有父記錄。

B. 子物件的主從關係數量限制：一個物件最多只能作為兩個不同主從式關係中的「明細 (Detail)」端。如果「發票明細」物件已經是另外兩個主從式關係的子物件，就不能再新增第三個。


【第一百八十八題 / NO. 188】


An app builder is creating a Lightning record page and has added Mobile & Lightning Actions to the page layout.
What two components could be included on the layout to display the actions? (Choose 2 answers)


一位應用程式建構者正在建立一個 Lightning 記錄頁面，並已將「行動與 Lightning 動作」新增到頁面版面配置中。
可以在版面配置中包含哪兩個元件來顯示這些動作？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Highlights panel
     

醒目提示面板

B. Chatter

C. Activities
     

活動

D. Path
     

路徑

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C

詳解 (Explanation):
To display the actions on the Lightning record page, two components could be included on the layout: Highlights panel: The highlights panel displays key information and actions for a record... Users can see and perform actions such as edit, clone, delete, etc. from the highlights panel. Activities: The activities component displays tasks and events related to a record. Users can also create new tasks and events, log calls, send emails...from this component.

在頁面版面配置的「行動與 Lightning 動作」區塊中定義的動作，會出現在 Lightning 記錄頁面的特定元件中：

A. 醒目提示面板 (Highlights Panel)：這個通常位於頁面頂部的元件會顯示記錄的關鍵欄位和主要的動作按鈕（如編輯、刪除以及您自訂的動作）。

C. 活動 (Activities)：這個元件用於顯示和建立工作、事件、記錄通話和傳送電子郵件。相關的動作（如「新增工作」、「記錄通話」）會顯示在此元件的索引標籤中。


【第一百八十九題 / NO. 189】


Cloud Kicks wants to efficiently increase the company's adoption of Salesforce while simultaneously moving away from their reliance on spreadsheets. An app builder is given a spreadsheet everyone is sharing that needs to be added to Salesforce. The object with fields needs to be created and the data inserted simultaneously.
Which tool should be used?


Cloud Kicks 希望有效提高公司對 Salesforce 的採用率，同時擺脫對試算表的依賴。一位應用程式建構者拿到了一個大家正在共用的試算表，需要將其新增到 Salesforce 中。需要同時建立帶有欄位的物件並插入資料。
應該使用哪種工具？

A. Import Wizard
     

匯入精靈

B. Lightning Object Creator
     

Lightning 物件建立器

C. Data Loader

D. Schema Builder
     

結構描述產生器

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
Lightning Object Creator is a tool that allows app builders to create an object with fields and import data from a spreadsheet simultaneously. It reads the column headers of the spreadsheet to suggest fields and data types for the new custom object and then imports the data from the file.

應使用「Lightning 物件建立器 (Lightning Object Creator)」。這個工具的特定用途就是讓您上傳一個試算表（如 .csv 或 .xlsx 檔案），它會自動讀取欄位標題來建議新自訂物件的欄位名稱和資料類型，並在建立物件的同時，將試算表中的資料匯入為記錄。這完美地滿足了「同時建立物件和插入資料」的需求。

【第一百九十題 / NO. 190】


An app builder received a request to extend record access beyond the organization-wide defaults configured.
Which two features satisfy this requirement? (Choose 2 answers)


一位應用程式建構者收到一個請求，需要將記錄的存取權限擴展到已設定的全組織預設值之外。
哪兩個功能可以滿足此需求？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Sharing Rules
     

共用規則

B. Public Groups
     

公開群組

C. Permission Set Groups
     

權限集群組

D. Manual Sharing Rules
     

手動共用規則

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, D

詳解 (Explanation):
Sharing rules and manual sharing are two features that can extend record access beyond the organization-wide defaults. Sharing rules are automatic rules that grant access to groups of users based on certain criteria. Manual sharing is a manual way of granting access to individual users or groups by the record owner. Public Groups are used by sharing rules, they are not a sharing mechanism themselves.

當 OWD（全組織預設值）設定得比較嚴格時（例如 Private），有幾種方法可以「擴展」或「開放」記錄的存取權限：

A. 共用規則 (Sharing Rules)：這是一種自動化的方式，根據記錄的負責人或記錄上的欄位值，將存取權限授予特定的公開群組、角色或區域。

D. 手動共用 (Manual Sharing)：這允許記錄的負責人或具有足夠權限的使用者，在個案基礎上，手動將單筆記錄的存取權限分享給其他使用者或群組。
公開群組 (B) 本身不是共用機制，而是共用規則所作用的對象。權限集群組 (C) 則是用於捆綁權限集，與記錄級別的共用無關。


【第一百九十一題 / NO. 191】


The CRM Manager at Universal Containers has requested that a custom text field be converted to a picklist in order to promote better data hygiene.
What needs to be considered before changing the field type? (Choose 2 answers)


Universal Containers 的 CRM 經理要求將一個自訂的文字欄位轉換為選項清單，以促進更好的資料衛生。
在更改欄位類型之前，需要考慮什麼？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Existing list views that reference the field may be deleted.
     

引用該欄位的現有清單檢視可能會被刪除。

B. Field references will be removed in Visualforce pages
     

Visualforce 頁面中的欄位引用將被移除。

C. All data should be backed up before converting a text field.
     

在轉換文字欄位之前，應備份所有資料。

D. Changing a field type will remove existing field history.
     

更改欄位類型將會移除現有的欄位歷史記錄。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C, D

詳解 (Explanation):
All data should be backed up before converting a text field to a picklist, as some data may be lost or truncated during the conversion. Any existing text values that do not exactly match one of the new picklist values will be lost. Changing a field type will remove existing field history, as the history tracking values are not converted.

在更改欄位類型時，有兩個重要的風險考量：

C. 備份資料：將文字欄位轉換為選項清單時，任何現有的文字值如果無法完全匹配您定義的選項清單值之一，這些資料將會遺失。因此，在進行任何可能導致資料遺失的操作前，備份資料是至關重要的步驟。

D. 移除欄位歷史：當您更改一個欄位的資料類型時，該欄位所有已有的「欄位歷史追蹤」記錄都會被刪除，因為新舊資料類型不相容，歷史記錄無法保留。


【第一百九十二題 / NO. 192】


After a deal is closed, Cloud Kicks (CK) wants to assign a user as a customer service manager (CSM) in addition to the account owner and would like a new field to easily track and report which CSM is assigned to the Account.
Which solution should an app builder use for this request?


交易結束後，Cloud Kicks (CK) 除了帳戶負責人之外，還想指派一位使用者作為客戶服務經理 (CSM)，並希望有一個新欄位來輕鬆追蹤和報告哪個 CSM 被指派給了該帳戶。
應用程式建構者應使用哪種解決方案來滿足此請求？

A. Multi-select picklist field
     

多選選項清單欄位

B. Picklist field
     

選項清單欄位

C. Lookup field
     

查詢欄位

D. Text field
     

文字欄位

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
The solution that an app builder should use for this request is a lookup field. A lookup field is a type of relationship field that links two objects together and allows users to select a record from another object. The app builder can create a lookup field on the account object that references the user object.

為了將一個記錄（帳戶）與一個特定的使用者（CSM）關聯起來，應該使用「查詢欄位 (Lookup Field)」。可以在「帳戶」物件上建立一個新的查詢關係欄位，使其查詢的對象是「使用者 (User)」物件。這樣，使用者就可以在這個欄位中選擇任何一位有效的 Salesforce 使用者作為該帳戶的 CSM。

【第一百九十三題 / NO. 193】


Cloud Kicks is redefining its entire business process to convert the Manager Notes field from a long text area field. The goal is to encourage managers to be more concise in their comments and stay at 255 characters or less. There is preexisting information in the Manager Notes field that often is well beyond the character limit.
What would happen to any existing information if the app builder tries to convert a preexisting long text area field to text area?


Cloud Kicks 正在重新定義其整個業務流程，要將「經理備註」欄位從「長文字區域 (long text area)」轉換。目標是鼓勵經理們的評論更簡潔，並保持在 255 個字元或更少。 「經理備註」欄位中已有的資訊通常遠超過這個字元限制。
如果應用程式建構者嘗試將一個已有的長文字區域欄位轉換為文字區域，現有的資訊會發生什麼情況？
(註：文字區域 (Text Area) 預設長度為 255 字元)

A. Preexisting information will truncate to the first 255 characters.
     

已有的資訊將被截斷為前 255 個字元。

B. Preexisting information will remain even if it was over 255 characters.
     

已有的資訊將會保留，即使它超過了 255 個字元。

C. Preexisting information will cause an error message to pop up.
     

已有的資訊將導致彈出錯誤訊息。

D. Preexisting information in the field will be completely lost.
     

欄位中已有的資訊將完全遺失。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
If the app builder tries to convert a preexisting long text area field to text area, preexisting information will truncate to the first 255 characters. This means that any information beyond 255 characters will be lost. (Note: This contradicts the answer for question 61 in the same document, but this is the correct Salesforce behavior).

如果將一個長文字區域欄位轉換為標準的文字區域（長度限制為 255），那麼所有現有記錄中該欄位超過 255 個字元的部分都將被截斷 (truncate)，也就是說，只有前 255 個字元會被保留下來，其餘的將永久遺失。 (註：這個答案與同一份文件中第 61 題的答案相矛盾，但這個答案 A 才是在 Salesforce 中的正確行為)。

【第一百九十四題 / NO. 194】

DreamHouse Realty 要求，在其 House__c 自訂物件上，某些欄位（如 Asking_Price__c 和 Real_Estate_Agent__c）的值變更需要顯著地顯示在 Chatter 上。

A. Thanks
     

感謝

B. Publisher Actions
     

發佈器動作

C. Topics
     

主題

D. Feed Tracking
     

動態追蹤

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
Feed Tracking is the Chatter feature that allows field value changes for certain fields to show up on Chatter.

應利用「動態追蹤 (Feed Tracking)」。這個功能允許您為一個物件選擇最多 20 個欄位進行追蹤。一旦啟用，每當這些被追蹤的欄位的值發生變更並儲存時，系統就會自動在該記錄的 Chatter 動態中發布一則貼文，說明欄位的舊值和新值。

【第一百九十五題 / NO. 195】


An app builder created multiple custom fields, page layouts, and reports in the sandbox and added them to a change set. After the change set was deployed to production, the reports were NOT deployed.
What should the app builder do?


一位應用程式建構者在沙箱中建立了多個自訂欄位、頁面版面配置和報告，並將它們新增到一個變更集中。變更集部署到生產環境後，報告卻沒有被部署。
建構者應該怎麼做？

A. Move the reports to the Unfiled Public Reports folder and add them to a new change set.
     

將報告移動到「未歸檔的公開報告」資料夾，並將它們新增到一個新的變更集中。

B. Move the reports from the Unfiled Public Reports folder and add them to a new change set
     

將報告從「未歸檔的公開報告」資料夾中移出，並將它們新增到一個新的變更集中。

C. Recreate the reports in production. Reports are not supported in change sets
     

在生產環境中重新建立報告。變更集不支援報告。

D. Add the reports to an unmanaged package and install the unmanaged package into production.
     

將報告新增到一個未管理封裝中，並將該封裝安裝到生產環境。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
Moving the reports from the Unfiled Public Reports folder and adding them to a new change set is what the app builder should do. According to the Salesforce documentation, "Reports in the Unfiled Public Reports folder aren't available for deployment."

建構者應該將報告從「未歸檔的公開報告 (Unfiled Public Reports)」資料夾中移出。Salesforce 的一個限制是，存放在這個預設資料夾中的報告和儀表板不能透過變更集進行部署。您必須先將報告儲存到一個自訂的或其他的公開資料夾中，然後才能將它們成功地新增到變更集並進行部署。

【第一百九十六題 / NO. 196】


Universal Containers uses a custom object called Reviews to capture information generated by interviewers during the candidate process. The Review records are visible to any user that has access to the related custom Candidate record. The VP of Human Resources wants the comment field on the Review to be private to anyone outside of the HR department.
How should the app builder meet this requirement?


Universal Containers 使用一個名為 Reviews 的自訂物件來擷取面試官在候選人流程中產生的資訊。任何有權限存取相關自訂「候選人 (Candidate)」記錄的使用者都可以看到 Review 記錄。人力資源副總希望 Review 上的「評論」欄位對人力資源部門以外的任何人都設為私有。
應用程式建構者應如何滿足此需求？

A. Create a page layout with the field and use field-level security to hide the field from all other users.
     

建立一個帶有該欄位的頁面版面配置，並使用欄位級別安全性向所有其他使用者隱藏該欄位。

B. Create an Apex sharing rule to share the field with users that have "HR" in their role.
     

建立一個 Apex 共用規則，將該欄位與角色中帶有 "HR" 的使用者共用。

C. Create a sharing rule to share the field with the VP of HR with Role and Subordinates.
     

建立一個共用規則，將該欄位與人資副總及其部屬共用。

D. Create a page layout with the field for HR users and another page layout without the field for all other users.
     

為 HR 使用者建立一個帶有該欄位的頁面版面配置，並為所有其他使用者建立另一個不帶該欄位的頁面版面配置。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
Create a page layout with the field and use field-level security to hide the field from all other users is how the app builder should meet the requirement. Field-level security can control which profiles can view or edit a field on a record. While using different page layouts (D) can hide the field from the UI, FLS is the true security control that prevents access via reports, API, etc.

滿足此需求的最佳方法是結合使用頁面版面配置和「欄位級別安全性 (Field-Level Security, FLS)」。
FLS：這是最根本的安全控制。應編輯非 HR 部門使用者的設定檔 (Profile) 或為他們建立一個權限集，將「評論」欄位的 FLS 設為「不可見 (Not Visible)」。這樣可以確保他們無論透過何種方式（UI、報告、API）都無法存取該欄位的資料。
頁面版面配置：同時，可以為 HR 和非 HR 使用者指派不同的頁面版面配置，在非 HR 使用者的版面配置中直接移除該欄位，以提供更乾淨的介面。
選項 A 提到了 FLS，這是最關鍵的步驟。

【第一百九十七題 / NO. 197】


Cloud Kicks has leads owned by users and queues. The sales manager wants the status to change to working when a user takes ownership.
What does an app builder need to have in the criteria to ensure the process runs without error?


Cloud Kicks 的潛在客戶由使用者和佇列擁有。銷售經理希望當「使用者」取得所有權時，狀態能變更為「處理中 (working)」。
應用程式建構者需要在條件中加入什麼來確保流程運行無誤？
(註：此題的題庫答案 D 與最佳實踐 A 有出入，我們依題庫答案解釋。)

A. BEGINS ([Lead].OwnerId, "005")

B. [Lead].Owner:User.Role.Id Is Null = False

C. [Lead].Owner:Queue.OwnerId Is Null = True

D. NOT(ISBLANK([Lead].OwnerId))


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D (根據題庫)

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder needs to have NOT(ISBLANK([Lead].OwnerId)) in the criteria to ensure the process runs without error. This formula checks if the OwnerId field on the Lead object is not blank, which means that the lead is owned by a user or a queue. This will prevent the process from running on leads that are not owned by anyone, which could cause an error. (Note: The best practice to distinguish a user owner from a queue owner is to use option A, as User IDs start with '005' and Queue IDs start with '00G'. The provided answer D is too broad but is what the source material indicates).

根據題庫答案的解釋：題庫的解釋是，為了防止流程在沒有負責人的潛在客戶上運行而出錯，需要在條件中加入 NOT(ISBLANK([Lead].OwnerId))，以確保該記錄至少有一個負責人（無論是使用者還是佇列）。
根據 Salesforce 最佳實踐的解釋：題目的要求是「當使用者取得所有權時」。Salesforce 中，使用者 ID 的前三碼是 005，而佇列 ID 的前三碼是 00G。因此，要精確地判斷負責人是否為使用者，最正確的條件應該是選項 A，BEGINS([Lead].OwnerId, "005")。題庫的答案 D 過於寬泛，不完全符合業務需求。

【第一百九十八題 / NO. 198】


DreamHouse Realty wants to make sure an Opportunity has a field Expected_Close_Date__c populated before it is allowed to enter the qualified stage.
How should an app builder solution this request?


DreamHouse Realty 希望確保一個機會在被允許進入「合格 (qualified)」階段之前，其 Expected_Close_Date__c 欄位已被填寫。
應用程式建構者應如何解決此請求？

A. Record Type
     

記錄類型

B. Validation Rule
     

驗證規則

C. Activity History
     

活動歷史

D. Page Layout
     

頁面版面配置

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
A validation rule is a formula that evaluates the data... and returns a value of "True" or "False". Validation rules verify that the data a user enters... meets the standards you specify before the user can save the record. In this case, a validation rule can be used to check if the Expected_Close_Date__c field is populated before the Opportunity stage is set to qualified.

應使用「驗證規則 (Validation Rule)」。可以建立一條驗證規則，其「錯誤條件公式」如下：
AND( ISPICKVAL(StageName, "Qualified"), ISBLANK(Expected_Close_Date__c) )
這條規則的含義是：如果「階段」被設為 "Qualified" 而且 Expected_Close_Date__c 欄位是空白的，則觸發錯誤，阻止記錄儲存，並顯示您設定的錯誤訊息。

【第一百九十九題 / NO. 199】


Which three options are available when activating a Lightning page from the Lightning App Builder? (Choose 3 answers)


從 Lightning 應用程式建構器啟用一個 Lightning 頁面時，哪三個選項是可用的？(選擇 3 個答案)

A. Assign the page to a combination of apps and profiles.
     

將頁面指派給應用程式和設定檔的組合。

B. Assign the page to a combination of apps and permission sets.
     

將頁面指派給應用程式和權限集的組合。

C. Make the page the org default.
     

將頁面設為組織預設。

D. Make the page the default homepage for specific roles.
     

將頁面設為特定角色的預設首頁。

E. Make the page the default homepage for specific apps.
     

將頁面設為特定應用程式的預設首頁。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C, E

詳解 (Explanation):
When activating a Lightning page from the Lightning App Builder, three options are available:

A. Assign the page to a combination of apps and profiles.

C. Make the page the org default.

E. Make the page the default for specific apps. (For record pages, you can also assign by record type).

在啟用一個 Lightning 頁面（例如首頁或記錄頁面）時，系統會提供幾個指派選項：

C. 設為組織預設 (Org Default)：將此頁面作為整個組織的預設頁面。

E. 設為應用程式預設 (App Default)：將此頁面作為一個或多個特定應用程式的預設頁面。

A. 指派給應用程式、記錄類型和設定檔的組合：這是最精細的控制，可以指定此頁面只對某個應用程式中的、具有某個設定檔的、查看某種記錄類型的使用者顯示。


【第二百題 / NO. 200】


Universal Containers has a private sharing model for Accounts and Opportunities and uses Territory Management to grant access to records.
Sales rep A manually shares an opportunity record with sales rep В.
Sales rep B has access to the Account even though the Account is NOT in sales rep B's territory.
Sales rep C CANNOT see either record.
Based on the information given, why can sales rep B see the Account related to the Opportunity?


Universal Containers 對帳戶和機會使用私人共用模型，並使用區域管理來授予記錄存取權。
銷售代表 A 手動將一筆機會記錄與銷售代表 B 共用。
銷售代表 B 能夠存取該帳戶，即使該帳戶不在銷售代表 B 的區域內。
銷售代表 C 無法看到這兩筆記錄中的任何一筆。
根據給定的資訊，為什麼銷售代表 B 能夠看到與該機會相關的帳戶？

A. Sales rep B has implicit access to the Account.
     

銷售代表 B 對該帳戶有隱含的存取權。

B. Sales rep B was added to the Account team.
     

銷售代表 B 被新增到了帳戶團隊。

C. Sharing set is granting access to the Account.
     

共用集正在授予對該帳戶的存取權。

D. Account was also manually shared.
     

帳戶也被手動共用了。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
Sales rep B has implicit access to the Account because of the manual sharing of the Opportunity. Implicit sharing grants access to parent records when a user has access to a child record. Because Rep B was given access to the child Opportunity, they implicitly gain read-only access to the parent Account record.

這是因為「隱含共用 (Implicit Sharing)」。在 Salesforce 的共用模型中，當使用者被授予對子記錄（如機會、個案、連絡人）的存取權限時，他們會自動獲得對其父層「帳戶」記錄的唯讀存取權限。因為銷售代表 B 被手動分享了「機會」記錄，所以他隱含地獲得了查看相關「帳戶」的權限。

【第二百零一題 / NO. 201】


Universal Containers has a customer base where many customers have the same or similar company names.
Which functionality should be configured to improve an end user's search experience? (Choose 2 answers)


Universal Containers 的客戶群中，許多客戶的公司名稱相同或相似。
應設定哪個功能來改善使用者的搜尋體驗？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Update the account search layout's view filter settings.
     

更新帳戶搜尋版面配置的檢視篩選器設定。

B. Update the account search layout's search results columns displayed.
     

更新帳戶搜尋版面配置中顯示的搜尋結果欄位。

C. Update the account search filter fields.
     

更新帳戶搜尋篩選欄位。

D. Update the account search layout's accounts tab columns displayed.
     

更新帳戶搜尋版面配置中帳戶索引標籤顯示的欄位。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C

詳解 (Explanation):
Updating the account search layouts search results columns displayed and updating the account search filter fields can improve an end user's search experience by showing more relevant information and allowing more refined filtering.

當名稱相似時，為了幫助使用者區分，可以進行以下設定：

B. 更新搜尋結果顯示的欄位：在「搜尋版面配置 (Search Layouts)」中，可以自訂「搜尋結果」中顯示的欄位。除了名稱之外，可以增加其他有區別性的欄位，如「帳單城市」、「電話」或「帳戶負責人」，讓使用者在搜尋結果頁面就能直接區分不同的帳戶。

C. 更新搜尋篩選欄位：可以設定在全域搜尋結果頁面的左側顯示哪些欄位作為「篩選器」。這樣使用者可以用其他條件（如產業、區域）來縮小搜尋範圍，更快找到目標。


【第二百零二題 / NO. 202】


Sales reps at Universal Containers create multiple quotes per opportunity.
What automation tool should an app builder recommend to delete rejected quotes?


Universal Containers 的銷售代表會為每個機會建立多個報價。應用程式建構者應推薦哪種自動化工具來刪除被拒絕的報價？

A. Approval process
     

批准流程

B. Validation rule
     

驗證規則

C. Workflow rule
     

工作流程規則

D. Flow


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
A flow is a powerful automation tool that can perform complex logic and data manipulation. A flow can be used to delete rejected quotes by using a record-triggered flow that runs when a quote is updated. Workflow Rules and Process Builder cannot delete records.

應推薦使用 Flow。因為這個需求的核心動作是「刪除記錄」。在 Salesforce 的宣告式自動化工具中，只有 Flow 具備「刪除記錄 (Delete Records)」的功能。您可以建立一個在「報價」記錄更新時觸發的流程，當報價的狀態變為「已拒絕」時，流程就執行刪除該筆報價記錄的動作。工作流程規則和 Process Builder 都無法刪除記錄。

【第二百零三題 / NO. 203】


Cloud Kicks (CK) wants to simultaneously delete a Supplier's record and all Supplier_Item__c records if a partnership ends with a supplier.
What solution could an app builder use to meet the requirement?


如果與供應商的合作關係結束，Cloud Kicks (CK) 希望能同時刪除該供應商的記錄以及所有相關的 Supplier_Item__c 記錄。
應用程式建構者可以使用哪種解決方案來滿足此需求？

A. Many-to-many
     

多對多

B. Indirect lookup
     

間接查詢

C. Hierarchical
     

階層

D. Master-detail
     

主從式

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
The solution that an app builder should use to meet this requirement is master-detail relationship. A master-detail relationship is a type of relationship that creates a parent-child relationship... when a Supplier__c record is deleted, all related SupplierItem__c records are also deleted automatically. This is called cascade delete.

應使用「主從式 (Master-detail)」關係。主從式關係的一個核心特性就是「級聯刪除 (cascade delete)」，即當主記錄 (Master) 被刪除時，其所有相關的明細記錄 (Detail) 都會被自動一併刪除。這完美地符合了「同時刪除供應商和其所有相關項目」的需求。

【第二百零四題 / NO. 204】


The convert button on leads should NOT appear until the lead status picklist is set to qualified.
What should an app builder suggest to meet these requirements?


潛在客戶上的「轉換」按鈕，在潛在客戶狀態選項清單被設為「合格 (qualified)」之前，不應該出現。
應用程式建構者應建議什麼方案來滿足這些需求？

A. Picklist dependency, page layouts, record types
     

選項清單相依性、頁面版面配置、記錄類型

B. Custom button, validation rule, record types
     

自訂按鈕、驗證規則、記錄類型

C. Process builder field update, quick action, record type
     

Process Builder 欄位更新、快速動作、記錄類型

D. Page layout, record types, process builder field update
     

頁面版面配置、記錄類型、Process Builder 欄位更新

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B (註：此答案的組合較為複雜，更現代的作法是使用動態表單/動作。此處依題庫答案。)

詳解 (Explanation):
A custom button, a validation rule, and record types can be used to meet the requirement of hiding the convert button on leads until the lead status picklist is set to qualified. The approach would be: use record types and page layouts to show/hide the button, and a validation rule to enforce the status logic.

這是一個組合解決方案：
記錄類型 (Record Types) 和頁面版面配置：建立至少兩個潛在客戶記錄類型，例如「未合格」和「已合格」。為它們指派不同的頁面版面配置。在「未合格」的版面配置中，移除標準的「轉換」按鈕。在「已合格」的版面配置中保留該按鈕。
自動化 (未在選項中明說，但為必要步驟)：建立一個 Flow，當潛在客戶的狀態變為「合格」時，自動將其記錄類型從「未合格」更改為「已合格」，這樣頁面就會刷新並顯示「轉換」按鈕。
驗證規則 (Validation Rule)：可以作為一個輔助措施，防止使用者在不滿足某些條件的情況下將狀態改為「合格」。
選項 B 包含了其中的關鍵元素。

【第二百零五題 / NO. 205】


Universal Containers would like to embed a chart of all related Opportunities, by stage, on the Account detail page.

   ˆ

一個關於「帳戶」物件的表格式報告。

D. A tabular report on the Opportunity object.
     

一個關於「機會」物件的表格式報告。

A summary report on the opportunity object should be created to add to the account page layout. The report must be based on Opportunities and grouped by Stage to create the required chart.

為了在頁面上嵌入圖表，您必須先建立一個包含圖表的報告。只有「摘要 (Summary)」和「矩陣 (Matrix)」類型的報告才能新增圖表。因為需求是按「階段」來劃分「機會」，所以報告必須是：
基於「機會」物件。
報告類型為「摘要報告」。

【第二百零六題 / NO. 206】


Universal Containers created a 'New Task' custom action on the Opportunity object. The action was added to all page layouts in the Mobile & Lightning Actions section.
Which Lightning component should the app builder add to the layout to display the action?


Universal Containers 在「機會」物件上建立了一個「新增工作」的自訂動作。該動作已被新增到所有頁面版面配置的「行動與 Lightning 動作」區塊中。
