【第二百零七題 / NO. 207】


An app builder has deployed a change set from a sandbox to production. There is a long delay in the deployment.
What can be causing the delay?


一位應用程式建構者從沙箱部署了一個變更集到生產環境。部署過程中有很長的延遲。
可能導致延遲的原因是什麼？

A. Profiles are included in the change set.
     

變更集中包含了設定檔。

B. A field type change is included in the change set.
     

變更集中包含了一個欄位類型變更。

C. Dependent fields are included in the change set.
     

變更集中包含了相依欄位。

D. Roles are included in the change set.
     

變更集中包含了角色。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
A field type change is included in the change set and that it can cause a delay in the deployment. A field type change is a change that modifies the data type of an existing field... A field type change can affect many aspects of Salesforce functionality... Therefore, deploying a change set that contains a field type change can take longer than usual.

部署緩慢的一個常見原因是變更集中包含了「欄位類型變更」。更改一個現有欄位的資料類型（例如，從文字變為數字）是一項破壞性變更，Salesforce 需要在後台執行大量的檢查，以確保這個變更不會破壞任何相依的自動化、程式碼、報告等。如果該欄位包含大量資料，系統可能還需要進行資料轉換，這些都會導致部署時間顯著延長。

【第二百零八題 / NO. 208】


An app builder wants to create a custom Sync button on Account that will call a Lightning Web Component that connects with an external system. This action should only be available if the custom Status field is set to Ready to Sync.
What should an app builder use to add this functionality to an Account record page?


一位應用程式建構者希望在「帳戶」上建立一個自訂的「同步 (Sync)」按鈕，該按鈕將呼叫一個與外部系統連接的 Lightning Web 元件。此動作應僅在自訂的「狀態」欄位被設為 Ready to Sync 時才可用。
應用程式建構者應使用什麼來將此功能新增到帳戶記錄頁面？

A. Formula field
     

公式欄位

B. Dynamic action
     

動態動作

C. AppExchange product
     

AppExchange 產品

D. Custom link
     

自訂連結

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
Dynamic actions are a feature that allow app builders to create custom buttons or actions that can call Lightning Web Components and display them conditionally based on field values or other criteria.

應使用「動態動作 (Dynamic Action)」。這是 Lightning 應用程式建構器的一項功能，它完美地滿足了所有需求：
可以建立一個呼叫 LWC 的快速動作。
在 Lightning 記錄頁面上，可以將這個動作設定為動態動作。
可以為該動作設定「可見度篩選條件」，例如「狀態 等於 Ready to Sync」。
這樣，按鈕就只會在滿足條件時才會顯示。

【第二百零九題 / NO. 209】


The Recruiting team at AW Computing captures the job acceptance and date of hire of a candidate on the Job Application custom object. Once the candidate accepts the recruiter's job offer, the date of hire should be entered and not be changed on subsequent record edits.
Which validation formula should the app builder use?


AW Computing 的招聘團隊在「工作申請」自訂物件上記錄候選人的工作接受情況和雇用日期。一旦候選人接受了招聘人員的工作錄用，就應該輸入雇用日期，並且在後續的記錄編輯中不應再被更改。
應用程式建構者應使用哪個驗證公式？

A. NOT(ISBLANK(Job_Accepted__c)) && ISCHANGED(Hire_Date__c)

B. (ISBLANK(Job_Accepted__c) || NOT (ISCHANGED(Hire_Date__c)))

C. NOT(ISBLANK(Job_Accepted__c)) || ISCHANGED (Hire_Date__c)

D. (ISBLANK(Job_Accepted__c) && NOT (ISCHANGED(Hire_Date__c)))


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A (註：此公式有瑕疵，更完整的公式應為 AND( ISCHANGED(Hire_Date__c), NOT(ISBLANK(PRIORVALUE(Hire_Date__c))) )，但 A 是選項中最接近的。)

詳解 (Explanation):
NOT(ISBLANK(Job_Accepted__c)) && ISCHANGED (Hire_Date__c) is the validation formula that the app builder should use to meet the requirement of preventing changes to Hire Date after Job Accepted is entered. This formula will return TRUE if Job Accepted is not blank and Hire Date is changed, which will display an error message.

驗證規則的目的是定義「錯誤條件」。錯誤的條件是：「工作已被接受」並且「雇用日期正在被更改」。
NOT(ISBLANK(Job_Accepted__c)): 檢查「工作接受」欄位是否不為空。
ISCHANGED(Hire_Date__c): 檢查「雇用日期」欄位是否在此次編輯中被更改。
AND 函數將兩者結合，表示只有當兩個條件同時滿足時，驗證才會失敗。這符合了「一旦接受，雇用日期就不能再改」的需求。 （這個公式的瑕疵在於，如果使用者在同一次編輯中同時勾選「接受」並填寫「雇用日期」，也會被阻止。更好的作法是使用 PRIORVALUE 函數）。

【第二百一十題 / NO. 210】


An app builder needs to create new automation on an object.
What best practice should the app builder follow when building out automation?


一位應用程式建構者需要在一個物件上建立新的自動化。
在建構自動化時，建構者應遵循什麼最佳實踐？

A. One Workflow rule per object.
     

每個物件一個工作流程規則。

B. One Flow per object.
     

每個物件一個 Flow。

C. One invocable process per object.
     

每個物件一個可叫用的流程。

D. One record change process per object.
     

每個物件一個記錄變更流程。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
The best practice that the app builder should follow when building out automation is one record change process per object. A record change process is a type of process in Process Builder that starts when a record is created or updated. Having one record change process per object can avoid conflicts or errors when multiple processes try to update the same record at the same time and helps control the order of execution.

應遵循「每個物件一個記錄變更流程」的最佳實踐。這裡的「記錄變更流程 (record change process)」特指由記錄的建立或更新所觸發的自動化流程（在 Process Builder 時代的術語）。Salesforce 推薦這樣做的主要原因是，當您有多個自動化流程作用於同一個物件時，您無法保證它們的執行順序，這可能導致遞迴錯誤和意外的結果。將所有邏輯合併到一個流程中，並使用不同的條件節點來處理不同的業務場景，可以讓您更好地控制執行順序，也更易於除錯和維護。這個原則現在同樣適用於 Record-Triggered Flow。

【第二百一十一題 / NO. 211】


Universal Containers has a custom picklist called Support_Level__c on the Account object. They would like to show the real-time value of Support_Level__c on all case records.
How should an app builder implement this requirement?


Universal Containers 在「帳戶」物件上有一個名為 Support_Level__c 的自訂選項清單。他們希望在所有「個案」記錄上即時顯示 Support_Level__c 的值。
應用程式建構者應如何實現此需求？

A. Create a formula field on the Case object using the TEXT function.
     

在「個案」物件上使用 TEXT 函數建立一個公式欄位。

B. Create a formula field on the Account object using the ISPICKVAL function.
     

在「帳戶」物件上使用 ISPICKVAL 函數建立一個公式欄位。

C. Create a Process Builder and use a field update on the Case object.
     

建立一個 Process Builder 並在「個案」物件上使用欄位更新。

D. Create a roll-up summary field using Support Level on the Account object.
     

在「帳戶」物件上使用「支援等級」建立一個總計欄位。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
Create a formula field on the Case object using the TEXT function. This is correct because a formula field can reference a field from a related object using dot notation, and the TEXT function can convert a picklist value to text. This way, the case record will always show the current value of the Support_Level__c field on the account record.

最佳方法是在「個案」物件上建立一個「跨物件公式欄位」。因為父物件 (Account) 的欄位是選項清單，所以在子物件 (Case) 的公式欄位中需要使用 TEXT() 函數將其轉換為文字來顯示。公式可以寫成 TEXT(Account.Support_Level__c)。這樣能確保個案上記錄的值永遠與其關聯帳戶的最新值保持即時同步。

【第二百一十二題 / NO. 212】


Cloud Kicks has created a custom object called Interests which is joined to Accounts by way of a junction object called Account_Interest__c.
What is the impact to users attempting to view an Account and the associated Account_Interest__c records if they are without read access to the Interests object?


Cloud Kicks 建立了一個名為 Interests 的自訂物件，該物件透過一個名為 Account_Interest__c 的連接物件與「帳戶」相連。
如果使用者對 Interests 物件沒有讀取權限，他們在嘗試檢視一個帳戶及其關聯的 Account_Interest__c 記錄時會受到什麼影響？

A. Users will be able to view the Account_Interest__c records and will have read-only access to the Interests records.
     

使用者將能夠檢視 Account_Interest__c 記錄，並對 Interests 記錄有唯讀存取權。

B. Users will be unable to view Account records that have a related Account_Interest__c record.
     

使用者將無法檢視有相關 Account_Interest__c 記錄的帳戶記錄。

C. Users will be unable to view the Account_Interest__c records or the Interests records.
     

使用者將無法檢視 Account_Interest__c 記錄或 Interests 記錄。

D. Users will be able to view the Account_Interest__c record, but unable to view the field or any information relating back to the Interests record.
     

使用者將能夠檢視 Account_Interest__c 記錄，但無法檢視與 Interests 記錄相關的欄位或任何資訊。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
Users will be unable to view the Account_Interest__c records or the Interests records because they do not have read access to the Interests object. This is a standard behavior of Salesforce when a user does not have access to a related object. In a many-to-many relationship, access to the junction object record requires access to both master records.

使用者將無法檢視 Account_Interest__c 記錄或 Interests 記錄。在多對多關係中，連接物件的記錄可見性取決於使用者是否對其兩個主記錄都有存取權限。因為使用者對 Interests 物件（其中一個主物件）沒有讀取權限，所以他們不僅看不到 Interests 記錄本身，也看不到任何與 Interests 記錄相關的 Account_Interest__c 連接物件記錄。

【第二百一十三題 / NO. 213】


Universal Containers generates leads from three different sources: web, trade shows, and partners. Some of the information collected is applicable to all sources, there is also information that is unique to each type of lead.
What should an app builder configure to meet these requirements?


Universal Containers 從三個不同來源產生潛在客戶：網站、商展和合作夥伴。收集的部分資訊適用於所有來源，但也有一些資訊是每種類型潛在客戶所獨有的。
應用程式建構者應如何設定來滿足這些需求？

A. Create three lead record types each with its own page layout containing the relevant fields
     

建立三種潛在客戶記錄類型，每種類型都有其自己的、包含相關欄位的頁面版面配置。

B. Create a partner community and a record type for web and trade show leads
     

建立一個合作夥伴社群以及一個用於網站和商展潛在客戶的記錄類型。

C. Create three sections on the lead layout and instruct users to collapse the non-relevant fields
     

在潛在客戶版面配置上建立三個區段，並指示使用者收合不相關的欄位。

D. Create custom page layouts for each type of lead only containing the relevant fields
     

為每種類型的潛在客戶建立僅包含相關欄位的自訂頁面版面配置。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The solution that the app builder should configure to meet these requirements is creating three lead record types each with its own page layout containing the relevant fields. This way, the app builder can customize the fields and sections that appear on each record type based on the source of the lead.

最佳解決方案是建立三種「記錄類型 (Record Types)」，分別對應網站、商展和合作夥伴。然後，為每種記錄類型指派一個專屬的「頁面版面配置 (Page Layout)」。這樣，您就可以在每個版面配置上只顯示該來源潛在客戶所需的通用欄位和獨有欄位，從而為使用者提供最相關、最簡潔的資料輸入介面。

【第二百一十四題 / NO. 214】


universal containers is migrating its sales operations from a legacy system that was used. opportunities need to be imported with the proper country currency.
Which two steps should an app builder configure to meet these requirements? (Choose 2 answers.)


Universal Containers 正在從一個舊系統遷移其銷售業務。機會需要以正確的國家貨幣匯入。
應用程式建構者應設定哪兩個步驟來滿足這些需求？(選擇 2 個答案。)

A. Include the currency ISO code in all currency fields in the import file.
     

在匯入檔案的所有貨幣欄位中包含貨幣 ISO 代碼。

B. Use Data Loader to import the records.
     

使用 Data Loader 匯入記錄。

C. Include the currency ISO Code Column in the import file.
     

在匯入檔案中包含貨幣 ISO 代碼欄。

D. Use import wizard to import the records.
     

使用匯入精靈匯入記錄。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C (註：題庫答案為 A, B，但 C 的描述更精確。此處依題庫答案解釋並補充。)

詳解 (Explanation):
To import opportunities with the proper country currency, the app builder needs to include the currency ISO code in the import file, and use Data Loader to import the records. Data Loader supports importing multiple currencies, while Import Wizard does not. The currency ISO code column in the import file specifies the currency for each record.

為了在啟用了多幣別的組織中匯入帶有不同貨幣的資料，需要：

B. 使用 Data Loader：Data Loader 支援多幣別資料的匯入，而匯入精靈 (Import Wizard) 不支援。

C. 在匯入檔案中包含貨幣 ISO 代碼欄：您的 CSV 檔案中必須有一欄專門用來存放每筆記錄的貨幣 ISO 代碼（例如 "USD", "EUR", "JPY"）。在 Data Loader 的欄位對應步驟中，將這一欄對應到 Salesforce 物件的 CurrencyIsoCode 欄位。
(註：選項 A 的描述「在所有貨幣欄位中包含」不精確，應該是新增一個獨立的欄位。)


【第二百一十五題 / NO. 215】


Cloud Kicks received a new requirement to calculate summaries from child objects of a standard object. The team would prefer to solve this declaratively.
What are two considerations an app builder should evaluate? (Choose 2 answers)


Cloud Kicks 收到一個新需求，需要從一個標準物件的子物件計算摘要。團隊希望以宣告式的方式解決此問題。
應用程式建構者應評估哪兩項考量因素？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. An app builder is unable to change a lookup to a master-detail relationship.
     

應用程式建構者無法將查詢關係更改為主從式關係。

B. An object can have up to two master-detail relationships.
     

一個物件最多可以有兩個主從式關係。

C. A trigger on save or update can kick off calculations.
     

儲存或更新時的觸發器可以啟動計算。

D. A value is required in all records of the lookup field prior to converting to a master-detail relationship.
     

在將查詢關係轉換為主從式關係之前，查詢欄位的所有記錄中都必須有值。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, D (註：題庫答案為 A, D，但 B, D 是更常見的考量。此處依題庫答案解釋並補充。)

詳解 (Explanation):
To calculate summaries declaratively, a Roll-Up Summary field is needed, which requires a Master-Detail relationship. The considerations for converting a lookup to a master-detail are: A value is required in all records of the lookup field prior to converting. And the object on the detail side can have a maximum of two master-detail relationships.

宣告式計算摘要通常指使用「總計欄位 (Roll-Up Summary Field)」，而這需要「主從式關係」。如果目前是查詢關係，就需要考慮轉換的可行性：

D. 查詢欄位必須都有值：這是轉換為 M-D 關係的硬性要求。因為 M-D 關係中的子記錄必須有父記錄，所以所有現存子記錄的查詢欄位都不能是空的。

B. 物件的主從關係數量限制：將要成為「明細 (Detail)」端的子物件，其身上最多只能有兩個 M-D 關係欄位。
(註：選項 A「無法更改」的說法太絕對，在滿足條件 D 的情況下是可以更改的，因此 A 是錯誤的。但題庫答案選了 A 和 D，可能是將 A 理解為「在不滿足條件的情況下無法更改」。)


【第二百一十六題 / NO. 216】


Universal Containers needs the 18-digit record ID from Opportunity records when exporting data to Excel in order to ensure each record is treated uniquely.
What formula should an app builder use to create this new field?


Universal Containers 在將資料匯出到 Excel 時，需要來自機會記錄的 18 位數記錄 ID，以確保每條記錄都被唯一對待。
應用程式建構者應使用哪個公式來建立這個新欄位？

A. ISNUMBER(Id)

B. CASESAFEID(Id)

C. TEXT(Id)

D. VALUE(Id)


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should use the CASESAFEID(Id) formula to create this new field. The CASESAFEID function returns the 18-digit case-insensitive version of the record ID, which is unique for each record in Salesforce. The 15-digit ID is case-sensitive and can cause issues in external systems like Excel that may not be case-sensitive.

應使用 CASESAFEID(Id) 公式。Salesforce 內部使用的 15 位數 ID 是區分大小寫的，而像 Excel 這樣的外部系統通常不區分大小寫，這可能導致資料處理時將不同的記錄誤認為是同一筆。CASESAFEID() 函數會將 15 位數的 ID 轉換為 18 位數、不區分大小寫的 ID，確保在任何系統中的唯一性。

【第二百一十七題 / NO. 217】


Universal Containers has a custom picklist called Support_Level__c on the Account object. They would like to show the real-time value of Support_Level__c on all case records.
How should an app builder implement this requirement?


Universal Containers 在「帳戶」物件上有一個名為 Support_Level__c 的自訂選項清單。他們希望在所有「個案」記錄上即時顯示 Support_Level__c 的值。
應用程式建構者應如何實現此需求？

A. Create a formula field on the Case object using the TEXT function.
     

在「個案」物件上使用 TEXT 函數建立一個公式欄位。

B. Create a formula field on the Account object using the ISPICKVAL function.
     

在「帳戶」物件上使用 ISPICKVAL 函數建立一個公式欄位。

C. Create a Process Builder and use a field update on the Case object.
     

建立一個 Process Builder 並在「個案」物件上使用欄位更新。

D. Create a roll-up summary field using Support Level on the Account object.
     

在「帳戶」物件上使用「支援等級」建立一個總計欄位。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The best way to implement this requirement is to create a formula field on the Case object using the TEXT function. A formula field can display the value of another field from a related object. The TEXT function can convert a picklist value into text, which can be displayed on the Case record.

最佳方法是在「個案」物件上建立一個「跨物件公式欄位」。因為父物件 (Account) 的欄位是選項清單，所以在子物件 (Case) 的公式欄位中需要使用 TEXT() 函數將其轉換為文字來顯示。公式可以寫成 TEXT(Account.Support_Level__c)。這樣能確保個案上記錄的值永遠與其關聯帳戶的最新值保持即時同步。

【第二百一十八題 / NO. 218】

應推薦使用「路徑 (Path)」。Path 功能專為引導使用者完成流程而設計。您可以在 Path 的每個階段設定「成功指引 (Guidance for Success)」，在其中可以放入說明文字、最佳實踐、政策連結、教學影片等，為使用者提供即時的、與當前階段相關的輔助資訊。

【第二百一十九題 / NO. 219】

DreamHouse Realty 正在建立一個自訂的 Lightning 應用程式來追蹤其不斷擴展的太陽能集水業務。該 Lightning 應用程式目前包含一個帶有標準元件的自訂 Lightning 記錄頁面。

C. Import Wizard

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

獲取自訂 Lightning 元件的主要來源有：

【第二百二十題 / NO. 220】


DreamHouse Realty (DR) has many properties for sale and wants to identify the highest value of all Offer__c records on each Property__c record.
What solution should the app builder use to meet DreamHouse Realty's needs?


DreamHouse Realty (DR) 有許多待售物業，並希望在每個 Property__c 記錄上識別出所有相關 Offer__c 記錄中的最高價值。
應用程式建構者應使用什麼解決方案來滿足 DR 的需求？

A. Master-Detail Child Object
     

主從式子物件

B. Text Area (Long)
     

長文字區域

C. Multi-select Picklist
     

多選選項清單

D. Lookup Object
     

查詢物件

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The solution that the app builder should use is Master-Detail Child Object. A master-detail relationship can be used to create a parent-child relationship between two objects... The app builder can create a roll-up summary field on the parent object (Property__c) to calculate the highest value (MAX) of all child records (Offer__c).

為了能夠在父物件 (Property__c) 上計算子物件 (Offer__c) 的摘要資訊（如最高價值），Offer__c 必須是「主從式關係」中的子物件。建立主從式關係後，就可以在 Property__c 物件上建立一個「總計欄位 (Roll-Up Summary Field)」，摘要類型選擇「最大值 (MAX)」，並選擇要計算的 Offer__c 上的金額欄位。

【第二百二十一題 / NO. 221】


At Ursa Major Solar, there is a single Lightning record page for the Celestial_Bodies__c custom object; however, there is a Lightning component the app builder wants to restrict to mobile app users.
Which feature on the Lightning app builder should be utilized?


在 Ursa Major Solar，Celestial_Bodies__c 自訂物件只有一個 Lightning 記錄頁面；然而，應用程式建構者希望將其中一個 Lightning 元件限制只給行動應用程式使用者看到。
應該利用 Lightning 應用程式建構器上的哪個功能？

A. Chatter feed
     

Chatter 動態

B. Highlights panel
     

醒目提示面板

C. Component visibility filter
     

元件可見度篩選器

D. Related list quick links
     

相關清單快速連結

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
Component visibility filter is the feature on the Lightning app builder that should be utilized to restrict a Lightning component to mobile app users. "Use component visibility filters to show or hide components on a record page based on field values or user profile." One of the available criteria is the device's form factor (Desktop or Phone).

應利用「元件可見度篩選器 (Component visibility filter)」。在 Lightning 應用程式建構器中，選中任何一個元件，都可以在右側的屬性面板中設定其可見度條件。其中一個篩選條件是「裝置 (Device)」，您可以設定該元件只在「裝置 等於 手機」時才顯示。

【第二百二十二題 / NO. 222】


Cloud Kicks (CK) is finding sales reps are inconsistent in data entry when deals are won. CK requires that custom shoes are shipped within two weeks after the close date. A custom field called Scheduled_Ship_Date__c on the opportunity records the ship date.
How should the app builder ensure this field is properly filled out before setting the opportunity to closed won?


Cloud Kicks (CK) 發現銷售代表在交易成交時的資料輸入不一致。CK 要求客製鞋必須在結束日期後的兩週內出貨。機會上一個名為 Scheduled_Ship_Date__c 的自訂欄位記錄了出貨日期。
應用程式建構者應如何確保在將機會設為「結案成交」之前，此欄位已被正確填寫？

A. OR(ISPICKVAL(StageName, "Closed Won") && (Scheduled_Ship_Date__c - CloseDate) > 14, ISBLANK(Scheduled_Ship_Date__c))

B. OR(ISPICKVAL(StageName = "Closed Won") && (Scheduled_Ship_Date__c - CloseDate) > 14, ISBLANK(Scheduled_Ship_Date__c))

C. ISPICKVAL(StageName, "Closed Won") && (Scheduled_Ship_Date__c - CloseDate) > 14

D. ISPICKVAL(StageName = "Closed Won") && (CloseDate - Scheduled_Ship_Date__c) > 14


點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The correct validation rule formula is OR(ISPICKVAL(StageName, "Closed Won") && (Scheduled_Ship_Date__c - CloseDate) > 14, ISBLANK(Scheduled_Ship_Date__c)). This formula checks two conditions: if the StageName is "Closed Won" and the Scheduled_Ship_Date__c is more than 14 days after the CloseDate, OR if the Scheduled_Ship_Date__c is blank when the stage is "Closed Won" (this part is implied but missing, the formula is not perfectly written). The intent is to ensure the date is filled and within the 14-day window. Option A is the closest syntactically correct formula to achieve parts of this logic.

這題需要一個驗證規則來定義錯誤條件。錯誤的條件有兩個，只要滿足其中一個就應該報錯：
當階段是 "Closed Won" 時，出貨日期不能是空的。
當階段是 "Closed Won" 時，出貨日期不能晚於結束日期 14 天以上。
選項 A 的公式 OR(ISPICKVAL(StageName, "Closed Won") && (Scheduled_Ship_Date__c - CloseDate) > 14, ISBLANK(Scheduled_Ship_Date__c)) 組合了這兩個條件。第一個部分檢查日期是否超過 14 天，第二個部分檢查日期是否為空。如果這兩個條件任一為真，驗證就會失敗。 (註：更精確的寫法應為 ISPICKVAL(StageName, "Closed Won") && ( OR( ISBLANK(Scheduled_Ship_Date__c), (Scheduled_Ship_Date__c - CloseDate) > 14 ) )，但選項 A 是最接近的答案)。

【第二百二十三題 / NO. 223】


Sales Managers want to be automatically notified any time there is a change to an Opportunity Close Date and want these changes to be tracked on the Opportunity.
Which two configurations should an app builder recommend? (Choose 2 answers)


銷售經理希望在「機會結束日期」有任何變更時都能自動收到通知，並希望這些變更能在機會上被追蹤。
應用程式建構者應推薦哪兩種設定？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Create an Opportunity outbound message.
     

建立一個機會傳出訊息。

B. Use Process Builder on Opportunities and a Chatter post action.
     

在機會上使用 Process Builder 和一個 Chatter 貼文動作。

C. Activate Historical Trending for Opportunities.
     

為機會啟用歷史趨勢。

D. Enable Feed Tracking on Opportunities.
     

為機會啟用動態追蹤。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, D

詳解 (Explanation):
Using Process Builder on Opportunities and a Chatter post action, and enabling Feed Tracking on Opportunities are two configurations that can meet the requirements. Process Builder can create a process that triggers a Chatter post action (e.g., @mentioning the manager) when the CloseDate field is changed. Feed Tracking can enable tracking of field history for the CloseDate field on the Opportunity feed, making the changes visible to followers.

為了滿足這兩個需求，可以使用：

D. 啟用動態追蹤 (Enable Feed Tracking)：為「機會」物件啟用動態追蹤，並特別勾選 CloseDate 欄位。這樣，每當該欄位的值發生變更時，系統都會自動在該機會的 Chatter 動態中生成一則貼文，記錄變更前後的值。這滿足了「追蹤變更」的需求。

B. 使用 Process Builder (或 Flow) 和 Chatter 貼文動作：建立一個在 CloseDate 欄位變更時觸發的流程。在流程的動作中，使用「發布到 Chatter」動作，並在貼文中 @提及 銷售經理。這滿足了「自動通知」的需求。


【第二百二十四題 / NO. 224】


Universal Containers uses Contracts for agreements with customers. A sales manager is required to provide approval for contracts and director approval for any contract over \$10,000.
Which two options should an app builder use to ensure all contracts route for the correct approval and also prevent the sales rep from making changes to the record while it is being approved? (Choose 2 answers)


Universal Containers 使用「合約」來處理與客戶的協議。銷售經理需要批准所有合約，而對於超過 \$10,000 的任何合約，還需要總監的批准。
應用程式建構者應使用哪兩個選項，以確保所有合約都能路由到正確的批准人，並防止銷售代表在記錄被批准期間進行更改？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Create an approval process on the Contract object with criteria on a second approval step set as 'Amount__c > 10,000' and set the approver as director.
     

在「合約」物件上建立一個批准流程，在第二個批准步驟上設定條件為 'Amount__c > 10,000'，並將批准人設為總監。

B. Create an approval process on the Contract object and set the field for 'Next Automated Approver Determined By' as 'Manager'.
     

在「合約」物件上建立一個批准流程，並將「下一個自動批准人決定者」欄位設為「經理」。

C. The default record locking prevents users from editing a record that has a pending approval request.
     

預設的記錄鎖定會防止使用者編輯有待處理批准請求的記錄。

D. Create an approval process on the Contract object with one step for each sales manager that sets the approver as the director.
     

在「合約」物件上為每個銷售經理建立一個批准流程步驟，將批准人設為總監。
(註：題庫文件中的選項 C 是一個描述而非可執行的動作，此處將其改為更符合問題情境的描述)

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, C (註：題庫的原始答案為 A 和 C，但 C 應理解為批准流程的一個內建特性，而非一個獨立的設定選項。)

詳解 (Explanation):

A. Create an approval process on the Contract object with criteria on a second approval step set as 'Amount__c > 10,000'...

C. ...the default behavior of an approval process is to lock the record once it is submitted for approval. This prevents the submitter from making changes.

滿足此需求的組合是：

A. 建立多步驟的批准流程：建立一個批准流程。第一步無條件地發送給銷售經理。然後新增第二步，設定「步驟進入條件」為「金額大於 10,000」，並將此步驟的批准人指定為總監。這樣就實現了條件式的多級批准。

C. 利用預設的記錄鎖定：批准流程的一個核心特性是，當記錄被提交以供批准後，它會自動被鎖定，提交者無法再對其進行編輯，直到批准流程結束（被批准或被拒絕）。這個預設行為直接滿足了「防止更改」的需求，無需額外設定。


【第二百二十五題 / NO. 225】


What are the limitations of Schema Builder when creating a custom object?


在使用結構描述產生器 (Schema Builder) 建立自訂物件時，有哪些限制？

A. "Save" should be clicked each time a new object, field, or relationship is created.
     

每次建立新物件、欄位或關係時，都應點擊「儲存」。

B. Fields and relationships can be created, but they will be unable to add the fields to the page layout from the canvas.
     

欄位和關係可以被建立，但無法從畫布上將欄位新增到頁面版面配置中。

C. Relationships can be made to any custom objects, but any relationships to standard objects should be built in Lightning Object Manager.
     

可以與任何自訂物件建立關係，但與標準物件的任何關係都應在 Lightning 物件管理員中建立。

D. Custom fields can be added to any custom objects, excluding formula field types.
     

自訂欄位可以新增到任何自訂物件，但不包括公式欄位類型。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
Schema Builder allows users to create custom objects, fields, and relationships using a drag-and-drop interface. However, one of the limitations of Schema Builder is that fields and relationships can be created, but they will be unable to add the fields to the page layout from the canvas. Users will need to go to the Lightning Object Manager or Setup to edit the page layout and add the fields.

結構描述產生器是一個強大的資料模型視覺化和編輯工具，您可以在上面快速建立物件、欄位和關係。然而，它的一個主要限制是，它只處理資料模型層面。您雖然建立了欄位，但無法在 Schema Builder 的介面中直接將這些新欄位拖曳到物件的「頁面版面配置」上。要讓使用者在 UI 上看到這些欄位，您仍然需要離開 Schema Builder，進入「物件管理員」來編輯頁面版面配置。

【第二百二十六題 / NO. 226】


The developer at Universal Containers wants to test code in a sandbox environment. In order to ensure the code works properly, the sandbox needs to have at least half a gigabyte of data. The sandbox will need to be refreshed after each three-day sprint.
What type of sandbox should the App Builder provision to the developer?


Universal Containers 的開發人員希望在沙箱環境中測試程式碼。為了確保程式碼能正常工作，該沙箱需要至少有 0.5 GB 的資料。該沙箱需要在每次為期三天的衝刺 (sprint) 後進行重新整理。
應用程式建構者應為開發人員佈建哪種類型的沙箱？

A. Developer
     

開發人員

B. Full Copy
     

完整複製

C. Developer Pro
     

開發人員專業版

D. Partial Data
     

部分資料

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should provision a Partial Data sandbox to the developer. A Partial Data sandbox can have up to 5 GB of data, which meets the requirement of having at least half a gigabyte of data. A Partial Data sandbox can also be refreshed every 5 days, which meets the requirement of refreshing after each three-day sprint.

我們來分析需求：
資料量：至少 0.5 GB (500 MB)。Developer Sandbox (200MB) 不足，Developer Pro (1GB) 和 Partial Data (5GB) 符合。
重新整理頻率：每次 3 天的衝刺後，意味著需要至少每 3 天重新整理一次。Developer Pro 和 Partial Data 的重新整理間隔都是 5 天，可以滿足。Full Sandbox 是 29 天，不滿足。
綜合來看，Partial Data Sandbox 是最佳選擇，因為它既滿足資料量需求，也滿足重新整理頻率，並且是專為包含部分資料的測試場景設計的。

【第二百二十七題 / NO. 227】


An app builder notices several Accounts converted from Leads are missing information they expected to be caught via Account validation rules.
What could be the source of this issue?


一位應用程式建構者注意到，一些從潛在客戶轉換過來的帳戶缺少了他們預期會被帳戶驗證規則攔截的資訊。
這個問題的根源可能 copious 是什麼？

A. The lead settings are unchecked to require validation for converted leads.
     

潛在客戶設定中未勾選「要求對已轉換的潛在客戶進行驗證」。

B. Account validation rules fail to validate on records converted from a lead.
     

帳戶驗證規則在從潛在客戶轉換來的記錄上驗證失敗。

C. The lead settings are allowing users to intentionally bypass validation rules.
     

潛在客戶設定允許使用者故意繞過驗證規則。

D. Lead validation rules fail to validate on records when they are being converted.
     

潛在客戶驗證規則在記錄被轉換時驗證失敗。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A

詳解 (Explanation):
The lead settings have an option to require validation for converted leads. If this option is unchecked, then the Account, Contact, and Opportunity validation rules will not be enforced when a lead is converted. This could result in missing or incorrect information on the converted records.

問題的根源在於潛在客戶的設定。在「設定 -> 潛在客戶設定 (Lead Settings)」中，有一個選項叫做「強制執行已轉換潛在客戶的驗證與觸發 (Enforce Validation and Triggers from Lead Convert)」。如果這個選項沒有被勾選，那麼在潛在客戶轉換過程中建立新的帳戶、連絡人和機會時，這些新記錄將會繞過目標物件上設定的驗證規則和部分 Apex 觸發器。

【第二百二十八題 / NO. 228】


An App Builder at UVC would like to prevent users from creating new records on an Account related list by overriding standard buttons.
Which two should the App Builder consider before overriding standard buttons? (Choose 2 answers)


UVC 的一位應用程式建構者希望透過覆寫標準按鈕，來阻止使用者在帳戶的相關清單上建立新記錄。
在覆寫標準按鈕之前，建構者應考慮哪兩點？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. Standard buttons can be changed on lookup dialogs, list views, and search result layouts
     

標準按鈕可以在查詢對話方塊、清單檢視和搜尋結果版面配置上更改。

B. Standard buttons can be overridden with a Visualforce page
     

標準按鈕可以用 Visualforce 頁面來覆寫。

C. Standard buttons that are not available for overrides can still be hidden on page layouts
     

無法被覆寫的標準按鈕仍然可以在頁面版面配置上被隱藏。

D. Standard buttons can be overridden, relocated on the detail page, and relabeled
     

標準按鈕可以被覆寫、在詳細資料頁面上重新定位以及重新標籤。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B, C

詳解 (Explanation):
Standard buttons can be overridden with a Visualforce page to provide custom functionality or user interface. For example, you can override the 'New' button to display a custom Visualforce page. Standard buttons that are not available for overrides can still be hidden on page layouts to prevent users from accessing them. For example, you can hide the 'Delete' button on an object to prevent users from deleting records.

在處理標準按鈕時，有兩個重要的考量：

B. 可以用 Visualforce 頁面覆寫：對於像「新增 (New)」、「檢視 (View)」、「編輯 (Edit)」這樣的標準按鈕，您可以將其預設行為覆寫為導向一個自訂的 Visualforce 頁面（或 Lightning 元件/Flow），從而實現自訂邏輯。

C. 可以在頁面版面配置上隱藏：即使某個按鈕不支援覆寫，或者您只是單純想阻止使用者點擊它，您都可以直接在「頁面版面配置」的編輯器中，將該按鈕從相關清單或按鈕區塊中移除，從而達到隱藏的效果。


【第二百二十九題 / NO. 229】


DreamHouse Realty wants to import its property records from an external system into Salesforce. The app builder will use an external ID field to house the property ID from the external system.
Which two details should the app builder know when using external ID fields? (Choose 2 answers)


DreamHouse Realty 希望將其物業記錄從外部系統匯入到 Salesforce。建構者將使用一個外部 ID 欄位來存放來自外部系統的物業 ID。
在使用外部 ID 欄位時，建構者應知道哪兩個細節？(選擇 2 個答案)

A. An external ID field can be a number field.
     

外部 ID 欄位可以是數字欄位。

B. An external ID field can be a URL field.
     

外部 ID 欄位可以是 URL 欄位。

C. An external ID field can be a phone field.
     

外部 ID 欄位可以是電話欄位。

D. An external ID field can be a text field.
     

外部 ID 欄位可以是文字欄位。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): A, D

詳解 (Explanation):
An external ID field can be a number field or a text field. It can also be an email field. An external ID field is used to store unique identifiers from an external system and it can be used for upsert operations. URL and Phone field types cannot be marked as External IDs.

可以被標記為「外部 ID (External ID)」屬性的欄位類型有限。其中最常用的包括：

A. 數字 (Number)

D. 文字 (Text)
電子郵件 (Email) (未在選項中)
像 URL 和 Phone 這類的欄位類型則不支援被設定為外部 ID。


【第二百三十題 / NO. 230】


universal containers has 20 different workflows on the opportunity object. To ensure that updates are processing properly for all field updates, UC has the re-evaluate workflow rules after field change checkbox checked. Recently after adding a new workflow, users have reported receiving errors about workflow limits.
What should an app builder look at to address this?


Universal Containers 在機會物件上有 20 個不同的工作流程。為了確保所有欄位更新都能正確處理，UC 勾選了「欄位變更後重新評估工作流程規則」的核取方塊。最近在新增了一個新的工作流程後，使用者回報收到了關於工作流程限制的錯誤。
應用程式建構者應該檢查什麼來解決這個問題？

A. Talk to a developer about apex code issues
     

與開發人員討論 Apex 程式碼問題。

B. Number of workflows per object limits
     

每個物件的工作流程數量限制。

C. Workflows that cause each other to fire back and forth recursively
     

導致彼此來回遞迴觸發的工作流程。

D. Workflows on other objects that are being re-triggered
     

正在被重新觸發的其他物件上的工作流程。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C

詳解 (Explanation):
Workflows that cause each other to fire back and forth recursively can result in workflow limits errors. For example, if workflow A updates a field that triggers workflow B, and workflow B updates a field that triggers workflow A, this can create an infinite loop of workflows that exceed the maximum number of workflow time triggers per hour or other governor limits.

最可能的原因是遞迴觸發 (recursion)。當您啟用了「重新評估工作流程規則」時，如果工作流程 A 更新了一個欄位，這個更新可能會觸發工作流程 B；而如果工作流程 B 的更新又滿足了工作流程 A 的觸發條件，就會形成一個無限循環。例如：A 說如果欄位 X 是 1 就把它改成 2，B 說如果欄位 X 是 2 就把它改成 1。這種循環會快速消耗 Salesforce 的 governor limits，導致錯誤。建構者需要檢查最近新增的工作流程以及現有的工作流程，找出這種相互觸發的遞迴邏輯。

【第二百三十一題 / NO. 231】


Universal Containers wants to track installation information once a container has been purchased on a custom object. Sales reps should have visibility of all the installations associated with their opportunities.
What kind of relationship should this new object have to the Opportunity?


一旦貨櫃被購買，Universal Containers 希望在一個自訂物件上追蹤安裝資訊。銷售代表應該能夠看到與他們機會相關的所有安裝資訊。
這個新物件應該與「機會 (Opportunity)」建立什麼樣的關係？

A. Lookup
     

查詢

B. Hierarchical
     

階層

C. Master-Detail
     

主從式

D. Many to Many
     

多對多

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): C (註：題庫答案為 A，但 C 是更常見的選擇。此處依題庫答案並補充。)

詳解 (Explanation):
The new object should have a lookup relationship to the Opportunity object. A lookup relationship creates a link between two objects and allows related records to be viewed in a related list. (Note: A Master-Detail relationship would also work and might be preferable if the installation's existence is entirely dependent on the opportunity. However, a lookup is a valid and more flexible option if they can exist independently).

根據題庫答案 A (查詢)：建立一個從「安裝」物件到「機會」物件的查詢關係，可以將兩者連結起來，並在機會頁面上以相關清單的形式顯示所有安裝記錄。這是一種較為鬆散的關係。
更可能的答案 C (主從式)：通常，「安裝」資訊是依附於「機會」而存在的；如果機會被刪除，相關的安裝記錄也應該被刪除。此外，如果未來需要在機會上匯總安裝的次數或成本，主從式關係可以支援總計欄位。因此，主從式關係通常是更合適的選擇。但查詢關係也是一個可行的選項。

【第二百三十二題 / NO. 232】


An app builder is tasked with adding key performance indicators on client pages. They want to see a summary of the number of open Opportunities and the number of won Opportunities for each Account.
Where should the app builder go to build these new rollups?


一位應用程式建構者被指派在客戶頁面上新增關鍵績效指標。他們希望看到每個帳戶的未結案機會數量和已成交機會數量的摘要。
建構者應該去哪裡建立這些新的匯總？

A. Lightning App Builder
     

Lightning 應用程式建構器

B. Account Object
     

帳戶物件

C. Lightning Object Creator
     

Lightning 物件建立器

D. Opportunity Object
     

機會物件

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
The app builder should go to the Account object to build these new rollups. A roll-up summary field is a type of field that can aggregate numeric values from child records...to a parent record. The roll-up summary fields must be created on the master (parent) object, which in this case is the Account object.

建構者應該去「帳戶物件 (Account Object)」的設定頁面。因為需求是將子物件「機會」的資訊匯總到父物件「帳戶」上，所以「總計欄位 (Roll-up Summary Field)」必須建立在父物件，也就是「帳戶」上。您需要進入「設定 -> 物件管理員 -> 帳戶 -> 欄位與關係」來建立這兩個新的總計欄位。

【第二百三十三題 / NO. 233】


The sales Operations team at AWS Computing deletes accounts for a variety of reasons. The sales ops director is worried that the Sales team may delete accounts that sales reps are actively selling into.
How should the app builder keep accounts with open opportunities from being deleted?


AWS Computing 的銷售運營團隊會因為各種原因刪除帳戶。銷售運營總監擔心銷售團隊可能會刪除那些銷售代表正在積極銷售中的帳戶。
應用程式建構者應如何防止擁有未結案機會的帳戶被刪除？

A. Create an Apex Trigger on the Account object
     

在帳戶物件上建立一個 Apex 觸發器。

B. Create a validation rule on the Account object.
     

在帳戶物件上建立一條驗證規則。

C. Remove the delete button on the account layout
     

從帳戶版面配置中移除刪除按鈕。

D. Remove the Delete permission from the Sales Rep profile.
     

從銷售代表的設定檔中移除「刪除」權限。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): B

詳解 (Explanation):
Create a validation rule on the Account object is how the app builder can keep accounts with open opportunities from being deleted. This is not possible with a standard validation rule. This requires a roll-up summary field on the Account to count open Opportunities, and then a validation rule on Account that fires on delete (which is not a standard feature). The most common way to achieve this is with a before-delete Apex Trigger (A) or a record-triggered Flow that runs before delete. However, the provided answer key says

B.

根據題庫答案的解釋：題庫認為應使用驗證規則。然而，標準的驗證規則不能在記錄被刪除時觸發，也不能直接查詢子記錄的數量。
根據 Salesforce 實際行為的正確解釋：要實現此功能，有兩種主要方法：
Apex 觸發器 (A)：建立一個 before delete 的 Apex 觸發器。在觸發器中，查詢該帳戶是否有任何未結案的機會，如果有，就拋出一個錯誤，阻止刪除操作。
記錄觸發的流程 (Record-Triggered Flow)：建立一個在帳戶記錄「被刪除之前」運行的 Flow。在 Flow 中，查詢相關的未結案機會。如果找到了任何記錄，就顯示一個自訂的錯誤訊息來阻止刪除。
鑒於選項，Apex 觸發器 (A) 是最傳統且直接的方法。


【第二百三十四題 / NO. 234】


Universal Containers is piloting new features in an existing sandbox and wants to prevent outbound email sends during testing.
What should the app builder do to meet the requirement?


Universal Containers 正在一個現有的沙箱中試行新功能，並希望在測試期間阻止所有外寄電子郵件的發送。
應用程式建構者應如何做來滿足此需求？

A. Email deliverability set to system email only.
     

將電子郵件傳送能力設為「僅限系統郵件」。

B. Email configured for SMTP authentication.
     

將電子郵件設定為 SMTP 驗證。

C. Email relay to the configured host enabled.
     

啟用電子郵件轉送到已設定的主機。

D. Email deliverability set to no access.
     

將電子郵件傳送能力設為「無存取權」。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
Setting email deliverability to no access would prevent outbound email sends during testing in a sandbox. This would ensure that no emails are sent to any users or external email addresses from the sandbox. 'System email only' would still allow some emails, such as password reset emails.

為了完全阻止沙箱發送任何電子郵件，應在「設定 -> 電子郵件 -> 傳送能力 (Deliverability)」中，將「存取層級 (Access Level)」選項更改為「無存取權 (No access)」。這會禁止所有從該沙箱發出的外寄電子郵件，確保在測試過程中不會意外地向客戶或使用者發送測試郵件。

【第二百三十五題 / NO. 235】


Universal Containers wants users to have access to the pricing guidelines document when viewing a Contract related to an Account.
What feature should an app builder use to create easy access to the document?


Universal Containers 希望使用者在檢視與帳戶相關的「合約」時，能夠存取定價指南文件。
應用程式建構者應使用哪個功能來建立對該文件的輕鬆存取？

A. Quick Action on the Contracts object
     

「合約」物件上的快速動作。

B. Quick Action on the Account object
     

「帳戶」物件上的快速動作。

C. A custom detail page link on the Account object
     

「帳戶」物件上的自訂詳細資料頁面連結。

D. A custom detail page link on the Contract object
     

「合約」物件上的自訂詳細資料頁面連結。

點此查看答案與詳解 (Click to see Answer & Explanation)

答案 (Answer): D

詳解 (Explanation):
The feature that the app builder should use to create easy access to the document is a custom detail page link on the Contract object. A custom detail page link is a type of custom button or link that can display a URL...when clicked. The app builder can create a custom detail page link on the Contract object that displays the pricing guidelines document.

應在「合約 (Contract)」物件上建立一個「自訂詳細資料頁面連結 (custom detail page link)」。這個連結可以被設定為指向儲存定價指南文件的 URL（例如，儲存在 Salesforce Files 中的文件連結，或外部網站連結）。然後，可以將這個連結新增到「合約」的頁面版面配置上，使用者在查看合約記錄時就可以直接點擊該連結來存取文件。
